<nav class="pi-navigation pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background pi-secondary-font"><small><a href="/wiki/Template:Individual_infobox" title="Template:Individual infobox">[Source]</a><span class="hidable-button"></span></small></nav>

</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I'm the sixth in our <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">family</a> to go to <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. You could say I got a lot to live up to. <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a> have already left — Bill was <a href="/wiki/Head_Boy_or_Girl" title="Head Boy or Girl">Head Boy</a> and Charlie was <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_Captain" title="Quidditch Captain">captain</a> of <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a>. Now <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>'s a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a>. <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> mess around a lot, but they still get really good marks and everyone thinks they're really funny. Everyone expects me to do as well as the others, but if I do, it's no big deal, because they did it first.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">family</a> and other's expectations<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p><b>Ronald Bilius</b><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup><b> "Ron" Weasley</b> (b. <a href="/wiki/1_March" title="1 March">1 March</a>, <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a>) was an <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">English</a>  <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a><sup id="cite_ref-blood_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-blood-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">wizard</a>, the sixth and youngest son of <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> <span class="template-c">(née <a href="/wiki/Prewett_family" title="Prewett family">Prewett</a>)</span>. He was also the younger brother of <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a>, <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>, and the elder brother of <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>. Ron and his siblings lived at the <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a>, on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Ottery_St_Catchpole" title="Ottery St Catchpole">Ottery St Catchpole</a>, <a href="/wiki/Devon" title="Devon">Devon</a>. 
</p><p>Ron began attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> and was Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a>. He soon became close friends with fellow student <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> and later <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>. Together, they made the <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">Golden trio</a>, they faced many challenges during their adolescence, including keeping the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> from Professor <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Quirinus Quirrell</a>, rescuing Ginny from the <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Basilisk</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>, saving Harry's godfather <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> of <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, guiding Harry through the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, forming <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> and fighting in numerous battles of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>: including the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> (<a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>), <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> (<a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> (1997). Ron also became a Gryffindor <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a> and a <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> during his fifth year at Hogwarts. 
</p><p>He skipped his last year of school in order to accompany Harry and Hermione on a <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">hunt</a> to destroy all of <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> and fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> in 1998, during which he lost his brother Fred, a loss which devastated him and his family, especially George, Fred's twin.
</p><p>After the war, Ron became an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> and helped reform and revolutionise the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Magic" title="Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PotterCast_28-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PotterCast-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> After two years as an Auror, he went to work at <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a> with his brother George.<sup id="cite_ref-Time_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Time-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> He and Hermione eventually married and had two children, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Weasley" class="mw-redirect" title="Hugo Weasley">Hugo Granger-Weasley</a>. Ron was also named the godfather of <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius Potter</a>, his sister Ginny Weasley's and Harry Potter's eldest child.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Biography">Biography</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=1" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Biography">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Biography"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id="Early_life_(1980-1991)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_.281980-1991.29">Early life <span class="template-c">(1980-1991)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=2" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Early life (1980-1991)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Early life (1980-1991)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Fred and George tried to get me to make one when I was about five. I nearly did, too, I was holding hands with Fred and everything when Dad found us. He went mental. Only time I've ever seen Dad as angry as Mum. Fred reckons his left buttock has never been the same since!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron on his brothers' attempt to get him to make an <a href="/wiki/Unbreakable_Vow" title="Unbreakable Vow">Unbreakable Vow</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest?cb=20150828154152" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The Burrow.png" data-image-key="The_Burrow.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20150828154152" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest?cb=20150828154152" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20150828154152" decoding="async" width="235" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The Burrow.png" data-image-key="The_Burrow.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/59/The_Burrow.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20150828154152" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_Burrow.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Burrow, where Ron grew up with his family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ronald Bilius Weasley was born <a href="/wiki/1_March" title="1 March">1 March</a>, <a href="/wiki/1980" title="1980">1980</a>, to <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur</a> and <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> (née <a href="/wiki/Prewett_family" title="Prewett family">Prewett</a>),<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> at the height of the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>. During this war his maternal uncles <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon Prewett</a>, both members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>, were murdered while fighting a group of four <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> While he was still a toddler, the war ended for a time after <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s first defeat at the hands of Ron's classmate-to-be <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> on <a href="/wiki/31_October" title="31 October">31 October</a>, <a href="/wiki/1981" title="1981">1981</a>.
</p><p>Ron and his five older brothers — <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>, <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> — as well as his younger sister, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>, grew up in <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">The Burrow</a> on the outskirts of <a href="/wiki/Ottery_St_Catchpole" title="Ottery St Catchpole">Ottery St Catchpole</a> in <a href="/wiki/Devon" title="Devon">Devon</a>, <a href="/wiki/England" title="England">England</a>. Like all his siblings, he was home educated in reading, writing and simple mathematics by his mother. The <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> was not wealthy at all, compared to other wizarding families.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Many other <a href="/wiki/Pure-blood" title="Pure-blood">pure-blood</a> families, particularly the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoys</a>, disdained them for their "<i><a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">blood traitor</a></i>" beliefs and lack of wealth. They tried their best to make up for this with their <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Weasley siblings, especially Fred and George, were fond of teasing and playing pranks on each other, and Ron was a particular target for Fred and George. They once <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">transfigured</a> Ron's teddy bear into a giant spider, sparking his arachnophobia. On another occasion, the twins nearly got him to make an Unbreakable Vow, which finally made their father truly furious (and Fred would later state that his left buttock has "<i>never been the same since</i>" after the row that ensued). They also once got him to eat an <a href="/wiki/Acid_Pops" title="Acid Pops">Acid Pop</a> which burnt a hole through his tongue.
</p><p>When Ron was younger, he had a pet rat named Scabbers, whom he had inherited from Percy. This rat was actually <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, a traitor to all wizard kind. Ron was very fond of Scabbers, but wasn't sad to let him go when he found out the truth about his old rat.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-FB_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FB-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Ron had a fairly happy childhood, which Harry, who had been brought up by his spiteful relatives the <a href="/wiki/Dursley_family" title="Dursley family">Dursleys</a>, envied. To compensate for their impoverishment, Ron's mother indulged him in three delicious meals daily. This became so habitual that missing a meal in later life would irritate Ron.
</p>
<h3><span id="Hogwarts_years_(1991-1997)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hogwarts_years_.281991-1997.29">Hogwarts years <span class="template-c">(1991-1997)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=3" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1997)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Hogwarts years (1991-1997)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="First_year">First year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=4" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Harry_and_Hermione">Meeting Harry and Hermione</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=5" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Meeting Harry and Hermione">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Meeting Harry and Hermione"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160215161419" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trio meet.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_meet.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160215161419" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160215161419" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160215161419" decoding="async" width="250" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trio meet.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_meet.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Trio_meet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160215161419" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trio_meet.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">trio</a> meet for the first time on the Hogwarts Express</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png/revision/latest?cb=20180607053436" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron And The Sorting Hat.png" data-image-key="Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607053436" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png/revision/latest?cb=20180607053436" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607053436" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron And The Sorting Hat.png" data-image-key="Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180607053436" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_And_The_Sorting_Hat.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron being <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">sorted</a> into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> by the <a href="/wiki/Sorting_Hat" title="Sorting Hat">Sorting Hat</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron began attending <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> at the customary age of eleven. He was Sorted into Gryffindor House, like every other Weasley. On his first trip on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, Ron met and became friends with the famous wizard <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>. Harry let him share his carriage on the Hogwarts Express and purchased a large amount of wizarding snacks from the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> <a href="/wiki/Honeydukes_Express" title="Honeydukes Express">food trolley</a> to share with him. Later on, Harry would stand up for Ron against <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> bully Draco Malfoy and Ron would elect to be his second for a midnight duel.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Ron and Harry first met <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">train</a> but Ron did not particularly take to her. Ron, especially, was annoyed by what he saw as Hermione showing off her knowledge of <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a>, such as when she corrected him on the pronunciation of the incantation <i><a href="/wiki/Levitation_Charm" title="Levitation Charm">Wingardium Leviosa</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="Hallowe'en"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Hallowe.27en">Hallowe'en</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=6" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hallowe&#039;en">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Hallowe&#039;en"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170719034426" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-harry ron troll.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170719034426" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170719034426" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170719034426" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter1-harry ron troll.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1c/Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170719034426" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter1-harry_ron_troll.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Harry after having defeated a fully grown Mountain troll</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Prior to the <a href="/wiki/Hallowe%27en_feast" class="mw-redirect" title="Hallowe&#39;en feast">Hallowe'en feast</a>, Ron said that Hermione was a know-it-all and did not have any friends. Hermione overheard and went running to the girl's bathroom in tears. That evening, during the Hallowe'en feast, it was announced that a <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell%27s_first_mountain_troll" title="Quirinus Quirrell&#39;s first mountain troll">mountain troll</a> was loose in the school. Ron and Harry came to Hermione's rescue after hearing that she was in trouble, with Ron successfully using the <a href="/wiki/Levitation_Charm" title="Levitation Charm">Levitation Charm</a> to <a href="/wiki/Levitation" title="Levitation">levitate</a> the <a href="/wiki/Troll" title="Troll">troll</a>'s club and drop it on its head, knocking it out. She, in return, lied to protect them from Professor McGonagall. The three then became very close friends.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Protecting_the_Stone">Protecting the Stone</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=7" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Protecting the Stone">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Protecting the Stone"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>I have a few last-minute points to dish out. Let me see. First — to Mr Ronald Weasley... for the best-played game of <a href="/wiki/Wizard%27s_Chess" title="Wizard&#39;s Chess">chess</a> Hogwarts has seen in many years, I award Gryffindor house fifty points.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron is awarded for winning the human chess match<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Ron_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140718155046" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron sacrifice.gif" data-image-key="Ron_sacrifice.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Ron_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140718155046" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Ron_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140718155046" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Ron_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140718155046" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron sacrifice.gif" data-image-key="Ron_sacrifice.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/Ron_sacrifice.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140718155046" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_sacrifice.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron sacrificing himself in the chess game in the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone_Chambers" class="mw-redirect" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone Chambers">Philosopher's Stone Chambers</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During their <a href="/wiki/First_year" title="First year">first year</a>, the three of them learnt that the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> was being hidden in Hogwarts and sought to protect it from being stolen by Severus Snape, whom the young wizards believed to be working for <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>. Ron's talent in <a href="/wiki/Wizard%27s_Chess" title="Wizard&#39;s Chess">Wizard's Chess</a> allowed them to pass one of the obstacles protecting the stone, which was a life-sized game. Ron sacrificed himself as a game piece so Harry could place the enemy king in checkmate, allowing Harry and Hermione to move on. Ultimately, it was discovered that Professor Quirrell was trying to steal the stone for Voldemort. Harry succeeded in defeating him and protecting the Philosopher's Stone, and Ron was awarded fifty <a href="/wiki/House_points" title="House points">House points</a> by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a> for "<i>the best played game of chess that Hogwarts has seen these many years,</i>" allowing Gryffindor to win the <a href="/wiki/House_Cup" title="House Cup">House Cup</a> for the first time in seven years.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_year">Second year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=8" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Second year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Second year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Flying_the_Ford_Anglia">Flying the Ford Anglia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=9" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Flying the Ford Anglia">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Flying the Ford Anglia"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">"<i>LETTER FROM DUMBLEDORE LAST NIGHT, I THOUGHT YOUR FATHER WOULD DIE OF SHAME, WE DIDN’T BRING YOU UP TO BEHAVE LIKE THIS, YOU AND HARRY COULD BOTH HAVE DIED —ABSOLUTELY DISGUSTED — YOUR FATHER’S FACING AN INQUIRY AT WORK, IT’S ENTIRELY YOUR FAULT AND IF YOU PUT ANOTHER TOE OUT OF LINE WE’LL BRING YOU STRAIGHT BACK HOME.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Molly Weasley's nasty howler<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718070817" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-flying car.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170718070817" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718070817" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170718070817" decoding="async" width="245" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-flying car.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ad/Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20170718070817" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-flying_car.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Harry flying a car to school in their <a href="/wiki/Second_year" title="Second year">second year</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Having not heard from <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> during the whole summer of <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, Ron, Fred and George Weasley, in a planned scheme to rescue him from <a href="/wiki/4_Privet_Drive" title="4 Privet Drive">4 Privet Drive</a>, drove Arthur Weasley's <a href="/wiki/Flying_Ford_Anglia" title="Flying Ford Anglia">flying Ford Anglia</a> to the <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggle</a> town of <a href="/wiki/Little_Whinging" title="Little Whinging">Little Whinging</a> and tore the bars from Harry's bedroom window using the car's horsepower. Ron helped Harry get his things in the car, and they left for the Weasley House. Upon landing Ron and his brothers were ratted out by Molly Weasley for having taken such a risky course of action. At the start of that year's school term, Ron and Harry missed the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> due to the tricks of <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> the house-elf and were forced to use the Ford Anglia to travel to Hogwarts. At the end of their journey, the car failed, causing the boys to crash-land into the Whomping Willow. They were nearly killed when the tree shook, and the car jettisoned them and took off into the <a href="/wiki/Forbidden_Forest" title="Forbidden Forest">Forbidden Forest</a>, where it remained.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Attempt_to_curse_Malfoy">Attempt to curse Malfoy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=10" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Attempt to curse Malfoy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Attempt to curse Malfoy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170831193739" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trio writing on wall.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170831193739" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170831193739" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170831193739" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trio writing on wall.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/60/Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170831193739" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trio_writing_on_wall.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The writing on the wall and the petrified form of <a href="/wiki/Mrs_Norris" title="Mrs Norris">Mrs Norris</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_first_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s first wand">Ron's wand</a> was damaged in the crash, causing him problems for the entire school year. It backfired when Ron attempted to <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a> <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> in payback for calling Hermione a "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" with the <a href="/wiki/Slug-vomiting_Charm" title="Slug-vomiting Charm">Slug-vomiting Charm</a>, resulting with him burping up <a href="/wiki/Slug" title="Slug">slugs</a> and slime. Malfoy's disdain towards <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a> led Ron, Harry, and Hermione to suspect that he was the <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Heir of Slytherin</a> who opened the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> that year, unleashing a "<a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Basilisk">monster</a>" that began to attack Muggle-born students.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Impersonating_Crabbe">Impersonating Crabbe</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=11" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Impersonating Crabbe">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Impersonating Crabbe"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>To investigate this theory, Hermione brewed <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> which greatly surprised Ron in that she was so overtly breaking the rules. When the time came to use the potion, Ron was made to impersonate <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a>, and Harry impersonated <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a>, while Hermione's transformation was unsuccessful because she mistook hair from <a href="/wiki/Millicent_Bulstrode" title="Millicent Bulstrode">Millicent Bulstrode</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Millicent_Bulstrode%27s_cat" title="Millicent Bulstrode&#39;s cat">cat</a> for her own. Ron and Harry realised that Malfoy was not the Heir of Slytherin.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_the_Forbidden_Forest">Return to the Forbidden Forest</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=12" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Return to the Forbidden Forest">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Return to the Forbidden Forest"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Ron and Harry were both greatly upset when Hermione became another victim of the "monster," ending up <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> in the Hospital Wing, though she left her friends a clue that led them to deduce that the monster was a <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s basilisk">basilisk</a>. Ron showed incredible bravery during the course of their investigation by venturing into the Forbidden Forest to an <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a> den led by <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, in spite of his extreme fear of spiders. They learned <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a> had nothing to do with opening the chamber, but when Aragog tried to make a meal of them, they narrowly escaped thanks to the magic that had engulfed the Flying Ford Anglia.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Skirmish_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets">Skirmish in the Chamber of Secrets</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=13" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Skirmish in the Chamber of Secrets">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Skirmish in the Chamber of Secrets"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718073143" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718073143" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170718073143" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718073143" decoding="async" width="250" height="103" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fc/Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170718073143" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter2-chamber.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, Harry, and Lockhart stading in the Chamber of Secrets next to Basilisk skin</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When he and Harry learned that <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> (Ron's younger sister) was dying in the Chamber of Secrets, they raced to save her, planning to give their information to Professor <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>. When the pair discovered that the professor was attempting to flee, they drew their wands on him and forced him to join them as they ventured into the Chamber of Secrets. Shortly after Ron, Harry, and Lockhart entered the Chamber, Lockhart attempted to <a href="/wiki/Memory_Charm" title="Memory Charm">wipe their memories</a> in order to get out of the Chamber and take credit for their efforts in a bid for fame. Unfortunately for him, he used Ron's damaged wand, and the spell backfired, causing permanent amnesia in Lockhart. Ron was left behind to tend to Lockhart, as Harry delved deeper into the Chamber, saving Ginny and defeating <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s basilisk">Salazar Slytherin's basilisk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ron was honoured with a <a href="/wiki/Special_Award_for_Services_to_the_School" title="Special Award for Services to the School">Special Award for Services to the School</a>, as well as earning two hundred House points for Gryffindor for his work concerning re-sealing the Chamber of Secrets.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_year">Third year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=14" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Third year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Third year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Where's the dog?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Not a dog. Harry, it's a trap... He's the dog... he's an Animagus.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron reveals that <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> is an Animagus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest?cb=20170104011643" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley Wizarding Vacation in Egypt.png" data-image-key="Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170104011643" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest?cb=20170104011643" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170104011643" decoding="async" width="235" height="156" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley Wizarding Vacation in Egypt.png" data-image-key="Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/50/Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20170104011643" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_Wizarding_Vacation_in_Egypt.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and his family in <a href="/wiki/Egypt" title="Egypt">Egypt</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the summer following Ron's second year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a> won the <a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet_Grand_Prize_Galleon_Draw" title="Daily Prophet Grand Prize Galleon Draw"><i>Daily Prophet</i> Grand Prize Galleon Draw</a>. Ron and his family used the money to travel to Egypt to visit Ron's eldest brother, <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>. News of their lucky break made the <i>Daily Prophet</i>, and Ron sent that newspaper clipping and a <a href="/wiki/Sneakoscope" title="Sneakoscope">Sneakoscope</a> to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> for his thirteenth birthday. They met on the last day of the summer, when Ron and his family visited <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a> with Harry and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> and took up rooms in the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a> in preparation for catching the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During their stay at the Leaky Cauldron, Ron shared a room with his brother Percy. Unfortunately, this led to a fight. Percy believed that Ron had taken his Head Boy badge, which had actually been stolen by Weasley twins Fred and George. Harry found the twins hiding, enchanting the badge to say "<i>Big Head Boy</i>". Later, Ron was also accused of smudging a picture of Percy's girlfriend, <a href="/wiki/Penelope_Clearwater" title="Penelope Clearwater">Penelope Clearwater</a> with tea (Penelope thus hid herself outside the frame so nobody could see her splotched nose).<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest?cb=20180424031501" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="89" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B3C5M7 Dementor on Hogwarts Express.png" data-image-key="B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424031501" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest?cb=20180424031501" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424031501" decoding="async" width="250" height="89" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B3C5M7 Dementor on Hogwarts Express.png" data-image-key="B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4b/B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180424031501" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B3C5M7_Dementor_on_Hogwarts_Express.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dementors board the Hogwarts Express in search of Sirius Black</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Also that summer, Sirius Black, the most famous prisoner in <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, escaped, and in light of this incident, security was tightened at Hogwarts which Ron and his friends noticed when the Hogwarts Express was stopped and searched by <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>. Once at the school, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> announced that Dementors would be stationed around the school gates to prevent Black from entering Hogwarts. This was done under the assumption that Harry was being targeted by Black.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Beginning_of_term">Beginning of term</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=15" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Beginning of term">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Beginning of term"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Upon starting the term, the <a href="/wiki/Third_year" title="Third year">third years</a> began taking new lessons. Ron and Harry had chosen <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> and <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>, while Hermione decided to take every possible class offered and began to exhibit strange behaviour that neither Ron nor Harry could figure out. The pair quickly decided that Divination was not a class they really liked and that the professor, <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>, was a fraud. Ron's first Care of Magical Creatures was a disaster. <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>, the new Care of Magical Creatures professor, had planned what he thought to be a spectacular class on <a href="/wiki/Hippogriff" title="Hippogriff">hippogriffs</a>, when a hippogriff named <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a> attacked <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> after Malfoy had insulted the rare creature, causing Malfoy to promise revenge. Also during that week, Ron had his first <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class with the new professor, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, and in short order Ron thought that Lupin was an excellent professor.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="First_time_in_Hogsmeade">First time in Hogsmeade</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=16" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: First time in Hogsmeade">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: First time in Hogsmeade"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e6/The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140306200454" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The trio laughing in the snow.gif" data-image-key="The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e6/The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140306200454" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e6/The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140306200454" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e6/The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140306200454" decoding="async" width="240" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The trio laughing in the snow.gif" data-image-key="The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e6/The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20140306200454" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The_trio_laughing_in_the_snow.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, Harry, and Hermione at <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On Hallowe'en, Ron and Hermione went on their first Hogsmeade trip. Harry, however, could not join them as his <a href="/wiki/Vernon_Dursley" title="Vernon Dursley">Uncle Vernon</a> had not signed his Hogsmeade permission slip. Meanwhile, Ron and Hermione visited every building in Hogsmeade and brought back loads of sweets from Honeydukes for Harry. That evening, Sirius Black sneaked into Hogwarts, and the students were forced to spend the night in the Dining Hall.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Scabbers_disappears">Scabbers disappears</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=17" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Scabbers disappears">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Scabbers disappears"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Just before <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a>, Rubeus Hagrid received a complaint from the <a href="/wiki/Committee_for_the_Disposal_of_Dangerous_Creatures" title="Committee for the Disposal of Dangerous Creatures">Committee for the Disposal of Dangerous Creatures</a> about Buckbeak the hippogriff. When he shared this incident with Ron, Harry, and Hermione, the trio promised to do everything in their power to help defend Buckbeak. Ron and Harry put the defence of Buckbeak on the back-burner when on Christmas Day, Harry received a <a href="/wiki/Firebolt" title="Firebolt">Firebolt</a> broomstick from a mysterious sender. When Hermione, afraid for Harry's safety, turned the Firebolt in, Ron stopped talking to Hermione. The Firebolt incident only added to the rough tension between the two, as Hermione's new pet <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a> had been continually trying to attack Ron's rat, Scabbers. A few weeks later, when the two were on the verge of making up, Scabbers disappeared and Ron blamed Crookshanks, threatening the friendship between them.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="Sirius_Black's_infiltration"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirius_Black.27s_infiltration">Sirius Black's infiltration</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=18" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sirius Black&#039;s infiltration">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Sirius Black&#039;s infiltration"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png/revision/latest?cb=20160723005744" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron Flying Firebolt.png" data-image-key="Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20160723005744" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png/revision/latest?cb=20160723005744" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20160723005744" decoding="async" width="246" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron Flying Firebolt.png" data-image-key="Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20160723005744" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_Flying_Firebolt.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron riding Harry's Firebolt for the first time on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Quidditch_pitch" title="Hogwarts Quidditch pitch">Hogwarts Quidditch pitch</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the meantime, Black was yet to be found, and the night following the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> vs <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match, he sneaked into Gryffindor tower. Hearing the sound of ripping bed curtains, Ron awoke with a start to see Sirius Black standing over him holding a knife. He screamed, and Black fled.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Defence_of_Buckbeak">Defence of Buckbeak</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=19" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Defence of Buckbeak">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Defence of Buckbeak"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>This incident made Ron famous among the other students, but he came back down to Earth when Hagrid scolded him and Harry about their treatment of Hermione, who Hagrid told them was in over her head with all of her classes and the work she was doing for Buckbeak. Shocked, the pair patched things up with her a few days later, when they received a letter from Hagrid saying that Buckbeak had been sentenced to execution.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>With exams coming up, the trio set about studying and attempting to help Hagrid with Buckbeak's appeal. The appeal took place on the <a href="/wiki/6_June" title="6 June">last day of their exams</a>. Hearing that Buckbeak had lost, and was to be executed, Ron, Harry and Hermione went to visit Hagrid in the evening just before the execution. They offered to help set the record straight, but Hagrid told them that they would be in big trouble if they were seen. Helping the sobbing Hagrid make tea, Hermione found Scabbers hiding inside a milk jar. Soon they were hurried out the back of the hut, all the while they continued to lobby for a chance to set the record straight. When they heard what sounded like the killing, Ron, Harry and Hermione set off for Hogwarts in a slight state of shock.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Prisoner_of_Azkaban">The Prisoner of Azkaban</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=20" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Prisoner of Azkaban">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: The Prisoner of Azkaban"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180101215935" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sirius ron whomping willow.jpg" data-image-key="Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180101215935" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180101215935" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180101215935" decoding="async" width="250" height="100" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sirius ron whomping willow.jpg" data-image-key="Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180101215935" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sirius_ron_whomping_willow.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> captures Ron and drags him to the Whomping Willow</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Before they made it back there, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew#Scabbers" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a> began to squirm in Ron's hands and escaped. Not wanting to lose his rat again, Ron chased after Scabbers with Harry and Hermione behind him. He caught up to Scabbers, but not before they were in the shadow of the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a> tree. He looked up to see a large black dog bearing down upon him. The dog dived at Ron and gripping Ron's arm in its mouth, it dragged him into the Whomping Willow. To try and stop the dog from pulling him further, Ron tied his feet around a tree branch, but the dog's grip was so powerful his leg snapped. When the dog reached the Shrieking Shack, it let go of Ron and revealed itself to be Sirius Black.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sirius ambushed Harry and Hermione, <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarming</a> them when they entered the room where Ron was being held hostage. Upon seeing him, Harry attacked Black with Hermione and the seriously injured Ron helping in any way they could, but Harry could not bring himself to finish the job when he had Black in his power, and he was disarmed by <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Professor Lupin</a>. Relieved at the sight of Lupin, Ron became worried when Lupin and Black greeted each other like brothers and demanded that Ron turn over his rat, Scabbers. Sirius and Lupin then told them about their own years spent at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> and how a wizard named <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> betrayed Harry's parents to Voldemort then framed Sirius and transformed into a rat to go into hiding. Still not fully convinced, Ron reluctantly handed over Scabbers when Lupin promised that if he was actually a rat, no harm would come to him. Scabbers was revealed to be Pettigrew, whom Sirius had recognised due to a missing toe. (Pettigrew has cut off one of his own fingers before transforming). A tearful Pettigrew confessed to the betrayal and begged for mercy from his former friends.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 236px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106042250" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="234" height="154" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore Bedside Manner POA.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20170106042250" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170106042250" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20170106042250" decoding="async" width="234" height="154" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore Bedside Manner POA.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d2/Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20170106042250" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore_Bedside_Manner_POA.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron in the Hospital Wing with his broken leg</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When it was decided that Pettigrew should be turned over to the <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a>, Lupin splinted Ron's leg, and the assembled company left for Hogwarts. Along the way, the full moon broke out, and Lupin began to transform into a werewolf. In the skirmish, Pettigrew stole Lupin's wand, <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunned</a> Ron, and escaped into the moonlight. Hours later in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> where he was recovering both from his broken leg and Pettigrew's attack, Ron was told that Harry and Hermione had managed to <a href="/wiki/Rescue_of_Sirius_Black_and_Buckbeak" title="Rescue of Sirius Black and Buckbeak">save</a> Sirius and Buckbeak from the <a href="/wiki/Dementor%27s_Kiss" title="Dementor&#39;s Kiss">Dementor's Kiss</a> with Hermione's <a href="/wiki/Time-Turner" title="Time-Turner">time turner</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="End_of_term">End of term</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=21" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: End of term">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: End of term"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Ron understood why Hermione did not immediately mention the time turner. Ron was slightly dismayed but, now knew the reason for her strange behaviour and timetable earlier on, he was nevertheless relieved that Sirius and Buckbeak were both safe and free. As a replacement for his lost pet, Sirius sent Ron a tiny owl, which Ginny immediately named <a href="/wiki/Pigwidgeon" title="Pigwidgeon">Pigwidgeon</a> because she thought the name was "<i>sweet</i>"; annoyed and disgusted at this, Ron tried to choose another name, but it was too late, so he settled for using the nickname "Pig".<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_year">Fourth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=22" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fourth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Fourth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Look, it's always you who gets all the attention, you know it is. I know it's not your fault. I know you don't ask for it...but — well — you know, Ron's got all those brothers to compete against at home, and you're his best friend, and you're really famous — he's always shunted to one side whenever people see you, and he puts up with it, and he never mentions it, but I suppose this is just one time too many...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's jealousy after Harry's name came out of the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108184623" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world cup.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108184623" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108184623" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108184623" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world cup.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4a/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108184623" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-world_cup.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron at the 1994 Quidditch World cup with his friends and family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In the summer of 1994, Ron invited Harry and Hermione to accompany the Weasleys to the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a>, which was being held in Britain for the first time in decades. While Hermione joined the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasleys</a> at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a>, Harry had to be picked up from the Dursleys. Arthur Weasley arranged to pick up Harry via <a href="/wiki/Floo_Network" title="Floo Network">Floo Network</a>, not knowing that the Dursleys' fireplace was blocked, so when Ron, Arthur, Fred, and George tried to fetch Harry they ended up stuck in the chimney. Part of the Dursley's house was destroyed before Harry returned to the Weasley's house.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The following day, Harry, Hermione, and all the Weasleys except Molly Weasley left for the Quidditch World Cup, where they set up camp and met many of their friends from Hogwarts or the Ministry. They had prime seats for the match, thanks to Mr Weasley, who had helped <a href="/wiki/Ludovic_Bagman" title="Ludovic Bagman">Ludo Bagman</a>, Head of the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Games_and_Sports" title="Department of Magical Games and Sports">Department of Magical Games and Sports</a>, out of a messy problem. During the match Ron watched <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Bulgaria" title="Bulgaria">Bulgarian</a> <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a>, play an excellent match and catch the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">Snitch</a>. Even though Krum caught the Snitch the Irish National Quidditch Team still won the match.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
