<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 242px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420183844" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="240" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C9M1 the trio seeing the Dark Mark.png" data-image-key="B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20180420183844" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest?cb=20180420183844" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20180420183844" decoding="async" width="240" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C9M1 the trio seeing the Dark Mark.png" data-image-key="B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20180420183844" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C9M1_the_trio_seeing_the_Dark_Mark.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> after the riot at the Quidditch World Cup</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>That night, while the Irish supporters were still awake celebrating their victory, trouble began. Some <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> who had managed to avoid imprisonment in Azkaban, attacked the camp where Ron and his friends and family were staying. Mr Weasley ordered Ron, Harry, Hermione, Fred, George, and Ginny to get to safety, while he and the older Weasley children set off to help the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>. Fred and George were responsible for Ginny's safety, which left the trio to themselves.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Running off into the woods, Ron, Hermione, and Harry quickly lost Fred, George and Ginny, but they did find <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. Malfoy meanly suggested that Hermione, being a Muggle-Born, could easily be targeted by the Death Eaters, causing Ron to insist that she and Harry join him in going deeper into the woods. Soon they reached a patch of woods giving off a silver glow, where the trio found a few <a href="/wiki/Veela" title="Veela">Veela</a> witches surrounded by admirers. Ron was entranced and stated that he would create a broom that would fly to space. They had reached an empty clearing when they heard an <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">unknown person</a> <a href="/wiki/Morsmordre" title="Morsmordre">cast</a> the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Mark" title="Dark Mark">Dark Mark</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_year_begins">The year begins</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=23" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The year begins">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: The year begins"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 251px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png/revision/latest?cb=20190313000729" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="249" height="90" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C14M1 DADA Unforgivable Curses.png" data-image-key="B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20190313000729" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png/revision/latest?cb=20190313000729" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20190313000729" decoding="async" width="249" height="90" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C14M1 DADA Unforgivable Curses.png" data-image-key="B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/249?cb=20190313000729" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C14M1_DADA_Unforgivable_Curses.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio during a Defence Against the Dark Arts lesson on the Unforgivable Curses</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On 1 September, Ron and his friends departed for Hogwarts aboard the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>. That evening at the <a href="/wiki/Welcoming_Feast" title="Welcoming Feast">Welcoming Feast</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> announced that Hogwarts would host the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. Ron found himself caught up in dreams of being a Triwizard Champion, but he was snapped back to reality by his fourth year classes. In <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> had his students tending to <a href="/wiki/Blast-Ended_Skrewt" title="Blast-Ended Skrewt">Blast-Ended Skrewts</a>, and in <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, Ron was impressed by the new professor, <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">"Mad-Eye" Moody</a>, when he taught the class about the three <a href="/wiki/Unforgivable_Curses" title="Unforgivable Curses">Unforgivable Curses</a>. It was announced that the students from the <a href="/wiki/Durmstrang_Institute" title="Durmstrang Institute">Durmstrang Institute</a> and <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons Academy of Magic</a> would be arriving at Hogwarts on 30 October. Ron was dumbstruck when he saw <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> among the Durmstrang students, not realising how young his hero was. He was disappointed when Krum sat among the Slytherin students.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Envying_Harry_Potter">Envying Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=24" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Envying Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Envying Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108180238" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron goblet.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108180238" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108180238" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108180238" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron goblet.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5b/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108180238" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-ron_goblet.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">An angry Ron and an upset Hermione watch as Harry's name comes out of the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Having discussed the possibility of somehow outsmarting the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Age_Line" title="Age Line">Age Line</a> that Dumbledore had cast around it, Ron was surprised to find that Harry's name had come out of the Goblet of Fire. Jealous of the fact that Harry always seemed to receive all the attention, Ron refused to accept that Harry didn't put his name in the cup. He even went as far as to accuse Harry of cheating his way into the tournament. After the argument, he and Harry stopped talking to each other, and Ron began hanging out with other Gryffindors like <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a> and <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Ron heard Harry talking to someone one night, he went down to see who it was since Harry didn't tell him about such a thing. Ron was deeply offended when Harry accused him of trying to spy on him and when he told him who he talked to was none of his business to the point where he tried to get Harry to tell him who he was talking to by accusing him of practising for an interview. This only made Harry throw one of Draco Malfoy's badges at him and tell him he could wear that during the First Task. This made Ron finally realise that the reason Harry had started avoiding him was because Harry felt betrayed by him to the point where he had lost Harry's trust and respect to the point where Harry no longer saw him as a friend, a realisation that deeply hurt Ron.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>  
</p><p>Ron and Harry did not talk to each other again until after the First Task of the Triwizard tournament. Seeing just how much danger was involved in the First Task, Ron realised Harry would never have put his own name into the Goblet of Fire, and the two became best friends once again.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Yule_Ball">The Yule Ball</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=25" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The Yule Ball">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: The Yule Ball"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160513210615" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160513210615" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160513210615" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160513210615" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/af/Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160513210615" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-goblet-of-fire-movie-screencaps.com-9205.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron with his date at the Yule Ball</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Soon after the first task, <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> told Ron and the other Gryffindor boys about the traditional <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, held during the Triwizard Tournament. While all students above fourth year scampered around trying to find dates, Ron and Harry found it hard to ask girls to the ball. Struck by the beauty and charm of <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, the Triwizard Champion from Beauxbatons Academy and a <a href="/wiki/Half-Veela" title="Half-Veela">part-Veela</a> witch, Ron asked her to attend the ball with him, but fled in embarrassment without waiting for an answer. He also offended Hermione by not asking her, and then by suggesting that she did not have a date and thus could accompany him. Harry was eventually able to get them both dates with twins <a href="/wiki/Parvati_Patil" title="Parvati Patil">Parvati</a> and Padma Patil. Ron's evening was a fiasco of the first sort. His "<i>traditional</i>" dress robes embarrassed him and his date, <a href="/wiki/Padma_Patil" title="Padma Patil">Padma Patil</a>, and when Ron saw Hermione with <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, he became intensely jealous. This led to a blazing argument between them during the end of the Yule Ball Ron made comments about Krum being too old for her and Hermione accusing him of ruining everything. Though their friendship did not suffer, it was clear that both had developed feelings for each other.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 236px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Harry_ron_second_task.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140818010125" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="234" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry ron second task.gif" data-image-key="Harry_ron_second_task.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Harry_ron_second_task.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20140818010125" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Harry_ron_second_task.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140818010125" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Harry_ron_second_task.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20140818010125" decoding="async" width="234" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry ron second task.gif" data-image-key="Harry_ron_second_task.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/90/Harry_ron_second_task.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/234?cb=20140818010125" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_ron_second_task.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> retrieving a captive Ron during the second task</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the Yule Ball, Ron had overheard <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> telling the Beaubaxtons Headmistress Olympe Maxime that he was half-giant. This information was also overheard by <i>Daily Prophet</i> Reporter <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>, who wrote an article telling the wizarding world of Hagrid's heritage. This drove Hagrid to stop teaching for a time until Ron, Harry, and Hermione told him that they he was still their friend, no matter what.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Imprisoned_by_sea_creatures">Imprisoned by sea creatures</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=26" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Imprisoned by sea creatures">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Imprisoned by sea creatures"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/24_February" title="24 February">24 February</a>, Ron was put into an enchanted sleep and tied up at the bottom of the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lake" title="Great Lake">Black Lake</a>, to be "rescued" by Harry as part of the second task of the Triwizard Tournament. When he found out that Harry had stayed behind to save Fleur's sister <a href="/wiki/Gabrielle_Delacour" title="Gabrielle Delacour">Gabrielle Delacour</a> as well, Ron jokingly took him to task, but was impressed when Harry was given extra points for "<i>outstanding moral fibre</i>". Fleur thanked Ron and Harry in turn for helping save Gabrielle, kissing both of them on the cheek. Ron gained much attention from the other students due to his being taken hostage for the task. He proceeded to exaggerate the events of what happened until Hermione called him on it.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Preparing_for_the_end">Preparing for the end</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=27" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Preparing for the end">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Preparing for the end"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest?cb=20180423221722" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" decoding="async" width="250" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B4C36M1 Snape Dark Mark reveal.png" data-image-key="B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180423221722" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B4C36M1_Snape_Dark_Mark_reveal.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron was present when the Minister for Magic visited Harry in the hospital wing</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Early in the spring, Ron joined Harry and Hermione in visiting <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, who had taken to hiding in Hogsmeade. There, they discussed the disappearances of Ministry officials <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Senior" title="Bartemius Crouch Senior">Barty Crouch Snr</a> and <a href="/wiki/Bertha_Jorkins" title="Bertha Jorkins">Bertha Jorkins</a>. In the weeks leading up to the final tournament task, Ron and Hermione helped Harry prepare by researching and trying out different jinxes and other helpful spells for the task. Ron and Hermione watched Harry together from the sidelines.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>They were shocked when Harry returned with <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a>'s dead body. Ron was relieved to see Harry when he was brought to the infirmary by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Professor Dumbledore</a>, eagerly wanted to question Harry about Diggory, but he was told off by Molly Weasley who, along with his brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill Weasley</a>, had come to watch Harry. Ron was furious with the Minister for Magic, <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a>, when he refused to believe Harry and Dumbledore, and calmed Molly when she was shocked by Black's appearance in the room. Ron did not go against Harry's story when he finally heard it, sticking by his best friend.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fifth_year">Fifth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=28" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fifth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Fifth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">"<i>Weasley cannot save a thing, he cannot block a single ring.<br />That's why Slytherins all sing, Weasley is our king!...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherins</a> mocking Ron's <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> abilities<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180420213240" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B5C6M1 Doxycide Grimmauld Place.jpg" data-image-key="B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420213240" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180420213240" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420213240" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B5C6M1 Doxycide Grimmauld Place.jpg" data-image-key="B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180420213240" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B5C6M1_Doxycide_Grimmauld_Place.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron with others in 12 Grimmauld Place preparing to clean</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Voldemort rose to power and the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a> began, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> reformed the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. In the summer of 1995, the Order moved into their headquarters at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> with the Weasley schoolchildren and Hermione Granger, where they helped <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Molly Weasley</a> clean the old house and remained watchful for information about Harry. In August, Harry arrived at the headquarters after a <a href="/wiki/Attack_in_Little_Whinging" title="Attack in Little Whinging">Dementor attack</a> on his cousin. Ron felt sorry that he had to keep Harry oblivious to the Order's plan and soon learnt that Harry's anger had been growing due to his isolation from his friends and his persecution by the media.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ron, Harry and Hermione stayed at Grimmauld Place throughout August. In late August, Ron and Hermione were made a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">prefect</a>, for which Molly and Arthur gave Ron a new <a href="/wiki/Cleansweep_Eleven" title="Cleansweep Eleven">Cleansweep Eleven</a>. Bound by their prefect duties, Ron and Hermione were separated from Harry on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> and could only join Harry in his compartment for the last part of the journey. When they arrived, Ron expressed concern that <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> was not at the welcoming feast and was suspicious of the new <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor, <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160606154912" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Umbridge teaching.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_teaching.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160606154912" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160606154912" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160606154912" decoding="async" width="250" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Umbridge teaching.jpg" data-image-key="Umbridge_teaching.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/07/Umbridge_teaching.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160606154912" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Umbridge_teaching.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The first DADA class with Umbridge as the professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At school, Ron was one of the many students who expressed frustration with Professor Umbridge's refusal to teach the class practical defensive magic. He also won the position of <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> but was described by the team captain as "needing improvement". Ron's <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> practice caused him to fall behind in his schoolwork, to Hermione's chagrin. Soon, Ron's brother <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a> sent him a letter advising him not to remain friends with Harry, whom he accused of being mad for supporting <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Ron was outraged by the letter's contents, tearing it into eight pieces and throwing it into the Gryffindor common room's fireplace, angrily declaring his brother to be "the world's biggest git."
</p>
<h5><span id="Initiating_Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Initiating_Dumbledore.27s_Army">Initiating Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=29" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Initiating Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Initiating Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Late in September, one evening when Harry returned from detention with Professor Umbridge, Ron, somewhat reluctantly, joined Hermione in convincing that Harry teach his fellow students defence against the dark arts. Harry initially disagreed, but after a few days he decided to give it a go. Around this time, Professor Umbridge was appointed the first <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_High_Inquisitor" title="Hogwarts High Inquisitor">Hogwarts High Inquisitor</a>, giving her the power to randomly create new school rules and inspect teachers' lessons.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/DA_meeting_ootp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180526232313" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DA meeting ootp.jpg" data-image-key="DA_meeting_ootp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/DA_meeting_ootp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180526232313" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/DA_meeting_ootp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180526232313" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/DA_meeting_ootp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180526232313" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DA meeting ootp.jpg" data-image-key="DA_meeting_ootp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5c/DA_meeting_ootp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180526232313" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DA_meeting_ootp.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron during the meeting of students in the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a> that would become known as Dumbledore's Army</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Late in October, students had their first visit to <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>. There, Harry, Ron, and Hermione met with several students who were interested in learning proper defence. Ron defended Harry against <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a><b> </b>when questions rose, and was among the first to sign the recruitment parchment. On the way home from Hogsmeade, Ron became upset when he learned from Hermione that his sister <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> was dating Ravenclaw student <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>. The following morning, Ron awoke to find that suddenly, by order of Professor Umbridge, all student groups had been disbanded including the House Quidditch teams, but he was mollified when Harry said they would continue with their secret group, which Ginny named "<i><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a></i>" during their first meeting, mocking the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>'s fears of student uprisings.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="Playing_Quidditch_and_Hagrid's_tale"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Playing_Quidditch_and_Hagrid.27s_tale">Playing Quidditch and Hagrid's tale</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=30" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Playing Quidditch and Hagrid&#039;s tale">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Playing Quidditch and Hagrid&#039;s tale"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>In the weeks following the first Dumbledore's Army meeting, Quidditch season arrived. Ron had nervous issues prior to the first match against Slytherin. They had made badges saying "<i>Weasley is our king</i>," which Harry decided could not mean anything good. In an attempt to distract Ron from the Slytherins, Hermione kissed him on the cheek for luck, effectively stunning Ron. Ron's play was abysmal, and it was not helped by the Slytherins' new song also entitled, "<i><a href="/wiki/Weasley_is_Our_King" title="Weasley is Our King">Weasley is Our King</a></i>". Following the game Ron wanted to resign, but learned he could not, as Harry Potter, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a>, and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George Weasley</a> had been banned from Quidditch for life. That evening Hagrid returned from his unknown disappearance. Although initially resistant he regaled the trio with his tales of the <a href="/wiki/Giant" title="Giant">giants</a>, though he refused to give them any hint about his gruesome injuries from Golgomath's tribe. Ultimately Hagrid's mission was a failure.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180711140556" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys harry.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711140556" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180711140556" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711140556" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys harry.jpg" data-image-key="Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711140556" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order-of-the-phoenix-weasleys_harry.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry informs the Weasleys of their father's attack at the Ministry</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following Hagrid's return, he took up his post as <a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a> professor. In Hagrid's first lesson, Ron learned about <a href="/wiki/Thestral" title="Thestral">Thestrals</a>, magical creatures that could only be seen by wizards and witches who had witnessed death.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="The_attack_on_Arthur_Weasley">The attack on Arthur Weasley</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=31" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: The attack on Arthur Weasley">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: The attack on Arthur Weasley"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Frequent Dumbledore's Army meetings, <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> homework, and his prefect duties took up most of Ron's time as the holidays approached. Following the last meeting of the term, Ron was amazed at Harry's "romantic" tale, earning him a stern talking to from Hermione who suggested that Ron had <i>"the emotional range of a teaspoon</i>." That night, Harry witnessed Ron's father, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a>, being attacked by Lord Voldemort's snake, <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>. When Harry's story was confirmed by Dumbledore and McGonagall, Ron, his siblings, and Harry were immediately sent to the Order's Headquarters, so they could look in on their father's convalescence, and there they spent the <a href="/wiki/Christmas_holidays" title="Christmas holidays">Christmas holidays</a>, joined by Hermione the next day.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During their first trip to <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's</a> Hospital, Ron overheard "<a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Mad Eye" Moody</a> thinking that Harry had been possessed by Voldemort. Ron was worried when Harry became quiet after the visit and wanted to talk to Harry about it. He got his chance after Hermione arrived and convinced Harry to come downstairs. Ron, Hermione, and Ginny told Harry how worried they had been and managed to confess that he was not being possessed. They had an enjoyable holiday, but on their second visit to the hospital, Ron learned the truth about the torture of <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>'s parents.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161217055928" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DA Luna Fred Ginny George Ron.jpg" data-image-key="DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161217055928" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161217055928" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161217055928" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DA Luna Fred Ginny George Ron.jpg" data-image-key="DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/93/DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161217055928" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DA_Luna_Fred_Ginny_George_Ron.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron with siblings Fred and George, and Ginny practising with the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">D.A.</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/RonExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416125024" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="RonExpectoPatronum.gif" data-image-key="RonExpectoPatronum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/RonExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416125024" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/RonExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190416125024" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/RonExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416125024" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="RonExpectoPatronum.gif" data-image-key="RonExpectoPatronum.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/RonExpectoPatronum.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190416125024" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:RonExpectoPatronum.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron conjuring his Patronus</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Throughout the term, Ron continued to learn defensive and offensive magic from Harry. He also stayed on the Gryffindor Quidditch team, despite his very poor performances. Due to Quidditch, he missed the <a href="/wiki/Valentine%27s_Day" title="Valentine&#39;s Day">Valentine's Day</a> visit to Hogsmeade. Though, he was impressed that Harry went public and hopeful that people might believe Harry when <i><a href="/wiki/The_Quibbler" title="The Quibbler">The Quibbler</a></i> came out. Soon, Umbridge managed to sack <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Professor Trelawney</a>, but her ability to name a replacement was pre-empted when <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> arranged to have <a href="/wiki/Firenze" title="Firenze">Firenze</a> the Centaur teach the subject. Umbridge was affronted by this new staffing appointment.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span id="Marietta_Edgecombe's_betrayal"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Marietta_Edgecombe.27s_betrayal">Marietta Edgecombe's betrayal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=32" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Marietta Edgecombe&#039;s betrayal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Marietta Edgecombe&#039;s betrayal"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Soon after Trelawney's sacking, <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>, a friend of Ravenclaw Student <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>'s who only reluctantly joined Dumbledore's Army, told Umbridge about the group, but was unable to give up any pertinent information once she saw a <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_parchment_jinx" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army parchment jinx">jinx</a> activate on her face. Ron was able to escape when Umbridge, raided the Dumbledore's Army headquarters, but he was incensed when Professor Dumbledore was forced out of the school. He was also wary when his brothers Fred and George Weasley said they were going to do their part for Professor Dumbledore. After Fred and George's secret escape from Hogwarts, Ron was certain that his mother would blame him, but he was saved from this fate when Harry revealed that it was he who financed <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108180822" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DA captured by Umbridge.jpg" data-image-key="DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108180822" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108180822" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108180822" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DA captured by Umbridge.jpg" data-image-key="DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/19/DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180108180822" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DA_captured_by_Umbridge.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and other D.A. members being held captive by Umbridge</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron played in the final Quidditch match of the season, though Harry and Hermione did not watch, as Hagrid finally revealed the source of his injuries to them. Ron played better, and Gryffindor won the <a href="/wiki/Inter-House_Quidditch_Cup" title="Inter-House Quidditch Cup">Quidditch Cup</a>. Ron was unable to settle to his studies the following day, but Harry and Hermione brought him down with Hagrid's secret injuries.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=33" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Battle of the Department of Mysteries"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5><p>
Shortly thereafter, their <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">Ordinary Wizarding Level</a> exams were upon them. Ron managed to do very well, but he made a few mistakes. During their final exam, Harry dozed off and had another vision. This time, he saw Sirius being tortured by Voldemort in the Ministry. When Harry told Ron and Hermione of this they were wary, and Hermione suggested that Harry try to contact Sirius first. Ron ran off to distract Umbridge, but the plan failed, and Ron and his friends were rounded up and taken to Umbridge's office. There, Ron, Ginny, Neville, and Luna Lovegood managed to fight off Umbridge and her Slytherin Guards and escape to find Harry and Hermione outside the forest.</p><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912125022" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="120" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="OOTP Death Chamber trio Ginny Neville Luna.gif" data-image-key="OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140912125022" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/98/OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140912125022" decoding="async" width="245" 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:OOTP_Death_Chamber_trio_Ginny_Neville_Luna.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> in the Death Chamber</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron insisted that he join Harry in rescuing Sirius, but also insisted that the rest remain behind, but realised when many Thestrals appeared. When Harry led them into the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Mysteries" title="Department of Mysteries">Department of Mysteries</a>, Ron stuck with him into the deepest recesses of the Department. There, the six Dumbledore's Army members were ambushed by twelve <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, led by wizarding aristocrat <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, and Ron helped defend the prophecy Harry took from the Hall Of Prophecies, but his fight was soon over as a Death Eater had wiped his brains. Ron was so confused that he summoned a tentacled-brain from a vat in the Thought Chamber and was attacked by it, but soon recovered later on. Ron was devastated by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius</a>'s death, but Hermione made sure that Sirius's death was not discussed around Harry.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sixth_year">Sixth year</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=34" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sixth year">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Sixth year"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>You said to us once before that there was time to turn back if we wanted to. We've had time, haven't we?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>We're with you, whatever happens.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A commit to Harry and his <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">Horcrux hunt</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>During the summer following the battle, Ron learned he had received seven <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.s</a>, only failing <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> and <a href="/wiki/History_of_Magic" title="History of Magic">History of Magic</a>. Ron explained he did not mind, as he, like Harry, didn't like those subjects very much, anyway. Also during that summer, Ron learned that his brother Bill was engaged to <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>. While this annoyed his mother, sister, and later Hermione, Ron took to defending Fleur and if she surprised him, he would still take on that dumbstruck look. His soft spot for Fleur particularly annoyed Hermione, who was finding it harder to keep her feelings for him under wraps. When Ron and Hermione learned that <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> was in fact the "Chosen One," Ron remained at Harry's side.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="A_rough_start">A rough start</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=35" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: A rough start">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=35" title="Edit section: A rough start"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720145922" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-ron tryouts.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720145922" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720145922" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720145922" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-half-blood-ron tryouts.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/30/Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180720145922" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-half-blood-ron_tryouts.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron trying out as <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> for the Gryffindor Quidditch team</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron would suffer much personal turmoil in his sixth year. Harry was named <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> team captain. Ron was nervous about Quidditch try-outs, but beat out <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a> in saves, partly because Hermione cast a <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a> on McLaggen in retaliation for him insulting Ron and Ginny. He was also envious when Harry and Hermione were invited to the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, while the new <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">Potions</a> professor <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> ignored him, and when attention was paid to him, Slughorn usually got his name wrong. During this time, Ron showed brief flashes of jealousy about Harry and Hermione's closeness. He would take exception whenever Hermione complimented Harry on something Ron thought was equally due to him. Ron was temporarily mollified about this when <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> asked if he would like to attend the club's Christmas party with her, and he agreed, but thought it was only as friends.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Ron_Keeper.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160513202125" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron Keeper.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Keeper.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Ron_Keeper.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160513202125" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Ron_Keeper.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160513202125" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Ron_Keeper.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160513202125" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron Keeper.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Keeper.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b6/Ron_Keeper.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160513202125" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_Keeper.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron playing as Keeper against Slytherin in the first match of the year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was also worried over his sister's increasing involvement with boys, and after stumbling upon her kissing <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, he blew up at her. In retaliation, Ginny belittled him for his complete inexperience with the opposite gender, declaring that Harry and Hermione had also snogged people. The siblings treated each other coldly afterwards, and Ron was so bothered by this — and by the revelation that Hermione had kissed Viktor Krum almost two years earlier — that he began to perform poorly in Quidditch. He also began to treat Hermione with a cold indifference, which confused her. He even offered to resign from the team. To boost his confidence, Harry pretended to pour the <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a> into Ron's <a href="/wiki/Pumpkin_Juice" title="Pumpkin Juice">Pumpkin Juice</a> at breakfast. Harry even allowed Hermione to see the vial, so she would object to the cheating. This convinced Ron that he had an edge in the game, which caused him to play excellently. However, when after the match Harry revealed it was a trick, Ron rounded on Hermione and accused her of having no faith in his abilities.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Dating_Lavender_Brown">Dating Lavender Brown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=36" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dating Lavender Brown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=36" title="Edit section: Dating Lavender Brown"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>Shortly thereafter, Ron began his exhibitionist relationship with <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>. Hermione, incredibly angry and hurt by Ron's vindictive actions, conjured a flock of canaries to <a href="/wiki/Oppugno_Jinx" title="Oppugno Jinx">attack</a> him; the birds scratched Ron badly. Although he did not report this, he spent a long time ranting about her violent and hypocritical act. He and Hermione stopped talking to each other after that. Hermione attended the Slug Club's Christmas party, she had originally wanted to attend with Ron but went with his hated rival, <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a>, while Ron snogged Lavender in public and made fun of Hermione's behaviour in <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> class, reducing her to tears.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By Christmas break, however, Ron was becoming disenchanted with his relationship with Lavender, who had become increasingly possessive, annoyed him with the nickname "<i>Won-Won</i>," and gave him a gift of a necklace that said "<i>My Sweetheart</i>". Hermione did not come to the<a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow"> Burrow</a> for the holidays, as she usually did, and Ron made an attempt to speak to her after returning to school, but she ignored him.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Poisoned_twice">Poisoned twice</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=37" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Poisoned twice">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=37" title="Edit section: Poisoned twice"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 246px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720144619" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="244" height="102" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter saving a poisoned Ronald Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20180720144619" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180720144619" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20180720144619" decoding="async" width="244" height="102" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter saving a poisoned Ronald Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/244?cb=20180720144619" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_saving_a_poisoned_Ronald_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron having a fit after ingesting the poisoned mead</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On <a href="/wiki/1_March" title="1 March">1 March</a> <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Ron ate chocolate that he believed to be one of the presents for <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_seventeenth_birthday" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s seventeenth birthday">his 17th birthday</a>, but was in fact a gift from <a href="/wiki/Romilda_Vane" title="Romilda Vane">Romilda Vane</a> to Harry spiked with a <a href="/wiki/Amortentia" title="Amortentia">love potion</a>. He found the box on the floor after Harry had chucked it out of his trunk thinking in was apart of his pile of presents by the foot of his bed. Upon ingesting the chocolate, Ron became maddened with an obsessive need to see and be with Romilda. Harry thinking fast proceeded to take Ron to Slughorn's office to get an antidote. When in Slughorn's office while Harry attempted to get Slughorn in a good mood hoping to get the true memory from him, Ron was nearly killed by poisoned mead intended for <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. Harry managed to save Ron with a <a href="/wiki/Bezoar" title="Bezoar">bezoar</a>. The bezoar was one Slughorn had in his kit taken from a previous potions lesson. If it wasn't for Harry's timely actions and quick thinking Ron would have died.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP18_33-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP18-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160830010138" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Poppy Pomfrey - Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160830010138" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160830010138" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160830010138" decoding="async" width="245" height="115" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Poppy Pomfrey - Ron Weasley.jpg" data-image-key="Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/3d/Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160830010138" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Poppy_Pomfrey_-_Ron_Weasley.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A poisoned Ron being attended by <a href="/wiki/Poppy_Pomfrey" title="Poppy Pomfrey">Madam Pomfrey</a> and visited by Harry, Hermione, and Ginny</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A panic-stricken Hermione arrived at the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a>, forgetting her anger with him. Ron said Hermione's name in his sleep upon hearing her speak for the first time all day, and the two quietly reconciled after his near-death experience. Ron also took to feigning sleep whenever Lavender tried to visit him. He remained in the hospital the following week and was not able to play Keeper on Saturday <a href="/wiki/8_March" title="8 March">8 March</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_vs_Hufflepuff_Quidditch_match_(1997)" title="Gryffindor vs Hufflepuff Quidditch match (1997)">Gryffindor vs Hufflepuff Quidditch match</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP19_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP19-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Re-embracing_friends">Re-embracing friends</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=38" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Re-embracing friends">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=38" title="Edit section: Re-embracing friends"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<p>On Monday <a href="/wiki/10_March" title="10 March">10 March</a> Ron and Harry, who suffered a cracked skull from a mishit <a href="/wiki/Bludger" title="Bludger">Bludger</a> during the match, were able to leave the hospital wing, although Ron did not tell Lavender this.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP20_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP20-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> His subsequent avoidance of Lavender and simultaneous spending more time with Hermione made Lavender suspicious; after she spotted him and Hermione leaving the boys' dormitories, seemingly alone (Harry was with them, but under his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Cloak of Invisibility</a>), Lavender ended the relationship, much to Ron's relief. A little later, Ron was suitably impressed when Harry told him and Hermione how he managed to obtain the Horcrux memory from Professor Slughorn. A few weeks later, when Harry used <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> on <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, Ron lent his potions book to Harry, so Professor Snape would not confiscate the Half-Blood Prince's book.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=39" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=39" title="Edit section: Battle of the Astronomy Tower"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h5>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20161209004341" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161209004341" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20161209004341" decoding="async" width="251" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B6C30M1 funeral of Albus Dumbledore.png" data-image-key="B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/06/B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20161209004341" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B6C30M1_funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The <a href="/wiki/Funeral_of_Albus_Dumbledore" title="Funeral of Albus Dumbledore">funeral of Albus Dumbledore</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the night of the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, Ron took Felix Felicis on Harry's instructions, along with Hermione and Ginny. Those three were joined by <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, whom Hermione had summoned using the <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army_coin" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army coin">D.A. coins</a>. While Hermione and Luna monitored Professor Snape's office, Ron and the others watched the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>. Ron fought in the battle and survived without any major injuries, thanks to the Felix Felicis. He was shaken by his oldest brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>'s scarring at the hands of the vicious <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a> <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>. Shortly afterwards, Ron attended the funeral of Albus Dumbledore, where he comforted a sobbing Hermione. He and Hermione informed Harry of their intention to accompany him on a quest to locate and destroy the <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> of Lord Voldemort, forgoing their seventh year of school.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Horcrux_Hunt_(1997-1998)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Horcrux_Hunt_.281997-1998.29">Horcrux Hunt <span class="template-c">(1997-1998)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=40" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Horcrux Hunt (1997-1998)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Horcrux Hunt (1997-1998)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>If you think I’m going to let six people risk their lives —&#160;!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>—because it’s the first time for all of us.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A argument over the seven Potters plan<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
