<p>During the summer of 1997, Ron began planning ahead for his mission with Harry and Hermione. With the help of <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">his father</a> and Fred and George Weasley, Ron <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">transfigured</a> the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family_ghoul" title="Weasley family ghoul">family ghoul</a> to resemble himself sick with <a href="/wiki/Spattergroit" title="Spattergroit">spattergroit</a>, which would serve as his alibi for not attending his seventh year of Hogwarts while travelling with his friends.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=41" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Battle of the Seven Potters"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Ron was great. Wonderful. Stunned one of the Death Eaters, straight to the head, and when you're aiming at a moving target from a flying broom —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's helpfulness during the battle<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest?cb=20170106051900" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C4M1 Seven Potters depart.png" data-image-key="B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106051900" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest?cb=20170106051900" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106051900" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C4M1 Seven Potters depart.png" data-image-key="B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/bc/B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170106051900" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C4M1_Seven_Potters_depart.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Seven Harrys and their protectors preparing to take off</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In late July, he participated in the Order's operation to remove Harry from his childhood home, taking <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> to be one of the "<i>seven Potters</i>." He flew with Nymphadora Tonks; they were pursued by at least three Death Eaters during the battle, including <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a> and <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus Lestrange</a>. Ron stunned one of the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in the face while flying. Ron reassured Hermione by nuzzling her back slightly upon landing as she had been quite worried about him and he was saddened at the death of <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">"Mad-Eye" Moody</a>. He was also saddened by the death of Harry's beloved pet owl <a href="/wiki/Hedwig" title="Hedwig">Hedwig</a>, over which he comforted Harry. Ron became concerned when Harry had a vision of an imprisoned <a href="/wiki/Garrick_Ollivander" title="Garrick Ollivander">Garrick Ollivander</a> being brutally tortured by Lord Voldemort in the cellar at Malfoy Manor.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 237px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128225544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="235" height="157" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Scrimgeour Trio.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20190128225544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128225544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20190128225544" decoding="async" width="235" height="157" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Scrimgeour Trio.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7a/DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/235?cb=20190128225544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_HQ_still_Scrimgeour_Trio.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, Harry, and Hermione during the reading of <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Will_and_Testament_of_Albus_Percival_Wulfric_Brian_Dumbledore" title="The Last Will and Testament of Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore's will</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Once Ron, Harry, and Hermione were all convened at the<a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow"> Burrow</a>, they made plans to leave, much to the displeasure of Ron's worried mother. During the preparations for Bill's wedding, Mrs Weasley set Ron, Harry, and Hermione to separate tasks to prevent them from planning. On Harry's seventeenth birthday, Ron gave Harry a copy of <i><a href="/wiki/Twelve_Fail-Safe_Ways_to_Charm_Witches" title="Twelve Fail-Safe Ways to Charm Witches">Twelve Fail-Safe Ways to Charm Witches</a></i>. Later that evening, <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> <a href="/wiki/Rufus_Scrimgeour" title="Rufus Scrimgeour">Rufus Scrimgeour</a> visited the Burrow to dispense the contents of Dumbledore's will. He questioned the trio, and Ron let slip that they had no idea why <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Dumbledore</a> would bequeath anything to him. Ron received Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Escape_from_the_Burrow">Escape from the Burrow</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=42" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Escape from the Burrow">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Escape from the Burrow"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Ron </b>: "<i>You know, we're not far from the <a href="/wiki/Leaky_Cauldron" title="Leaky Cauldron">Leaky Cauldron</a> here, it's only in Charing Cross —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Ron, we can't!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron </b>: "<i>Not to stay there, but to find out what's going on!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>We know what's going on! Voldemort's taken over the Ministry, what else do we need to know?</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; The trio looking for a safe place to stay after escaping the Burrow<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>The trio attended the wedding for which, all summer, they had been forced to prepare the <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">Burrow</a>; the marrying couple was Ron's older brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> to <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a> on 1 August. Ron was irked and jealous that <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> was a guest, especially since he immediately complimented Hermione, who Ron quickly asked to dance shortly afterwards. When Viktor Krum asked who he thought was Barny Weasley (though it was really Harry in disguise) about the pair, he was somewhat disappointed to learn that they were "<i>sort of</i>" together, but not officially a couple.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Ron_stupefy.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20110406000135" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron stupefy.JPG" data-image-key="Ron_stupefy.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Ron_stupefy.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110406000135" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Ron_stupefy.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20110406000135" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Ron_stupefy.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110406000135" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron stupefy.JPG" data-image-key="Ron_stupefy.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/Ron_stupefy.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110406000135" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_stupefy.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron casting a <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a> in the café while battling Death Eaters</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The celebrations were interrupted with the news that the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> had fallen to Voldemort, and Hermione Disapparated herself, Ron, and Harry away from the danger to <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Court_Road" title="Tottenham Court Road">Tottenham Court Road</a>. This was the starting point to the trio's adventure and search for the Horcruxes they needed to bring down Lord Voldemort. After they arrived at Luchino café they were ambushed by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a> and <a href="/wiki/Thorfinn_Rowle" title="Thorfinn Rowle">Thorfinn Rowle</a> there and a skirmish broke out. After stunning and wiping the memories of the Death Eaters, the trio took refuge in Harry's inherited house <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> left to him by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Infiltration_of_the_Ministry_of_Magic">Infiltration of the Ministry of Magic</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=43" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Infiltration of the Ministry of Magic">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Infiltration of the Ministry of Magic"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Dad said everyone from Magical Maintenance wears navy blue robes.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>But you never told us that!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Discussion of the Ministry infiltration plan<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128092906" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Catching the crook.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20190128092906" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190128092906" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20190128092906" decoding="async" width="251" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 HQ still Catching the crook.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/2b/DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20190128092906" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_HQ_still_Catching_the_crook.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus</a> talking to the trio about the Horcrux locket</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>There, the trio learned from <a href="/wiki/Kreacher" title="Kreacher">Kreacher</a> that <a href="/wiki/Regulus_Black" title="Regulus Black">Regulus Black</a> had stolen the Horcrux Voldemort had made of <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Slytherin's Locket</a> in 1979, and that it had been stolen from 12 Grimmauld Place by Mundungus Fletcher. Under interrogation, he informed them that the locket was now in the possession of <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While they were waiting for Kreacher to fetch Mundungus, they were visited by <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>. He informed the trio about the goings on in the wider wizarding world. He told them that Harry was now the most wanted wizard in Britain and that <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a> witches and wizards were being rounded up. Ron immediately said that he would vouch for Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Infiltration.png/revision/latest?cb=20160812020055" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Infiltration.png" data-image-key="Infiltration.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Infiltration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160812020055" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Infiltration.png/revision/latest?cb=20160812020055" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Infiltration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160812020055" decoding="async" width="245" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Infiltration.png" data-image-key="Infiltration.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/54/Infiltration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20160812020055" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Infiltration.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio disguised during their infiltration of the ministry. Ron is on the far right</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>They formulated a plan to <a href="/wiki/Infiltration_of_the_Ministry_of_Magic" title="Infiltration of the Ministry of Magic">infiltrate the Ministry</a>, involving the use of <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> to assume the forms of Ministry employees Reginald Cattermole, Albert Runcorn and Mafalda Hopkirk. Ron, disguised as <a href="/wiki/Reginald_Cattermole" title="Reginald Cattermole">Reginald Cattermole</a>, quickly found himself forced to separate from his friends, as Death Eater and new head of the <a href="/wiki/Department_of_Magical_Law_Enforcement" title="Department of Magical Law Enforcement">Department of Magical Law Enforcement</a>, <a href="/wiki/Corban_Yaxley" title="Corban Yaxley">Yaxley</a>, demanded that "Cattermole" fix the rain in his office.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ron was in over his head, but may have found a solution to the problem after asking Arthur, who had no idea of Ron's true identity, for help. The trio reunited after Harry and Hermione stole the locket from Umbridge and freed some Muggle-born witches and wizards being held by the <a href="/wiki/Muggle-Born_Registration_Commission" title="Muggle-Born Registration Commission">Muggle-Born Registration Commission</a>, and then escaped, but were forced to abandon Grimmauld Place as a hideout. Ron splinched himself during their escape into the countryside and was weakened by his injury. After receiving some treatment from Hermione, Ron fretted over the fate of the Cattermoles.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Exit_and_homecoming">Exit and homecoming</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=44" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Exit and homecoming">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=44" title="Edit section: Exit and homecoming"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>So why are you still here?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Search me.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>Go home then</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Yeah, maybe I will!’ Didn’t you hear what they said about my sister? But you don’t give a rat’s fart, do you, it’s only the Forbidden Forest, Harry I’ve-Faced-Worse Potter doesn’t care what happens to her in here, well, I do, all right, giant spiders and mental stuff –</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron lashes out against Harry resulting in an intense row<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140620222047" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry and Ron arguing.gif" data-image-key="Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140620222047" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140620222047" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140620222047" decoding="async" width="250" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry and Ron arguing.gif" data-image-key="Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1d/Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140620222047" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_and_Ron_arguing.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Harry fight right before Ron abandons the <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a> hunt</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Afterward, weeks passed with no further progress. This, as well as the locket's negative influence, caused great tension and animosity amongst the group of friends. When he wore the locket, Ron was sullen and suspicious, lashing out at his friends and continuously complaining. Ron abruptly abandoned his friends one evening after getting into a fight with Harry over the additional task of locating <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a> in order to destroy the locket. He accused Harry of having no plan and of not being very concerned about <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>, whom they had learned was punished back at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. When Ron asked if Hermione was going with him and she told him that she was staying, he accused her of choosing Harry over him, and left, despite Hermione screaming and crying for him to come back.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As soon as he was outside the influence of the Horcrux, Ron came to his senses and tried to return. However, he had a run-in with <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> first, who interrogated him. Ron claimed to be <a href="/wiki/Stanley_Shunpike" title="Stanley Shunpike">Stan Shunpike</a>, and then took an opportunity to escape. He apparated numerous times to try to find Harry and Hermione, splinching fingernails off at one point, but could not find them. He then went to stay with Bill and Fleur at their new home, <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>. Soon after Christmas, Ron used the <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a> Dumbledore bequeathed him to locate his friends.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Locket_destruction.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140807061926" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Locket destruction.gif" data-image-key="Locket_destruction.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Locket_destruction.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140807061926" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Locket_destruction.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140807061926" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Locket_destruction.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140807061926" decoding="async" width="245" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Locket destruction.gif" data-image-key="Locket_destruction.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/00/Locket_destruction.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140807061926" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Locket_destruction.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron returns to the hunt and destroys the <a href="/wiki/Slytherin%27s_Locket" title="Slytherin&#39;s Locket">locket</a> Horcrux</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron made his way to the <a href="/wiki/Forest_of_Dean" title="Forest of Dean">Forest of Dean</a>, where he arrived just in time to rescue Harry from drowning in a semi-frozen pond. When Ron attempted to use Godric Gryffindor's Sword to destroy the locket, horrible incorporeal images of Harry and Hermione came forth which cruelly mocked Ron about his many insecurities, including his fears that Hermione would choose Harry over him. This brought Ron to the point of tears. However, Ron successfully stabbed the Horcrux with Godric Gryffindor's Sword.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Afterwards, Harry took Ron aside to assuage his fears about Harry and Hermione. Saving Harry's life earned him Harry's forgiveness, but Hermione — who was unaware of what the Horcrux had done — was still furious with him for his abandonment for some time and attacked him mercilessly upon sight until Harry cast a <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> to stop her.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Visit_to_the_Lovegood_House">Visit to the Lovegood House</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=45" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Visit to the Lovegood House">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Visit to the Lovegood House"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Aha! That's got to be Luna's house, who else would live in a place like that? It looks like a giant rook!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron describing the Lovegood's house<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Upon his return, Ron was happy to the point of giddiness, because he thought that they had an ally out there somewhere. He sought to hide this happiness when around Hermione in an act of contrition. When Hermione proposed a trip to the Lovegood's house to investigate a recurring symbol, Ron wholeheartedly agreed. Harry privately accused Ron of only agreeing to get back on Hermione's good side, a fact that he did not deny stating, "<i>All's fair in love and war, and this is a bit of both.</i>"<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest?cb=20141031144607" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="111" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-image-key="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141031144607" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest?cb=20141031144607" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141031144607" decoding="async" width="246" height="111" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-image-key="Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/80/Xenophilius-Lovegood.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20141031144607" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Xenophilius-Lovegood.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio speaking with Xenophilius Lovegood at his home, near the village of <a href="/wiki/Ottery_St_Catchpole" title="Ottery St Catchpole">Ottery St Catchpole</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The trio learned of the existence of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a> from <a href="/wiki/Xenophilius_Lovegood" title="Xenophilius Lovegood">Xenophilius Lovegood</a>. Xenophilius, worried for his daughter <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna</a>, who was being held hostage by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, tried to capture the trio. They narrowly escaped, Hermione engineering it in a way that preserved Ron's alibi of being sick at home. While Harry obsessed over the Hallows, Ron and Hermione thought they should focus on finding the Horcruxes, as Dumbledore had instructed them. During Harry's period of listless obsession, Ron's leadership qualities began to show. He suggested that they search many wizarding settlements for clues if only to be in motion and actively searching.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=46" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Skirmish at Malfoy Manor"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Bellatrix Lestrange</b>: "<i>All except... except for the Mudblood.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>No! You can have me, keep me!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Bellatrix Lestrange</b>: "<i>If she dies under questioning, I'll take you next. Blood traitor is next to Mudblood in my book. Take them downstairs, Greyback, and make sure they are secure, but do nothing more to them — yet.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron begging <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a> while in <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180115183807" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Greyback Hermione and Ron.jpg" data-image-key="Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180115183807" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180115183807" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180115183807" decoding="async" width="250" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Greyback Hermione and Ron.jpg" data-image-key="Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/62/Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180115183807" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Greyback_Hermione_and_Ron.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione held captive at the Malfoy Manor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the Easter holidays of 1998, the trio was captured by a gang of <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a> led by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> after Harry accidentally  broke the <a href="/wiki/Taboo" title="Taboo">Taboo curse</a> on Voldemort's name. Hermione hit Harry in the face with a <a href="/wiki/Stinging_Jinx" title="Stinging Jinx">Stinging Hex</a> in order to disguise him. Harry, Hermione, and Ron quickly lied and gave fake names; Harry being Vernon Dudley, Hermione being <a href="/wiki/Penelope_Clearwater" title="Penelope Clearwater">Penelope Clearwater</a>, and Ron being Stan Shunpike. Ron was beaten (his mouth extremely bloody) and was then forced to use another name, Barny Weasley. This was due to the Snatchers already knowing who Stan Shunpike was. The Snatchers also found Godric Gryffindor's sword in their tent, there was no explaining that.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>They were then brought to Malfoy Manor, where Lucius Malfoy attempted to get his son to identify Harry. Draco said that he did not know whether it was Harry or not, but immediately recognised Ron and Hermione. The trio then meet with Bellatrix Lestrange, whom separated them. Ron tried to persuade Bellatrix to take him for questioning instead of Hermione. She responded that she would interrogate him next if Hermione died during questioning, as "<i>blood-traitor was next to mud-blood in her book</i>". Ron was forced into the dungeon with Harry, <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, and the goblin <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a>. In the dungeon they found Luna and Mr Ollivander, whom were captured in 1996.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/B7C23M1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161209020454" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C23M1.jpg" data-image-key="B7C23M1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/B7C23M1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209020454" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/B7C23M1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161209020454" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/B7C23M1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209020454" decoding="async" width="250" height="98" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C23M1.jpg" data-image-key="B7C23M1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/B7C23M1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161209020454" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C23M1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Dobby dropping the chandelier allowing the prisoners time to escape</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hermione was kept upstairs and tortured by Bellatrix, her screams reducing Ron to tears. The group was saved by <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a>, who was sent by <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>. He freed Harry and Ron to run upstairs to save Hermione, who managed to lie under torture about where they had obtained <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Gryffindor's Sword</a>. Ron disarmed Bellatrix after she avoided a chandelier dropped by Dobby, and pulled Hermione from the wreckage of the fallen chandelier, Disapparating them both to Bill and Fleur's home <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>. They stayed there with Luna, Fleur, Bill, Mr Ollivander, and Griphook. He attended the burial of Dobby, where he humbly gave him his shoes and socks.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Gringotts_break-in">Gringotts break-in</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=47" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Gringotts break-in">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Gringotts break-in"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Travers</b>: "<i>Who is your friend? I do not recognise him.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>This is Dragomir Despard. He speaks very little English, but he is in sympathy with the Dark Lord's aims. He has travelled here from Transylvania to see our new regime.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; A disguised Hermione introducing a disguised Ron to Travers<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 253px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108172400" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="251" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180108172400" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108172400" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180108172400" decoding="async" width="251" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1a/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/251?cb=20180108172400" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-255.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio speaking with Griphook about what lies within the Lestrange vault at Gringotts</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>At the cottage Hermione recovered and she, Ron, and Harry planned to break into <a href="/wiki/Gringotts_Wizarding_Bank" title="Gringotts Wizarding Bank">Gringotts Wizarding Bank</a> in order to take<a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup"> Hufflepuff's cup</a>, and a <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcrux</a>, within the <a href="/wiki/Lestrange_Vault" title="Lestrange Vault">Lestrange Vault</a>. <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a> the goblin agreed to help them in exchange for Gryffindor's Sword. Ron, knowing that the sword was needed to destroy Horcruxes was reluctant to let Harry part with it. Harry suggested that they delay handing the sword over until the Horcruxes were destroyed. As the planning went forward, Ron along with Harry and Hermione found Griphook to be increasingly distasteful.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310225013" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Break-in 1998.jpg" data-image-key="Break-in_1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180310225013" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180310225013" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180310225013" decoding="async" width="246" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Break-in 1998.jpg" data-image-key="Break-in_1998.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/31/Break-in_1998.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180310225013" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Break-in_1998.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione, disguised as Dragomir Despard and <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>On the morning of 1 May, 1998, they broke into Gringotts with Hermione disguised as Bellatrix Lestrange, Ron as a fictional foreign wizard named "Dragomir Despard," and Harry under his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a> with Griphook. As they were headed down into the vaults, the Gringotts defences (the <a href="/wiki/Thief%27s_Downfall" title="Thief&#39;s Downfall">Thief's Downfall</a> in particular) were set against them, and Ron's disguise melted away. Once in the vault, it was discovered that all the treasure had <a href="/wiki/Doubling_Charm" title="Doubling Charm">Geminio</a> and <a href="/wiki/Flagrante_Curse" title="Flagrante Curse">Flagrante</a> curses put on them. Although they were betrayed by Griphook, the trio obtained Helga Hufflepuff's cup and escaped the wizarding bank on the back of a dragon.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_of_Hogwarts"><a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=48" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Battle of Hogwarts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>They can help. We don't know where it is. We've got to find it fast. We don't have to tell them it's a Horcrux.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron persuades Harry to let Dumbledore's Army help<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 235px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/Hogsmeade.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20161206055316" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="233" height="153" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hogsmeade.jpeg" data-image-key="Hogsmeade.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/Hogsmeade.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/233?cb=20161206055316" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/Hogsmeade.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20161206055316" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/Hogsmeade.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/233?cb=20161206055316" decoding="async" width="233" height="153" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hogsmeade.jpeg" data-image-key="Hogsmeade.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4c/Hogsmeade.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/233?cb=20161206055316" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hogsmeade.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The trio <a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparate</a> into Hogsmeade before the start of the final battle</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After getting off the dragon escaping from the wizarding bank, Ron saw Harry having one of his visions. He was told that <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> finally knew that they were hunting Horcruxes and that the final one was at Hogwarts. Harry, Ron, and Hermione apparated under the <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility cloak</a> to Hogsmeade looking for a way into Hogwarts. They were soon cornered by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> set to watch the town. Ron drew his wand ready to fight them, but Harry suggested that advantage lay in stealth and that attacking would give away their position. Once the Death Eaters ordered <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> to search the town for the trio, Harry was forced to perform the Patronus Charm. After Harry's Patronus chased away the Dementors the trio found refuge in the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A heated discussion with the proprietor followed, who turned out to be <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>. The discussion revolved around Harry's mission and the seeming defeat of the Order of the Phoenix. After this they were lead into Hogwarts by a badly beaten <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, whom in Harry's absence became the defcto leader of the D.A. They arrived in the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a> and found that the reformed Dumbledore's Army was hiding out there. Harry whom had developed trust issues, did not like the idea of allowing the other DA members to help. Ron persuaded Harry to let the others do so anyway.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 248px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108173526" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="246" height="106" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180108173526" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180108173526" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180108173526" decoding="async" width="246" height="106" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/82/Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/246?cb=20180108173526" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter7-movie-screencaps.com-6084.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron destroying the cup in the Chamber</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Harry searched for <a href="/wiki/Rowena_Ravenclaw%27s_Diadem" class="mw-redirect" title="Rowena Ravenclaw&#39;s Diadem">Ravenclaw's diadem</a>, Ron and Hermione entered the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> to retrieve basilisk fangs. Ron mimicked the <a href="/wiki/Parseltongue" title="Parseltongue">Parseltongue</a> he had heard Harry use to open Salazar Slytherin's locket and succeeded in gaining entrance to the Chamber. Hermione used the fangs to destroy the Horcrux of <a href="/wiki/Helga_Hufflepuff%27s_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="Helga Hufflepuff&#39;s Cup">Hufflepuff's cup</a>, and they then reunited with Harry. When Ron expressed desire to evacuate the <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a> from the Kitchens, Hermione, who had always been concerned for creatures so often mistreated by society, was so touched that she ran, nuzzled and kissed him, much to Ron's delight. However, their kiss was interrupted by Harry, who pointed out that there was a war going on and that they could carry on later, to which Ron pointed out there might not be later.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140308202617" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="104" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fiend fyre Fleeing GIF.gif" data-image-key="Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140308202617" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140308202617" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140308202617" decoding="async" width="245" height="104" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fiend fyre Fleeing GIF.gif" data-image-key="Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/41/Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140308202617" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fiend_fyre_Fleeing_GIF.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> and Ron run from the towering flames</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry, Ron, and Hermione entered the Room of Requirement to find Ravenclaw's diadem, but were ambushed by <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Malfoy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Crabbe</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Goyle</a>. When Crabbe unleashed a <a href="/wiki/Fiendfyre" title="Fiendfyre">cursed fire</a>, the trio escaped by means of broomsticks; Harry saved Draco, and Ron and Hermione saved Goyle. They then witnessed the death of Ron's brother Fred in combat, which devastated Ron, who wanted revenge. Hermione managed to calm him by reminding him that they would have to fight on their way to finding <a href="/wiki/Nagini" title="Nagini">Nagini</a>, Voldemort's final Horcrux. The trio made their way to the <a href="/wiki/Shrieking_Shack" title="Shrieking Shack">Shrieking Shack</a>, and witnessed the snake kill <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> on Voldemort's orders. While dying, Severus Snape's memories leaked out of him, which Harry collected into a glass phial to latter view in the headmaster's office.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest?cb=20150904231059" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" decoding="async" width="250" height="97" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="B7C36M2 Voldemort vanquished.png" data-image-key="B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/b/b0/B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20150904231059" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:B7C36M2_Voldemort_vanquished.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron witnessing Harry's final defeat of Lord Voldemort</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the pause in the Battle of Hogwarts, Ron went to the <a href="/wiki/Great_Hall" title="Great Hall">Great Hall</a>, where Bill comforted him over Fred's death and Hermione comforted Ginny. Harry went up to Dumbledore's office and emptied Snape's memories into the Pensieve. He entered the <a href="/wiki/Pensieve" title="Pensieve">Pensieve</a> and finally learned the truth of it all. After emerging from the Pensieve, he made use of the distraction to slip out and confront Voldemort. Following his alleged death, the battle resumed, and Ron and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> brought <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> down together. Ron witnessed Harry defeat Lord Voldemort once and for all, and survived the battle without serious injury.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="After_Hogwarts_(1998-2014)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="After_Hogwarts_.281998-2014.29">After Hogwarts <span class="template-c">(1998-2014)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=49" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: After Hogwarts (1998-2014)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: After Hogwarts (1998-2014)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Albus Potter</b>: "<i>Why are they all </i>staring<i>?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Don't let it worry you. It's me. I'm extremely famous.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Why everyone on the platform was staring at them<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<p>Ron never received a seventh year of education at Hogwarts. Instead of completing his education, he moved on to become an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> (along with Harry) at the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PotterCast_28-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PotterCast-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Their work in the Ministry revolutionised the Auror department, and along with Hermione the trio helped <i>"make a new world</i>" for the wizarding community.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Two years after he started at the Auror Office, he left to help his brother <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> at <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a> in <a href="/wiki/Diagon_Alley" title="Diagon Alley">Diagon Alley</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PM-QWC_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-QWC-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> His decision to do so was questioned by <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a>, who thought that Ron was tired of standing in Harry's shadow, and wrote in her gossip column that Ron was likely mentally ill (this must, of course, be taken with more than a small pinch of salt due to Rita's habit of writing scathing lies in articles), having said himself that the <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">Horcrux hunt</a> had "<i>took its toll</i>" on him.<sup id="cite_ref-PM-QWC_26-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-QWC-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime between 1998 and 2006, Ron married Hermione, and later the couple had two children: <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo</a>. Ron was also the godfather and uncle of Harry and Ginny's oldest son.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> At some point, Ron, Harry, and Hermione were all featured on <a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Cards</a> for their accomplishments, which Ron considered his "<i>finest hour</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-CFC_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CFC-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Ron himself noted that he and Hermione were quite young when they were married and that he became rather drunk afterward, having very little memory of the night after the ceremony.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Recent_life_(2014-)"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Recent_life_.282014-.29">Recent life <span class="template-c">(2014-)</span></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=50" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Recent life (2014-)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Recent life (2014-)"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="2014_Quidditch_World_Cup">2014 Quidditch World Cup</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=51" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: 2014 Quidditch World Cup">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=51" title="Edit section: 2014 Quidditch World Cup"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Ron, Hermione and their children Rose and Hugo all attended the final of the <a href="/wiki/2014_Quidditch_World_Cup" title="2014 Quidditch World Cup">427th Quidditch World Cup</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Patagonian_Desert" title="Patagonian Desert">Patagonian Desert</a> in July 2014, alongside Harry, Ginny, James, Albus, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a>, Neville, Hannah, Luna, Rolf, Bill, Fleur, Victoire, and potentially others.<sup id="cite_ref-PM-QWC_26-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-QWC-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> <span>Ron also became close with Harry's children, one of whom, James, was his godson. Lily Luna Potter and Ron's son were close in age and good friends, as were Ron's daughter and Albus Severus Potter.</span>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Calamity_and_nineteen_years_later">Calamity and nineteen years later</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=52" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Calamity and nineteen years later">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=52" title="Edit section: Calamity and nineteen years later"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 244px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140813031055" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="242" height="123" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione &amp; Ron with their children at platform nine and three quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_&amp;_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20140813031055" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140813031055" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20140813031055" decoding="async" width="242" height="123" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione &amp; Ron with their children at platform nine and three quarters.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_&amp;_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9e/Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20140813031055" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_%26_Ron_with_their_children_at_platform_nine_and_three_quarters.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron seeing his daughter off to <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">platform 9¾</a> in 2017</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>During the <a href="/wiki/Calamity" title="Calamity">Calamity</a>, Ron would assist the members of the <a href="/wiki/Statute_of_Secrecy_Task_Force" title="Statute of Secrecy Task Force">Statute of Secrecy Task Force</a> who pursued a Professor Profession when he ran into them in the Leaky Cauldron by debating on defensive footwork during duelling, causing them to gain increased resilience.<sup id="cite_ref-WU_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WU-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August of 2017, Ron, having settled into a rotund middle age, obtained a Muggle driving licence. He also admitted putting a <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a> on the Muggle driving inspector because he had forgotten to use his wing mirror properly, excusing this mistake because casting a <a href="/wiki/Supersensory_Charm" title="Supersensory Charm">Supersensory Charm</a> would be more effective. That year, he and Hermione sent their daughter off for her first year at Hogwarts, and Ron encouraged Rose to be Sorted into <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor House</a> and to beat <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> in marks. He hugged Hugo gently.<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 244px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811150508" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="242" height="101" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter Epilogue.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20180811150508" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180811150508" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20180811150508" decoding="async" width="242" height="101" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter Epilogue.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/69/Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/242?cb=20180811150508" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter_Epilogue.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A 37 year old Ron with his family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As the train faded away, Ron remembered his time at Hogwarts and how he would love to be going back. At a gathering with Hermione, Harry and Ginny, they talked about the meeting and Ron attempted to cheer everyone up by making jokes which led them them telling him to stop. Before the start of the new school year, Ron and Hermione told Rose to try and befriend Albus again since they have drifted apart since starting Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_41-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fighting_Delphini">Fighting Delphini</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=53" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fighting Delphini">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Fighting Delphini"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>A while later, Ron attended a meeting at the Ministry of Magic. Hermione was worried about how Harry was having nightmares and his scar was hurting again. Ron got into an argument with Draco Malfoy.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 243px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160802193002" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="241" height="127" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron Hermione cursed child.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20160802193002" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160802193002" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20160802193002" decoding="async" width="241" height="127" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron Hermione cursed child.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e1/Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/241?cb=20160802193002" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_Hermione_cursed_child.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hermione and Ron standing in her office at the Ministry of Magic</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Albus and Scorpius meddled with time, they changed Ron's life. In one <a href="/wiki/Alternate_reality" title="Alternate reality">alternate reality</a>, Ron helped Harry and Ginny find Albus. Ron never married Hermione and instead married Padma Patil. In another alternate reality where Voldemort won, Ron was in hiding with Hermione as a member of what remained of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. They were visited by <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and Scorpius who told them about the original timeline where they won. Ron agreed to help correct time by time-travelling to the moments where Albus and Scorpius changed time and use a <a href="/wiki/Shield_Charm" title="Shield Charm">Shield Charm</a> to stop them. However, when they stopped them the first time, they returned to a present that hadn't changed much. They were attacked by <a href="/wiki/Dementor" title="Dementor">Dementors</a> and Ron and Hermione sacrifice their souls after professing their love for each other to give Scorpius time to escape. Their sacrifice, combined with Snape's a short time later, allowed Scorpius to return to the Second Task and set things right completely.
</p><p>When the original timeline was restored, Ron was asked to attend a meeting with <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> to talk about what happened. He turned up late having somehow ended up in the kitchens instead. Ron, Hermione, Harry, Ginny and Draco were very forgiving of Albus and Scorpius so McGonagall reminded them of the great dangers of what they had done.
</p><p>When Albus and Scorpius were kidnapped by <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphi</a> and made to time-travel to 31 October, 1981, Ron went with Hermione, Harry, Ginny and Draco to the past to save them and stop Delphi. Ron helped Harry duel Delphi and they apprehended her. Ron then returned to the present where Delphi was sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_appearance">Physical appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=54" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Physical appearance">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Physical appearance"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602175711" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="200" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg" data-image-key="Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140602175711" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602175711" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140602175711" decoding="async" width="150" height="200" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg" data-image-key="Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20140602175711" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron-Weasley-harry-potter-and-the-deathly-hallows-movies-17179892-1919-2560.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron at age 17</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron inherited the typical <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">Weasley family</a> traits: fiery red hair and a freckled complexion. When he became embarrassed, his ears notably turned red. He had blue eyes, a long nose, and was described as being very tall and lanky, with big hands and feet.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> In this way, his stature was similar to those of his older brothers <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a>, rather than the heavily built <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HPLE_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HPLE-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
