</p><p>His sister <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> once joked to the trio that Ron had a <a href="/wiki/Pygmy_Puff" title="Pygmy Puff">Pygmy Puff</a> <a href="/wiki/Tattoo" title="Tattoo">tattoo</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> though it is doubtful that the remark had any truth in it.
</p><p>By 2014, when he was at the age of 34, <a href="/wiki/Rita_Skeeter" title="Rita Skeeter">Rita Skeeter</a> remarked on a <i><a href="/wiki/Daily_Prophet" title="Daily Prophet">Daily Prophet</a></i> gossip column that his "<i>famous ginger hair appears to be thinning slightly</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-PM-QWC_26-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PM-QWC-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>By 2017, Ron had settled into a round middle age<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> and was later described to be getting "a bit of a gut" by his nephew, yet hiding it extremely well.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality_and_traits">Personality and traits</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=55" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Personality and traits">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Personality and traits"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>...Ron's got all those brothers to compete against at home and you're his best friend, and you're really famous --he's always shunted to one side whenever people see you, and he puts up with you and he never mentions it...</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Description of Ron's loyalty, despite his insecurities.<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/83/180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130812162023" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg" data-image-key="180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/83/180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130812162023" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/83/180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20130812162023" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/83/180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130812162023" decoding="async" width="180" height="270" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg" data-image-key="180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/83/180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20130812162023" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:180px-Ron-Order-of-the-Phoenix-ronald-weasley-4959523-285-428.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron in his fifth year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was a very loyal, brave, strong and humourous person, but sometimes immature, and insensitive.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> He had a sardonic, wisecracking sense of humour that often brought his friends laughter and relaxation. However, as <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> pointed out, his humour could occasionally be hurtful, even if unintentionally.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> During his time searching for <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> with <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and Hermione, Ron matured greatly, and even took to leading the trio when Harry temporarily fell into a depressive mood.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Though his loyalty and bravery never faltered Ron's character was also marked by occasional jealousy and insecurity rising from feeling overshadowed by his five older brothers and his parents' constant comparisons between him and their other children. He could be argumentative, a trait particularly displayed in his bickering with the equally argumentative and occasionally highly critical Hermione. Though their bickering was frequent, it was never malicious (with the brief exception of sixth year) and generally a way to hide their deeper feelings for each other. Inheriting the Weasley trait of a strong temper Ron was not above provocation especially when dealing with the spiteful treatment of Professor Snape and the bigotry and hatred of Draco Malfoy. Always willing to stand up for his friends and family even when angry with them, Ron never stopped standing up for Hermione when she faced Muggle-born related prejudice and hatred. He also stood by Harry's side when he was met with disbelief and scorn from his classmates and Wizard society in general. Ron frequently demonstrated great bravery in attempting to protect those he loved, from facing his arachnophobia to stand by Harry in his second year<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> to trying to take Hermione's place when <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> isolated her for interrogation with the <a href="/wiki/Cruciatus_Curse" title="Cruciatus Curse">Cruciatus Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Ron</b>: "<i>What are you doing? Are you staying, or what?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>I... Yes — yes, I'm staying. Ron, we said we'd go with Harry, we said we'd help —</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>I get it. You choose him.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Ron, no — please — come back, come back!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron abandoning Harry and Hermione after an intense row<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 238px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Ron_as_Keeper.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140501121334" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="236" height="135" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron as Keeper.gif" data-image-key="Ron_as_Keeper.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Ron_as_Keeper.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20140501121334" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Ron_as_Keeper.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140501121334" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Ron_as_Keeper.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20140501121334" decoding="async" width="236" height="135" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron as Keeper.gif" data-image-key="Ron_as_Keeper.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/33/Ron_as_Keeper.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/236?cb=20140501121334" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_as_Keeper.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron playing <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> as <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As a boy, Ron was very sensitive about his family's poverty, and sometimes embarrassed by them. Many, if not all, of Ron's possessions were hand-me-downs, including his robes, school books, wand, and even a pet rat whom he called <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>. His family's lack of finances often made Ron a target for taunting by <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, a spoiled, arrogant <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Ron was also prone to insecurity about his abilities, when compared to his older siblings and to his famous best friend. When he felt insecure or embarrassed, it was noted that his ears turned red. This became his tell-tale sign of his anger and embarrassment.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> He felt as if he was consistently overshadowed by the legacy of his older brothers and the fame of Harry; this lead to a feeling of being "<i>second-best</i>".
</p><p>Although passionate about Quidditch, especially the <a href="/wiki/Chudley_Cannons" title="Chudley Cannons">Chudley Cannons</a>, and a fine flyer, Ron had a problem with nerves, and sometimes his playing ability suffered for it.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> revealed that Ron's deepest fears were that his mother loved him least and that Hermione preferred Harry to him.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He also suffered from arachnophobia, a fear originating from his brother <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> transfiguring his teddy bear into a spider when Ron was a child.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ron's point of view on many topics was often that of the stereotypical wizard, which clashed many times with those of Harry and Hermione because they were both raised by <a href="/wiki/Non-magic_people" title="Non-magic people">Muggles</a>; but in exchange, he was typically more aware of standard factors abided by wizardkind. Examples of this are that while he liked Lupin the entire third year, the moment he discovered that Lupin was a werewolf he exclaimed "<i>Get away from me, <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>!</i>"; that he was more shocked and disgusted than Harry and Hermione at discovering that Hagrid was half giant; and when he got into an argument with <a href="/wiki/Griphook" title="Griphook">Griphook</a> over wizards not giving <a href="/wiki/Goblin" title="Goblin">goblins</a> wands. However, he was clearly very much appreciative of Dobby's sacrifice for them, as he helped Harry dig the grave, found it difficult to say stuff at the grave (it is mentioned it "<i>came out thickly</i>", implying he was choked up), and he had sat on a rock and stripped off his shoes and socks, giving them to Dobby to be buried in.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Ron_eating_chicken.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160730204129" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron eating chicken.gif" data-image-key="Ron_eating_chicken.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Ron_eating_chicken.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160730204129" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Ron_eating_chicken.gif/revision/latest?cb=20160730204129" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Ron_eating_chicken.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160730204129" decoding="async" width="250" height="99" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron eating chicken.gif" data-image-key="Ron_eating_chicken.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/34/Ron_eating_chicken.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160730204129" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_eating_chicken.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron showing his fondness for food as he enthusiastically eats chicken legs</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was particularly fond of food. He had a tendency to talk with his mouth full, often to Hermione's disgust, and a great fondness for bacon sandwiches, though he disliked corned beef sandwiches, as mentioned in his first year; his love of food eventually made him settle into a portly middle age. And like Harry, Ron was intelligent, but lacked the motivation to put forth effort in class due to incredible laziness; during their years at school, Ron frequently expected Hermione's help, and when she either refused or was unavailable, he was often dumbfounded about how to proceed. If not for Hermione's help, he would have undoubtedly failed his exams.
</p><p>Ron was also shown to have a habit of swearing. In 1993, he called <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> something that caused Hermione to exclaim: "<i>Ron!</i>". Also, after <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> insulted him, Ron told him to do something he would never have dared say in front of Mrs Weasley. He also called Draco Malfoy a "<i>two face-bastard</i>" during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> after saving him from a Death Eater, and rescuing him for a second time, from death.
</p><p>Ron was brave, to a level which would put him on a par with his best friend Harry; he never hesitated to put himself into extremely dangerous situations with his best friends Harry and Hermione, and as shown many times, he would rather die than have someone else he cared about be harmed. He risked his life on many occasions, and his bravery was not unnoticed by his friends.
</p><p>Ron was also a person who liked to do things the easy way, as he did not like to work hard. This quality was reflected in his first year when he just picked up books from the Hogwarts Library shelves randomly when finding out about <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Flamel" title="Nicolas Flamel">Nicolas Flamel</a>. He also had a tendency to make up predictions for his <a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a> homework, and frequently copied most of his homework from Hermione Granger. However, he could afford to let go of this tendency of his during tougher times, like when he researched information to help <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> in letting off Buckbeak in his third year. His peculiar trait did not seem to vanish, even after he grew up, as he <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">confunded</a> his driving examiner (breaking the International Statute of Secrecy which is considered illegal) and shrugged off his guilt by saying "<i>I could always use a <a href="/wiki/Supersensory_Charm" title="Supersensory Charm">Supersensory Charm</a> for that</i>".
</p><p>Ron was very protective of those he cared about, and this was shown perhaps, best of all, when Ginny was involved in a relationship with <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>. He was, of course, looking out for her, but his temper got the best of him and he lashed out at her, as she did the same to him.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Magical_abilities_and_skills">Magical abilities and skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=56" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=56" title="Edit section: Magical abilities and skills"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 217px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/Ron%27s_dog_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170108234321" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="215" height="176" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron&#39;s dog Patronus.jpg" data-image-key="Ron&#39;s_dog_Patronus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/Ron%27s_dog_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/215?cb=20170108234321" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/Ron%27s_dog_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170108234321" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/Ron%27s_dog_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/215?cb=20170108234321" decoding="async" width="215" height="176" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron&#39;s dog Patronus.jpg" data-image-key="Ron&#39;s_dog_Patronus.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7b/Ron%27s_dog_Patronus.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/215?cb=20170108234321" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron%27s_dog_Patronus.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron's corporeal <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> (form of a Jack Russell Terrier)</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>First — to Mr Ronald Weasley for the best played game of chess Hogwarts has seen in many years, I award Gryffindor house fifty points.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's talent at Wizard's Chess<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Ron was often insecure about his own abilities when compared to his elder brothers and famous best friend. However, once that lessened a bit he proved to be a powerful wizard in his own right. Ron was able to conjure a corporeal <a href="/wiki/Jack_Russell_terrier" title="Jack Russell terrier">Jack Russell terrier</a> Patronus, which is a mark of superior magical ability.
</p>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Wizard%27s_Chess" title="Wizard&#39;s Chess">Wizard's Chess</a></b>: Ron was extremely talented at chess. It was he who taught Harry how to play. Ron and Harry often played Wizard's Chess together when they had free time.<sup id="cite_ref-PS12_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS12-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> In his first year, his logistic ability helped him, Hermione, and Harry play past Professor McGonagall's <a href="/wiki/Chessboard_Chamber" title="Chessboard Chamber">magically Transfigured giant chessboard</a> to get to the Philosopher's Stone and prevent it being stolen by Voldemort. As a result, he got fifty points for his house for "<i>the best played game of chess that Hogwarts has seen these many years</i>", as Dumbledore himself noted.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110926233856" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="93" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron casting Stupefy.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110926233856" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest?cb=20110926233856" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110926233856" decoding="async" width="250" height="93" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron casting Stupefy.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/d/d3/Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110926233856" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_and_Ron_casting_Stupefy.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ronald and Hermione casting the <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a> during the Battle of the Department of Mysteries</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Duelling" title="Duelling">Duelling</a></b>: He was more than capable in battle; it is notable that he survived both the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a><sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a><sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and fought very courageously in both. He fought well in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stunning</a> a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a> while flying. This was seen as such a noticeable feat that Tonks stated that she couldn't believe it and that it was a very hard thing to do.He also <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">disarmed</a> Bellatrix Lestrange, and saved Hermione during the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>. Later he took down <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a> with <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a> and defeated several other Death Eaters during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. He also escaped a group of Snatchers, unharmed after he temporarily left the <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore_and_Harry_Potter%27s_Horcrux_Hunt" title="Albus Dumbledore and Harry Potter&#39;s Horcrux Hunt">Horcrux hunt</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> It should also be noted that Ron had a <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">physical approach to fighting</a> as well as magical, as more than one occasion, he resorted to <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">fighting physically</a> rather than magically especially in his earlier years. He advised Harry to punch <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> if his wand did not work during his first year as well as fought him with Neville during a Quidditch match.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He took this trait to his later years when he wrestled with Wormtail at Malfoy Manor and punched Draco Malfoy after saving his life a second time during the Battle of Hogwarts.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> When Ron became an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, his skills greatly improved as he was able to track down and defeat multiple Death Eaters after the Battle of Hogwarts. He was also shown to help in overpowering <a href="/wiki/Delphini" title="Delphini">Delphini</a> when she tried to go back in time to stop Voldemort from killing Harry Potter when he was a baby.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/RonRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402103336" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="RonRiddikulus.gif" data-image-key="RonRiddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/RonRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190402103336" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/RonRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest?cb=20190402103336" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/RonRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190402103336" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="RonRiddikulus.gif" data-image-key="RonRiddikulus.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/2/25/RonRiddikulus.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190402103336" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:RonRiddikulus.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron repelling his spider <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a> with <i>Riddikulus</i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a></b>: Ron was very skilled in this subject as, in 1996, he managed to achieved an 'Exceeds Expectations' grade on his O.W.L. exam which allowed him to study it further at N.E.W.T. level.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He was able to use succesfully use various defensive spells, such as <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a> which mastered in his third year.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Ron was also the co founder of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> and mastered all the defensive and offensive spells that Harry taught. Ron partcipated in several battles against the <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> (dangerous and powerful <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizards</a>) during the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, which all he fought vigorously and skilfully in, and survived all of them, showing his highly impressive defensive abilites.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> When he became an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a> his defensive and offensive magic greatly improved as he was constantly put up against fighting the <a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Dark_Arts" title="Dark Arts">Dark Arts</a></b>: Ron was shown to be rather good with dark magic, as he was able to succesfully cast many <a href="/wiki/Dark_charm" title="Dark charm">dark charms</a> succesfully. He was able to successfully cast the <a href="/wiki/Slug-vomiting_Charm" title="Slug-vomiting Charm">Slug-vomiting Charm</a> in an attempt to <a href="/wiki/Curse" title="Curse">curse</a> <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> in his second year (although the curse backfired upon himself due his broken wand at that point).<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> Other dark charms Ron mastered were the <a href="/wiki/Knockback_Jinx" title="Knockback Jinx">Knockback Jinx</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POAG_46-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAG-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Impediment_Jinx" title="Impediment Jinx">Impediment Jinx</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Melofors_Jinx" title="Melofors Jinx">Melofors Jinx</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GOFG_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOFG-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Revulsion_Jinx" title="Revulsion Jinx">Revulsion Jinx</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tickling_Hex" title="Tickling Hex">Tickling Hex</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-TCG_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-TCG-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Full_Body-Bind_Curse" title="Full Body-Bind Curse">Full Body-Bind Curse</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Leg-Locker_Curse" title="Leg-Locker Curse">Leg-Locker Curse</a><sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Reductor_Curse" title="Reductor Curse">Reductor Curse</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">Charms</a></b>: Ron was rather good at this field, being able to cast the <a href="/wiki/Levitation_Charm" title="Levitation Charm">Levitation Charm</a> successfully in his first year,<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> and receiving an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' on his O.W.L. exam in the <a href="/wiki/Charms_(class)" title="Charms (class)">subject</a>, allowing him to study it further at N.E.W.T. level.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He was also known to be able to proficiently cast <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus Charm</a> by his <a href="/wiki/Fifth_year" title="Fifth year">fifth year</a>, the latter of which is noted to be extremely advanced and powerful <a href="/wiki/Magic" title="Magic">magic</a> not usually taught on the Hogwarts Curriculum.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> His Patronus assumed the corporeal form of a <a href="/wiki/Jack_Russell_terrier" title="Jack Russell terrier">Jack Russell terrier</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OPM_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OPM-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> He could also cast succesfully cast many simple charms such as the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTPG_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPG-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Cheering_Charm" title="Cheering Charm">Cheering Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Wand-Lighting_Charm" title="Wand-Lighting Charm">Wand-Lighting Charm</a>, <a href="/wiki/Boggart-Banishing_Spell" title="Boggart-Banishing Spell">Boggart-Banishing Spell</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Seize_and_Pull_Charm" title="Seize and Pull Charm">Seize and Pull Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POAG_46-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAG-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Summoning_Charm" title="Summoning Charm">Summoning Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Banishing_Charm" title="Banishing Charm">Banishing Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POAG_46-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAG-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Impervius_Charm" title="Impervius Charm">Impervius Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Severing_Charm" title="Severing Charm">Severing Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Unlocking_Charm" title="Unlocking Charm">Unlocking Charm</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-POAG_46-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POAG-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Locking_Spell" title="Locking Spell">Locking Spell</a><sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and various others. He was also very skilled with <a href="/wiki/Defensive_Charm" title="Defensive Charm">Defensive Charms</a> such as the <a href="/wiki/Disarming_Charm" title="Disarming Charm">Disarming Charm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">Stunning Spell</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Furthermore, he claimed to be able to perform the <a href="/wiki/Supersensory_Charm" title="Supersensory Charm">Supersensory Charm</a> and <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a> in his adult years.<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_41-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Potion" title="Potion">Potions</a></b>: Although Ron had disliked the <a href="/wiki/Potions_(class)" title="Potions (class)">subject</a> just as much as Harry due to Snape and frequently achieved poor results in Potions that was among the worst as a result, when Snape was not around, he proved to be surprisingly talented and proficient in the field, as he was able to achieve an 'Exceeds Expectations' grade on his <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> exam and was one of only twelve students able to go on to <a href="/wiki/Nastily_Exhausting_Wizarding_Test" title="Nastily Exhausting Wizarding Test">N.E.W.T.</a>-level in 1996.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> After becoming an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>, it is safe to assume that Ron had became at least sufficiently adept in <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poisons</a> and <a href="/wiki/Antidote" title="Antidote">antidotes</a> considering it was deemed to be essential as an auror.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Apparition" title="Apparition">Apparition</a></b>: Despite not achieving a licence in his sixth year,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Ron was still able to Apparate during the hunt for the Horcruxes, though he did <a href="/wiki/Splinching" title="Splinching">splinch</a> himself on occasion.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">Transfiguration</a></b>: Ron advanced to N.E.W.T.-level and achieved an 'Exceeds Expectations' on his O.W.L. exam, showing aptitude in the subject.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He was also able to cast <a href="/wiki/Transforming_Spells" title="Transforming Spells">Transforming Spells</a> successfully, including the <a href="/wiki/Avifors_Spell" title="Avifors Spell">Avifors Spell</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lapifors_Spell" title="Lapifors Spell">Lapifors Spell</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOFG_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOFG-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> As an Auror, Ron's skills likely improved as being sufficiently skilled in transfiguring and untransfiguring was essential to the job. He was capable of helping in turning Harry into a doppelganger of Voldemort, further showing he had increased his skills in the field.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a></b>: Ron achieved an '<a href="/wiki/Exceeds_Expectations" title="Exceeds Expectations">Exceeds Expectations</a>' on his O.W.L. exam. He attended N.E.W.T.-level Herbology in his sixth year.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He could also cast Herbology related <a href="/wiki/Charm" title="Charm">charms</a> such as the <a href="/wiki/Fire-Making_Spell" title="Fire-Making Spell">Fire-Making Spell</a><sup id="cite_ref-OOTPG_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTPG-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Herbivicus_Charm" title="Herbivicus Charm">Herbivicus Charm</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-GOFG_47-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOFG-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Divination" title="Divination">Divination</a></b>: Like Harry, Ron disliked <a href="/wiki/Professor" title="Professor">Professor</a> <a href="/wiki/Sybill_Trelawney" title="Sybill Trelawney">Sybill Trelawney</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Divination_(class)" title="Divination (class)">Divination class</a>, but unlike Harry, who entirely lacked ability in the subject, Ron apparently had some innate skill in Divination as he did make at least two accurate predictions. In his first attempt at reading tea leaves, he predicted that Harry would receive "a windfall, unexpected gold".<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Harry received unexpected gold the following year (by winning the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a> after <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> secretly submitted his name). He later inherited gold from his godfather, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, after the death of Sirius. Ron also saw "a blob a bit like a bowler hat" among the tea leaves. <a href="/wiki/Cornelius_Fudge" title="Cornelius Fudge">Cornelius Fudge</a> had a bowler hat when he met with Dumbledore and Harry after <a href="/wiki/Rebirth_of_Tom_Riddle" class="mw-redirect" title="Rebirth of Tom Riddle">Voldemort's re-birth</a>, and refused to believe Harry's story about the incident.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Nonverbal_spell" title="Nonverbal spell">Nonverbal magic</a></b>: Ron was able to <a href="/wiki/Stunning_Spell" title="Stunning Spell">stun</a> a man who attempted to attack <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a> without saying the <a href="/wiki/Incantation" title="Incantation">incantation</a>, which is highly advanced magic.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He is also noted to have been able to achieve this at a young age as demonstrated in his second year when he attempted to "<a href="/wiki/Slug-Vomiting_Charm" class="mw-redirect" title="Slug-Vomiting Charm">curse</a>" Draco when he insulted Hermione. The curse worked without him saying the incantation, even though it backfired due to him using a broken wand.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Astronomy_(class)" title="Astronomy (class)">Astronomy</a></b>: Ron earned on <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> in this subject.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown if he was able to continue on to the N.E.W.T. class, seeing as he did not apply for advancement.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Care_of_Magical_Creatures" title="Care of Magical Creatures">Care of Magical Creatures</a></b>: Ron got an 'Exceeds Expectations' on his <a href="/wiki/Ordinary_Wizarding_Level" title="Ordinary Wizarding Level">O.W.L.</a> in the subject.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He showed talent in handling dangerous <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">creatures</a> like his brother <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie Weasley</a>.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20131228052710" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="109" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron playing Quidditch.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20131228052710" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20131228052710" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20131228052710" decoding="async" width="180" height="109" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron playing Quidditch.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20131228052710" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_playing_Quidditch.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron playing Quidditch</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Flight" title="Flight">Flying</a></b>: Like his brothers, Ron was excellent at flying. He was good enough to be on the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> and he flew successfully during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>. Ron was a reasonably good Keeper for the team, however his performance sometimes suffered due to his lack of confidence, but overall he was a highly talented <a href="/wiki/Broomstick" title="Broomstick">broomstick</a> flyer and <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> player.</li>
<li><b>Tactical thinking</b>: Ron was good with tactical thinking and showed a talent for thinking outside of the box. For example, it was Ron who suggested that Harry use <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a> to try to get <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a>'s memory of telling <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Tom Riddle</a> about the <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and Ron's idea to go to the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> in order to get <a href="/wiki/Basilisk" title="Basilisk">Basilisk</a> fangs to destroy the Horcruxes.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> Ron was also able to keep a level head in highly stressful situations, and was generally more pragmatic than either of his best friends. His knack for strategy allowed him to consistently outclass his peers in both combat and strategy games such as Wizards Chess. His tactical mindset allowed him to recognise Quidditch plays and strategies almost instantly, which is an impressive feat, given that Quidditch is a sport with a three-dimensional playing field.</li>
<li><b>Impersonation</b>: Ron was clever at imitating voices. While at Malfoy Manor, he was able to convincingly imitate Peter Pettigrew to avoid arousing the suspicions of Bellatrix and the Malfoys. He was also able to mimic Parseltongue effectively, which is a rather difficult language to learn or even imitate, enough to open the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> after previously hearing Harry do it.</li>
<li><b>Leadership skills</b>: While it was mostly Harry or Hermione who did the leading, Ron also had relatively good leadership skills as he took charge of the Wizard's Chess obstacle during their search for the Philosophers Stone and ordered Harry and Hermione to continue searching for it when he decided to become a sacrifice in the end. He later formed and co-lead Dumbledores Army alongside Harry and Hermione, and temporarily lead their Horcrux hunt when Harry briefly fell into depression over his obsession for the Deathly Hallows. After the war ended, his leadership skills were again shown when he, Harry and Hermione helped to reform the Auror department and Ministry of Magic, and help reduce the prejudice towards non-pure bloods and other underprivileged magical creatures, and when he co owned Weasley Wizard Wheezes afterwards alongside George Weasley.</li>
<li><b>Business</b>: As Ron co-owned <a href="/wiki/Weasleys%27_Wizard_Wheezes" title="Weasleys&#39; Wizard Wheezes">Weasleys' Wizard Wheezes</a> alongside his brother George after leaving his profession as an Auror, he likely developed good business skills as he helped turn the business into a big "money-spinner" and helped George run it after Fred's death.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Possessions">Possessions</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=57" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Possessions">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Possessions"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>You never get anything new, either, with five brothers. I've got Bill's old robes, Charlie's old wand and Percy's old rat.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron talking about being the youngest son in the family to Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 109px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Ron_weasley_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111106111114" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="107" height="224" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron weasley wand.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_weasley_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Ron_weasley_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/107?cb=20111106111114" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Ron_weasley_wand.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20111106111114" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Ron_weasley_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/107?cb=20111106111114" decoding="async" width="107" height="224" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron weasley wand.jpg" data-image-key="Ron_weasley_wand.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Ron_weasley_wand.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/107?cb=20111106111114" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_weasley_wand.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron's second wand</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_first_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s first wand">Ron's first wand (formerly Charlie Weasley's)</a></b>: Ron initially used his brother <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>'s old, chipped <a href="/wiki/Wand" title="Wand">wand</a>, made of <a href="/wiki/Ash" title="Ash">ash</a> with a <a href="/wiki/Unicorn_hair" title="Unicorn hair">unicorn hair</a> sticking out of the end. He held the wand together with <a href="/wiki/Spello-tape" class="mw-redirect" title="Spello-tape">Spellotape</a> after nearly breaking it in half at the start of his second year, but it malfunctioned dreadfully after this, backfiring spells, making strange noises, and emitting objects out from the wrong end. It eventually exploded when <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a> tried to cast a <a href="/wiki/Memory_Charm" title="Memory Charm">Memory Charm</a> with it on Ron and Harry in the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_second_wand" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s second wand">Ron's second wand (first own wand)</a></b>: Before his third year, he received a wand, fourteen inches, willow and unicorn hair. This wand seemed to suit him better, but he lost it at Malfoy Manor in 1998 and it is questionable whether he ever retrieved it.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s wand">Ron's third wand (formerly Peter Pettigrew's)</a></b>: Ron took this wand from Peter Pettigrew during the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a> and used it from then on; it was made of chestnut, long 9¼ inches and had a Dragon heartstring core.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> It is unknown whether he ever recovered his own wand or kept using Pettigrew's.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a></b>: Ron inherited Scabbers from Percy, who was gifted of an owl (<a href="/wiki/Hermes" title="Hermes">Hermes</a>) by his father in 1991 for becoming a Prefect.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> It was an old, grey rat which missed a toe. Scabbers was already very old when Ron got it, and even if Ron complained about it all the time, saying that Scabbers was useless, he got angry when it seemed that <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a> ate the rat. At the end of Ron's third year, it turned out that Scabbers was actually the unregistered <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, who was believed to have died in 1981.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 112px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pigwidgeon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123054507" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="110" height="147" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pigwidgeon.jpg" data-image-key="Pigwidgeon.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pigwidgeon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/110?cb=20161123054507" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pigwidgeon.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123054507" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pigwidgeon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/110?cb=20161123054507" decoding="async" width="110" height="147" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pigwidgeon.jpg" data-image-key="Pigwidgeon.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ce/Pigwidgeon.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/110?cb=20161123054507" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pigwidgeon.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron's first owl Pigwidgeon</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Pigwidgeon" title="Pigwidgeon">Pigwidgeon</a></b>: Ron's first pet owl he was gifted to him from <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> in June <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, when Sirius used the owl to carry a letter to Harry. Black said that Ron might keep the owl as he didn't have a rat anymore. Pigwidgeon was described by Harry as resembling a "fluffy <a href="/wiki/Golden_Snitch" title="Golden Snitch">snitch</a>". Though Ron acted very rude to Pigwidgeon in public, he was actually very attached to Pig, since this was his first owl. The name was chosen by Ginny Weasley, but Ron thought it was "a stupid name" and tried to change it; it was too late however, and the owl wouldn't respond to anything else.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF5_50-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF5-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Cleansweep_Eleven" title="Cleansweep Eleven">Cleansweep Eleven</a></b>: In the summer of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Ronald Weasley was given a Cleansweep Eleven as a present from his parents for becoming a <a href="/wiki/Prefect" title="Prefect">Prefect</a>, and used it when he played as <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Shooting_Star" title="Shooting Star">Shooting Star</a></b>: Ron had a Shooting Star when he was young.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Weasley_jumper" title="Weasley jumper">Weasley jumpers</a></b>: As every other member of the Weasley family, Ron got from his mother a home-made jumper with a "R", his first initial, as a Christmas gift every year. On Christmas 1991 he complained about his jumpers being "always <i>maroon</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-PS12_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS12-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ron_Weasley%27s_dress_robes" class="mw-redirect" title="Ron Weasley&#39;s dress robes">Dress robes</a></b>: Ron wore a set of dress robes to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>. They were very traditional in style, and thus old-fashioned and frilly, much to Ron's distaste. Ron also owns a second set of dress robes, a present from the twins in the summer break of <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. These robes were bought with some of Harry's Triwizard winnings, as a stipulation of him giving the money to Fred and George. These robes were only mentioned, never described.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_sweetheart_necklace" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s sweetheart necklace">Sweetheart necklace</a></b>: Ron received the <a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_sweetheart_necklace" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s sweetheart necklace">necklace</a> from <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a> as a Christmas present in 1996, though it is unlikely that he kept it following their break up.<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 112px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Ron%27sNecklace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090418231902" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="110" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron&#39;sNecklace.jpg" data-image-key="Ron&#39;sNecklace.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Ron%27sNecklace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/110?cb=20090418231902" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Ron%27sNecklace.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20090418231902" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Ron%27sNecklace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/110?cb=20090418231902" decoding="async" width="110" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron&#39;sNecklace.jpg" data-image-key="Ron&#39;sNecklace.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/81/Ron%27sNecklace.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/110?cb=20090418231902" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron%27sNecklace.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron's Christmas present from <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Prefect_badge" title="Prefect badge">Prefect badge</a></b>: Just like all of his brothers except the twins, Ron became a Prefect during his fifth year, and received his badge in the summer of 1995.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><i><b><a href="/wiki/The_Adventures_of_Martin_Miggs,_the_Mad_Muggle" title="The Adventures of Martin Miggs, the Mad Muggle">The Adventures of Martin Miggs, the Mad Muggle</a></b></i>: In his youth, Ron was an avid reader of this comic, and he kept a large stack of issues in his bedroom.<sup id="cite_ref-COS3_51-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-COS3-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Chudley Cannons' posters</b>: Ron was a supporter of the Chudley Cannons and he put posters of the team everywhere in his bedroom.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Spello-tape" class="mw-redirect" title="Spello-tape">Spello-tape</a></b>: Ron used Spellotape to hold together his first wand after nearly breaking it in half at the start of his second year, but it malfunctioned dreadfully after this, backfiring spells, making strange noises and emitting objects from the wrong end. He borrowed the tape from <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/The-Deluminator.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20180514155044" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="The-Deluminator.jpeg" data-image-key="The-Deluminator.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/The-Deluminator.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180514155044" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/The-Deluminator.jpeg/revision/latest?cb=20180514155044" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/The-Deluminator.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180514155044" decoding="async" width="180" height="75" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="The-Deluminator.jpeg" data-image-key="The-Deluminator.jpeg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/0/0c/The-Deluminator.jpeg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20180514155044" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:The-Deluminator.jpeg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron with the Deluminator in Malfoy Manor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li><b><a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a></b>: Ron inherited the Deluminator from Dumbledore's <a href="/wiki/The_Last_Will_and_Testament_of_Albus_Percival_Wulfric_Brian_Dumbledore" title="The Last Will and Testament of Albus Percival Wulfric Brian Dumbledore">will</a>, which helped him during his Horcrux mission to "illuminate the darkness".<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_watch" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s watch">Watch</a></b>: He received a golden wristwatch on his 17th birthday from his parents.</li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Chocolate_Frog_Card" title="Chocolate Frog Card">Chocolate Frog Cards</a></b>: Ron had about five hundred chocolate frog cards in 1991, including six cards of Morgana and probably at least one of Albus Dumbledore, but none of Agrippa nor Ptolemy.<sup id="cite_ref-PS6_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS6-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> Supposedly, in his adulthood, he owned his own card, which he was extremely proud of.<sup id="cite_ref-CFC_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CFC-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Wizard's Chess Set</b>: Ron had a battered old <a href="/wiki/Wizard%27s_Chess" title="Wizard&#39;s Chess">Wizard's Chess</a> set in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>. Like most other things he had, it was secondhand, being passed down to him by his grandfather — it was left unsaid whether it was Septimus Weasley's or his Prewett grandfather's. However, his chessmen were therefore more likely to trust his judgement in battle.<sup id="cite_ref-PS12_45-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS12-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley%27s_car" title="Ronald Weasley&#39;s car">Car</a> (supposedly)</b>: Ron mentioned having parked this car near King's Cross on September 1st, 2017, when he carried his family to the <a href="/wiki/Platform_Nine_and_Three-Quarters" title="Platform Nine and Three-Quarters">Platform Nine and Three-Quarters</a>. It is however left unclear if the car was Ron's or Hermione's. He said that the <a href="/wiki/Supersensory_Charm" title="Supersensory Charm">Supersensory Charm</a> could be used for parking, so he probably charmed the car with that.<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_41-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li><b>Muggle driving licence</b>: On September 1st, 2017, Ron mentioned having obtained the Muggle driving licence, even if Hermione, according to him, didn't believe that he could pass the exam without <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confunding</a> the examiner. (As a matter of fact, however, Ron admitted <i>having</i> Confunded the examiner, because he forgot to look in the wing mirror).<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_41-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=58" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Relationships">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=58" title="Edit section: Relationships"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Family">Family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=59" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=59" title="Edit section: Family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Weasley_family">Weasley family</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=60" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Weasley family">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=60" title="Edit section: Weasley family"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Ah! Another Weasley... I know just what to do with you... GRYFFINDOR!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;The Sorting Hat putting Ron into Gryffindor, like the rest of his family<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="142" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20200417054614" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest?cb=20200417054614" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20200417054614" decoding="async" width="245" height="142" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Weasley family.png" data-image-key="Weasley_family.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/9f/Weasley_family.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20200417054614" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Weasley_family.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Weasley family</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was quite close with his <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">family</a>. Although he was sometimes embarrassed by their lack of money, Ron was fiercely protective of his siblings, and always stoutly defended his parents. He was outraged when his brother <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy</a> called their <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">father</a> a failure and greatly upset their <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">mother</a> with his estrangement, as Ron was close to both of his parents.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ron looked up to his older brothers <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Charles_Weasley" title="Charles Weasley">Charlie</a>, though their accomplishments also made him feel insecure about what he had to live up to.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Percy tried to be a role model for Ron, but Ron considered him rather pompous and annoying, and took after <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> more in terms of personality. Notably, Ron was the only family member Percy contacted after his estrangement from his family,<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> and the one who comforted him over Fred's death during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> The twins delighted in teasing Ron, as did his younger sister <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a>, though they were all close. Ron was very protective of Ginny, particularly in disapproving of her love life, which sometimes led to them fighting.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Other relatives of Ron were <a href="/wiki/Fabian_Prewett" title="Fabian Prewett">Fabian</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gideon_Prewett" title="Gideon Prewett">Gideon Prewett</a>, who were his uncles and members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. During the <a href="/wiki/First_Wizarding_War" title="First Wizarding War">First Wizarding War</a>, the brothers were attacked by five <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>, including <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>. Both were killed in battle and were described as having "<i>fought like heroes</i>."
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron's family was extended when four of his siblings were married and had children. He also had two children with <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo</a> Weasley.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Harry_Potter">Harry Potter</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=61" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Harry Potter">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=61" title="Edit section: Harry Potter"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>If you want to kill Harry, you'll have to kill us too!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's loyalty to Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140603201724" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140603201724" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140603201724" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry Potter.jpg" data-image-key="Harry_Potter.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/97/Harry_Potter.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140603201724" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_Potter.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, his best friend and future brother-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Harry Potter had been Ron's best friend since <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>. The two were as close as brothers, as the Weasleys became like a surrogate family to Harry soon after the pair met on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> at the start of their first year. They took to each other immediately, bonding over the vast array of wizarding sweets Harry happily shared with Ron, who was not able to afford his own from the Hogwarts Express <a href="/wiki/Trolley_witch" title="Trolley witch">food trolley</a>. When <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> spoke disparagingly of Ron's family, Harry rejected Draco's offer of friendship in favour of Ron's. Both Ron and Harry were <a href="/wiki/Sorting_ceremony" title="Sorting ceremony">Sorted</a> into Gryffindor and therefore shared a dormitory. Ron defended Harry from fellow classmates and even Professor Snape.
</p><p>Like all real brothers, Harry and Ron occasionally fought, especially when Ron's insecurities got the best of him. When Harry was chosen by the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> as Champion for the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, Ron believed Harry had indeed cheated to get into the contest. The two briefly fell out, but the friendship was repaired after the Tournament's First Task, when Ron realised that Harry could possibly lose his life to an event he had genuinely not wanted to enter.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140405164157" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="110" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry and Ron hugging.gif" data-image-key="Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140405164157" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140405164157" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140405164157" decoding="async" width="245" height="110" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry and Ron hugging.gif" data-image-key="Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1b/Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140405164157" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry_and_Ron_hugging.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Harry and Ron reunite before the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The two had another falling out in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, when the negative energy in <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> affected Ron to the point of making him resentful of Harry and unreasonably jealous of Harry's relationship with <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, their other best friend and Ron's love interest. Ron temporarily abandoned his friends, though he instantly regretted it, and returned to save Harry's life.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> By and large, Ron was always fiercely loyal to Harry and risked life and limb on countless occasions for him. Even in 2020, Ron tried to prevent Harry from being transfigured into Voldemort due he didn't want Harry to be affected by his trauma. The two eventually became brothers-in-law when Harry married <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ron's sister</a>. Ron was the uncle of Harry's three children, and was godfather to Harry and Ginny's son <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James</a>. Since the two became Aurors, it is likely that they worked together later in life.
</p>
