<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hermione_Granger">Hermione Granger</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=62" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=62" title="Edit section: Hermione Granger"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;MuggleNet">"<i>Oh, maybe she and Ron will be alright with a bit of counselling, you know. I wonder what happens at wizard marriage counselling? They'll probably be fine. He needs to work on his self-esteem issues and she needs to work on being a little less critical.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> on Hermione and Ron's adult relationship<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/MuggleNet" title="MuggleNet">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521112839" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione Granger 2.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521112839" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521112839" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521112839" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione Granger 2.jpg" data-image-key="Hermione_Granger_2.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/5e/Hermione_Granger_2.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521112839" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_Granger_2.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, his future wife and mother of his children</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry%2C_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190109134358" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="225" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Trio in their younger days Harry, Ron and Hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry,_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry%2C_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190109134358" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry%2C_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190109134358" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry%2C_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190109134358" decoding="async" width="180" height="225" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Trio in their younger days Harry, Ron and Hermione.jpg" data-image-key="Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry,_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/ac/Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry%2C_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20190109134358" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Trio_in_their_younger_days_Harry,_Ron_and_Hermione.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron, Scabbers, Harry and Hermione together in their first year</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron's relationship with Hermione was rocky, but by and large, the two were good friends for most of their adolescence, with building romantic tension that culminated in a kiss during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. From the time Ron first met Hermione on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> at the start of their first year, he found her annoying for "<i>showing off</i>" and regularly reciting the school's rules. His first thought was that he didn't want to be in her house and he groaned when she was Sorted into Gryffindor. Later on, he informed others of his annoyance with her, and mentioned that it was unsurprising that she didn't have any friends, which she overheard. Hurt, Hermione hid in the bathroom, crying, until Harry and Ron saved her from a troll that had been let into Hogwarts by <a href="/wiki/Quirinus_Quirrell" title="Quirinus Quirrell">Professor Quirrell</a>. Following the troll incident, Hermione lied to <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Professor McGonagall</a> to prevent Harry and Ron from getting into trouble.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> From that time onwards, the trio were best friends, in spite of Ron and Hermione's tendency to bicker.
</p><p>Ron first began showing signs of romantic interest in Hermione in their <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">second year</a>; he was irritated by her crush on <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor <a href="/wiki/Gilderoy_Lockhart" title="Gilderoy Lockhart">Gilderoy Lockhart</a>, became so angry that <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a> called her a "<a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a>" that he tried to hex him, and was even more upset than Harry when she became one of the victims of the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_basilisk" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s basilisk">basilisk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> In their third year, Ron and Hermione had their first real fight, when Ron accused Hermione's cat <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a> of eating his pet rat <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Scabbers</a>, which had gone missing.
</p><p>The two stopped speaking to each other for a time, but made up after <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a> scolded Ron and Harry for their treatment of Hermione; Ron offered to help her with <a href="/wiki/Buckbeak" title="Buckbeak">Buckbeak</a>'s trial, and Hermione hugged him. Also in their third year during their <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> class when Professor Lupin was "<a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">ill</a>" and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Professor Snape</a> was teaching instead, Ron was the only person that had enough courage to go as far as standing up to Snape when he called Hermione an "<i>insufferable know-it-all</i>".<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In their fourth year, Ron and Hermione's romantic feelings for one another began to grow and become more obvious. Hermione was jealous of Ron's crush on <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Part-Veela" class="mw-redirect" title="Part-Veela">part-Veela</a> champion from <a href="/wiki/Beauxbatons_Academy_of_Magic" title="Beauxbatons Academy of Magic">Beauxbatons</a>, and Ron became jealous of <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, with whom Hermione attended the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> after Ron failed to ask her in time and then offended her with his clumsy attempt to do so. Though they rowed heatedly over Hermione seeing Krum, their friendship only suffered slight strain.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> Hermione's frustration over Ron's failure to realise and act on his feelings continued into their fifth year, as she commented that he had "<i>the emotional range of a teaspoon</i>". Ron was visibly affected when Hermione kissed him on the cheek before his first <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> game and irked that Hermione maintained a correspondence with Viktor Krum.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140611234353" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron kissing in the Chamber of Secrets.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140611234353" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140611234353" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140611234353" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hermione and Ron kissing in the Chamber of Secrets.gif" data-image-key="Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/32/Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140611234353" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hermione_and_Ron_kissing_in_the_Chamber_of_Secrets.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione kiss in the Chamber of Secrets</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Their sixth year would be a trying time for Ron and Hermione. When Hermione and Harry were invited to the <a href="/wiki/Slug_Club" title="Slug Club">Slug Club</a>, while <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a> ignored Ron, Ron became resentful and jealous. He brightened up considerably after Hermione asked him to go to Slughorn's Christmas party with her. However, Ron had a row with <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">his sister</a> after catching her snogging <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, during which she revealed that Hermione had snogged <a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a> sometime during their fourth year. Ron started acting coldly towards Hermione, much to her bewilderment. 
</p><p>In an attempt to boost Ron's confidence for an upcoming Quidditch match, Harry pretended to slip him some <a href="/wiki/Felix_Felicis" title="Felix Felicis">Felix Felicis</a> in Ron's morning pumpkin juice, giving Ron the desired placebo effect that kept his nerves from hindering his performance as a <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a>. Harry had managed to trick Hermione into thinking he had given Ron a drop of the Felix Felicis as well, and she berated both Harry and Ron for taking an unfair advantage in the game. Though Ron had initially believed the Felix was behind his flawless performance, when Harry revealed he had not actually slipped anything in Ron's drink, Ron accused Hermione of not having faith in his abilities and thenceforth started ignoring her completely.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110416015544" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="DH1 Ron and Hermione picking up stones.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110416015544" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110416015544" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110416015544" decoding="async" width="250" height="167" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="DH1 Ron and Hermione picking up stones.jpg" data-image-key="DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/3/39/DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110416015544" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:DH1_Ron_and_Hermione_picking_up_stones.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron teaching Hermione how to skip rocks</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>All this caused Ron to begin a shallow relationship with <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>. Hermione was hurt and furious, <a href="/wiki/Bird-Conjuring_Charm" title="Bird-Conjuring Charm">conjuring a flock of canaries</a> to attack Ron, after which the two did not speak for months. Hermione even retaliated by attending the aforementioned Christmas party with <a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a>, an older <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> whom Ron despised, simply to annoy Ron. By this time, Ron was already growing tired of his relationship with the very clingy Lavender. 
</p><p>When Ron was accidentally poisoned with mead on his birthday, Hermione forgot her anger in her worry for him, staying by his side until he recovered. Ron looked forward to these visits from her while pretending to be asleep whenever Lavender visited him. By the time Ron was allowed to leave the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a>, he and Hermione were closer than ever, and the former's romance with Lavender ended quickly when Lavender saw Ron and Hermione coming down from the boys' dormitories together, while Harry was with them under his <a href="/wiki/Cloak_of_Invisibility" title="Cloak of Invisibility">Invisibility Cloak</a>. At the end of the year, their mutual affection was visible when Ron gently comforted Hermione as she cried on his shoulder at Dumbledore's funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Afterwards, the two grew much closer, though were only "<i>sort of</i>" together, according to Harry. They danced together at <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_William_Weasley_and_Fleur_Delacour" title="Wedding of William Weasley and Fleur Delacour">wedding</a>, where Ron also showed his continuing jealous dislike of Viktor Krum, who was a guest. During the hunt for the <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a> with Harry, Ron comforted Hermione several times by putting his arm around her, and the two were generally kinder to one another; Harry even suspected that they had fallen asleep in <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> holding hands after waking up and noticing that their hands were barely an inch away from each other.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140503020828" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron and Hermione sleeping.gif" data-image-key="Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140503020828" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140503020828" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140503020828" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron and Hermione sleeping.gif" data-image-key="Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/46/Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140503020828" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_and_Hermione_sleeping.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Hermione fell asleep hand-in-hand in <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Remus Lupin informed them of the Ministry's crack down on Muggle-borns, Ron offered to vouch for her by telling people that Hermione was his cousin, at which Hermione affectionately touched his hand and reminded him that they were on the run with the most wanted wizard in Britain. When Ron temporarily left his friends, Hermione cried over him for weeks; Ron was able to return by hearing Hermione's voice saying his name through his <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a>. When Ron destroyed the <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">locket Horcrux</a>, it taunted him with visions of his greatest fears, one of which was Hermione preferring Harry to him. Hermione was initially furious with Ron for his abandonment, to the point of physically attacking him, though she eventually forgave him.
</p><p>Later on, when the trio was brought to <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a> isolated Hermione for interrogation by the means of torture. Ron begged in vain to be taken in her stead, and after being thrown into the basement, Hermione's screams from above caused Ron to call her name in anguish, eventually reducing him to tears. During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Hermione was touched when Ron expressed concern for the castle's <a href="/wiki/House-elf" title="House-elf">house-elves</a>, for whom she had always been concerned, and initiated a kiss, to which Ron responded very enthusiastically.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime after the end of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron and Hermione married and had two children, <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DHE_41-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DHE-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>They were rather young when they married, as noted by Ron in 2020. His nephew, Albus, noted that Ron was rather openly affectionate towards his wife and was known to kiss her in public rather frequently. At this time Ron proposed to Hermione again after reading about renewing wedding vows, showing that Ron had become rather romantic as he matured, which made Hermione melt, deeply touched by her husband's romantic gesture and agreeing on the spot to it. This shows hows Ron and Hermione's relationship had evolved and much of their bickering subsiding a bit for a more gentle marriage, yet still rife with their uniquely combative and verbally alarming undertones to it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Children">Children</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=63" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Children">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Children"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>Don't get too friendly with him, though, Rosie. Granddad Weasley would never forgive you if you married a pure-blood</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron joking with his daughter <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> about Scorpius Malfoy<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter-hugo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160712034020" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="293" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Harry-potter-hugo.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-hugo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter-hugo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160712034020" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter-hugo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160712034020" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter-hugo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160712034020" decoding="async" width="180" height="293" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Harry-potter-hugo.jpg" data-image-key="Harry-potter-hugo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/63/Harry-potter-hugo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160712034020" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Harry-potter-hugo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Hugo_Granger-Weasley" title="Hugo Granger-Weasley">Hugo Weasley</a>, his second child and son</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the Second Wizarding War, Ron and Hermione had two children, Rose and Hugo. As Rose was preparing to leave for her first year at Hogwarts in 2017, Ron jokingly told her that if she wasn't in <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> he'd disinherit her. He also told her to beat <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>'s son <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius Malfoy</a> on their tests, and that he was grateful she had inherited her <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">mother</a>'s brains.
</p><p>Ron's daughter Rose was close in age to Harry and Ginny's younger son <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus Severus</a>, while Ron's son Hugo was close in age to Harry and Ginny's daughter, <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily Luna</a> and they all appeared quite close.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Nieces_and_nephews">Nieces and nephews</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=64" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nieces and nephews">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=64" title="Edit section: Nieces and nephews"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>You interrupted them? You are </i>so<i> like Ron —</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;<a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> to her son <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_II" title="James Potter II">James Sirius</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron had many nieces and nephews through his siblings. Bill and Fleur had three children: <a href="/wiki/Victoire_Weasley" title="Victoire Weasley">Victoire</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dominique_Weasley" title="Dominique Weasley">Dominique</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Louis_Weasley" title="Louis Weasley">Louis</a>. Percy and his wife, <a href="/wiki/Audrey_Weasley" title="Audrey Weasley">Audrey,</a> had two daughters, <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley_II" title="Molly Weasley II">Molly</a> (after <a href="/wiki/Molly_Weasley" title="Molly Weasley">Ron's mother</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Lucy_Weasley" title="Lucy Weasley">Lucy</a>. George and <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina</a> had two children, a son named <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley_II" title="Fred Weasley II">Fred</a> (after Ron's <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">older brother</a>) and a daughter named <a href="/wiki/Roxanne_Weasley" title="Roxanne Weasley">Roxanne</a>. Ginny also married <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> and had three children, James (to whom Ron was godfather), <a href="/wiki/Albus_Potter" title="Albus Potter">Albus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Lily_L._Potter" title="Lily L. Potter">Lily</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fleur_Delacour">Fleur Delacour</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=65" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Fleur Delacour">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=65" title="Edit section: Fleur Delacour"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire"><b>Ron</b>: "<i>There she was, just walking by... you know how I like it when they walk... I couldn't help it... it just sort of slipped out!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny Weasley</b>: "<i>Actually, he sort of screamed at her. It was a bit frightening.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron's humiliating attempt to ask Fleur to the Yule Ball<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222230" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Fleur Delacour.jpg" data-image-key="Fleur_Delacour.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222230" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222230" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222230" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Fleur Delacour.jpg" data-image-key="Fleur_Delacour.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/1e/Fleur_Delacour.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222230" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Fleur_Delacour.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, his sister-in-law</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Fleur Delacour was a very beautiful, <a href="/wiki/France" title="France">French</a>, <a href="/wiki/Half-Veela" title="Half-Veela">part-Veela</a> <a href="/wiki/Wizardkind" title="Wizardkind">witch</a>. Ron developed a crush on her when he met her in 1994, during the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>. He asked her to go with him to the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a>, but she refused. However, after the the second task in the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Tournament</a>, when Harry "saved" Fleur's younger sister, <a href="/wiki/Gabrielle_Delacour" title="Gabrielle Delacour">Gabrielle</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Great_Lake" title="Great Lake">Black Lake</a>, Fleur treated both Harry and Ron (whom she believed helped Harry save Gabrielle) much more warmly. Following the death of <a href="/wiki/Cedric_Diggory" title="Cedric Diggory">Cedric Diggory</a> and the end of the Tournament, Fleur kissed Ron and Harry and said goodbye to them before she left. After the Tournament, Fleur started dating Ron's brother, <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a>. Bill sent her to live with his family for a few days, so that she could become more familiar with them. Ron told Harry that it was difficult to get used to her visiting when she kept appearing suddenly, leaving Ron in a sort-of trance.
</p><p>Fleur eventually married Bill, and they lived at their own house, <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>. While Ron was looking for <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, he abandoned Harry and Hermione temporarily after they fought and spent that time at Shell Cottage with Bill and Fleur. Ron went to Shell Cottage again, after the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>, and Fleur cared for him and his friends like a mother.
</p><p>Eventually, Ron and Fleur fought alongside each other and survived the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Neville_Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=66" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Neville Longbottom"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>No, you're not. <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">You</a> just said that to get rid of Neville.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron to Hermione Granger regarding Neville's invite to the Yule Ball<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220929" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville HBP 1996.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_HBP_1996.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220929" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141122220929" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220929" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville HBP 1996.jpg" data-image-key="Neville_HBP_1996.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/4/4e/Neville_HBP_1996.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20141122220929" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville_HBP_1996.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, a good friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Neville Longbottom became Ron's room mate in their first year at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. Neville was shy and nervous, and regularly found himself being bullied by <a href="/wiki/Slytherin" title="Slytherin">Slytherin</a> students, like <a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>. Ron encouraged Neville to be more confident and to stand up for himself, and the two became close friends. Both Ron and Neville became members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a> in 1995, and fought together in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> in 1996, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>.
</p><p>Ron was shocked when he learned that Neville's parents were patients at <a href="/wiki/St_Mungo%27s_Hospital_for_Magical_Maladies_and_Injuries" title="St Mungo&#39;s Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries">St Mungo's Hospital for Magical Maladies and Injuries</a>, having been tortured to the point of insanity by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rodolphus_Lestrange" title="Rodolphus Lestrange">Rodolphus</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Rabastan_Lestrange" title="Rabastan Lestrange">Rabastan Lestrange</a>, and sympathised with his friend.
</p><p>While Ron, Harry and Hermione left Hogwarts to find Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, Neville led <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a> and several other students in reviving Dumbledore's Army and maintaining a steady opposition against the new Headmaster <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> and professors <a href="/wiki/Amycus_Carrow" title="Amycus Carrow">Amycus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Alecto_Carrow" title="Alecto Carrow">Alecto Carrow</a>. Neville was adamant that the rest of the DA be included in whatever Ron, Harry and Hermione were doing to bring down <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, and he fought together with them in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, ultimately beheading Nagini with the <a href="/wiki/Sword_of_Gryffindor" title="Sword of Gryffindor">Sword of Gryffindor</a> and destroying the last remaining Horcrux. Together, Ron and Neville took down <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>.
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron and Neville remained close and saw each other regularly, as Neville was appointed <a href="/wiki/Herbology" title="Herbology">Herbology</a> professor at Hogwarts, and taught <a href="/wiki/Rose_Weasley" class="mw-redirect" title="Rose Weasley">Ron's daughter</a> in 2017.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Draco_Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=67" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Draco Malfoy"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Think my name’s funny, do you? No need to ask who </i>you<i> are. My father told me all the Weasleys have red hair, freckles, and more children than they can afford.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Draco Malfoy upon first meeting Ron<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200347" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="274" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy (HBP promo).jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200347" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140623200347" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200347" decoding="async" width="180" height="274" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Draco Malfoy (HBP promo).jpg" data-image-key="Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/84/Draco_Malfoy_%28HBP_promo%29.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140623200347" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Draco_Malfoy_(HBP_promo).jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Draco_Malfoy" title="Draco Malfoy">Draco Malfoy</a>, his school bully</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron and <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">his family</a> were looked down upon by the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_family" title="Malfoy family">Malfoy family</a> for their lack of wealth and “<a href="/wiki/Blood_traitor" title="Blood traitor">blood traitor</a>” status. Upon meeting Ron on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a> at the beginning of their first year, Draco Malfoy immediately expressed his disdain for the Weasleys. He was further irritated when Harry turned down his offer of friendship in favour of Ron’s.<sup id="cite_ref-PS_11-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PS-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Like their fathers, <a href="/wiki/Arthur_Weasley" title="Arthur Weasley">Arthur Weasley</a> and <a href="/wiki/Lucius_Malfoy" title="Lucius Malfoy">Lucius Malfoy</a>, Ron and Draco despised each other and frequently exchanged insults.
</p><p>In their second year, Ron tried to hex Draco to vomit slugs after he called Hermione a “<i>filthy little <a href="/wiki/Mudblood" title="Mudblood">Mudblood</a></i>”, but the charm backfired due to a broken wand. He also attempted to physically attack him after Draco expressed a wish that Hermione was killed rather than <a href="/wiki/Petrification" title="Petrification">petrified</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> affair.<sup id="cite_ref-CS_31-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CS-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> In their fourth year, Ron was immensely amused when <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor Moody</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a> in disguise) <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration" title="Transfiguration">transfigured</a> Draco into a ferret. The following year, Draco invented the song <i><a href="/wiki/Weasley_is_Our_King" title="Weasley is Our King">Weasley is Our King</a></i> to demean Ron’s abilities as a <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> After he, Harry, and Hermione saved Draco and <a href="/wiki/Gregory_Goyle" title="Gregory Goyle">Gregory Goyle</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Room_of_Requirement" title="Room of Requirement">Room of Requirement</a>, Ron <a href="/wiki/Muggle_duelling" title="Muggle duelling">punched</a> Draco in the face and called him a “<i>two-faced bastard</i>” upon seeing him with a <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>.
</p><p>By <a href="/wiki/2017" title="2017">2017</a>, Ron and his friends' enmity with Draco had faded, though none of them were near friends. Ron discouraged his daughter <a href="/wiki/Rose_Granger-Weasley" title="Rose Granger-Weasley">Rose</a> from becoming "too friendly" with Draco’s son <a href="/wiki/Scorpius_Malfoy" title="Scorpius Malfoy">Scorpius</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> In 2020, it is shown Ron is slightly annoyed with Draco becoming friendly with Harry, and even cited that despite this he still disliked him. Nevertheless, he admitted that he felt sorry for Draco for the loss of Astoria, showing that despite their mutual enmity, even Ron in the end was not entirely without empathy for him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Luna_Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=68" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Luna Lovegood"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>You know, she's grown on me, Luna. I know she's insane, but it's in a good way.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron regarding Luna during his sixth year<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100925141354" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Luna HPHBP.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_HPHBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100925141354" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20100925141354" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100925141354" decoding="async" width="180" height="251" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Luna HPHBP.jpg" data-image-key="Luna_HPHBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/ca/Luna_HPHBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20100925141354" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Luna_HPHBP.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, a good friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron met Luna Lovegood in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a> on the <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_Express" title="Hogwarts Express">Hogwarts Express</a>, and found her very odd. She found him very funny, but Ron suspected she was making fun of him when she laughed uproariously at a joke he made. After getting to know her better through <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, Ron gradually became fonder of Luna, especially after she was one of the only D.A. members to come to the trio’s assistance when they ventured to the <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry of Magic</a> and <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">a battle</a> ensued, during which Luna protected a <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">cursed</a> Ron and his injured <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">sister</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-OOTP_7-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-OOTP-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>Ron was very amused when Luna commentated on a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match the <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">following year</a>, and when she danced by herself at the wedding of his older brother <a href="/wiki/William_Weasley" title="William Weasley">Bill</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>. He thought highly of her bravery, but still teased her on occasion, regardless the two remained close friends in their adulthood.<sup id="cite_ref-DH_9-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DH-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Seamus_Finnigan_and_Dean_Thomas">Seamus Finnigan and Dean Thomas</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=69" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Seamus Finnigan and Dean Thomas">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Seamus Finnigan and Dean Thomas"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Seamus Finnigan</b>: "<i>Do you believe the rubbish he's come out with about <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">You-Know-Who</a>?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Yeah, I do.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron sticking up for <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> against his friend, Seamus<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Neville%2C_Dean%2C_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150316172335" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Neville, Dean, and Seamus-ootp.jpg" data-image-key="Neville,_Dean,_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Neville%2C_Dean%2C_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150316172335" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Neville%2C_Dean%2C_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150316172335" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Neville%2C_Dean%2C_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150316172335" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Neville, Dean, and Seamus-ootp.jpg" data-image-key="Neville,_Dean,_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c2/Neville%2C_Dean%2C_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150316172335" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Neville,_Dean,_and_Seamus-ootp.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>: his friends and roommates</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In addition to Harry and Neville, Ron’s room mates at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> were Dean Thomas and Seamus Finnigan. Although he was not as close to them as he was to Harry, Ron was nevertheless friendly with both of them. When he and Harry had a falling out over the <a href="/wiki/Goblet_of_Fire" title="Goblet of Fire">Goblet of Fire</a> drawing Harry’s name, Ron spent a lot of time with Seamus and Dean.<sup id="cite_ref-GOF_30-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-GOF-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Ron stood up for Harry against Seamus when he and Harry argued about <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s return. Also, when Dean began dating his <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">younger sister</a> in <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Ron became irritated with him, especially after catching the two snogging,<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> though they seemed to have put the matter behind them completely by the time Ron, Harry and Hermione met Dean again in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>.
</p><p>Seamus and Dean were also members of <a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>. Dean, like Ron, Harry and Hermione, left Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, because it was supposed that he was a <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-born</a>. He was caught by a group of <a href="/wiki/Snatchers" title="Snatchers">Snatchers</a>, led by <a href="/wiki/Fenrir_Greyback" title="Fenrir Greyback">Fenrir Greyback</a>, along with Ron, Harry and Hermione. They escaped from <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>, where they had gone, and lived for a few days at <a href="/wiki/Shell_Cottage" title="Shell Cottage">Shell Cottage</a>.
</p><p>Seamus and Dean eventually fought along with Ron in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p>
<h3><span id="Scabbers/Peter_Pettigrew"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Scabbers.2FPeter_Pettigrew">Scabbers/Peter Pettigrew</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=70" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Scabbers/Peter Pettigrew">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Scabbers/Peter Pettigrew"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">"<i>I let you sleep in my bed!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron disgusted at Peter Pettigrew<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602041920" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="267" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Wormtail DH1.jpg" data-image-key="Wormtail_DH1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140602041920" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" decoding="async" width="180" height="267" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Wormtail DH1.jpg" data-image-key="Wormtail_DH1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/7f/Wormtail_DH1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140602041920" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Wormtail_DH1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, his once pet</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Scabbers was an unusually old and scraggly-looking rat that originally belonged to <a href="/wiki/Percy_Weasley" title="Percy Weasley">Percy Weasley</a>, but was passed down to Ron when Percy was given <a href="/wiki/Hermes" title="Hermes">Hermes</a>. At first, Ron showed little outward affection for Scabbers, as the rat was uninteresting and one of Ron's many hand-me-downs. However, Ron later demonstrated that he genuinely cared for the rat; he was so devastated when Scabbers disappeared during the 1993–1994 school year that he nearly ended his friendship with <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, believing her cat, <a href="/wiki/Crookshanks" title="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</a>, had eaten Scabbers. Ron was clearly overjoyed when they later discovered Scabbers hiding in Rubeus Hagrid's cabin. When <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a> and <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> revealed that Scabbers was actually an <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> named Peter Pettigrew, Ron refused to believe it until they forced the rat to transform back into his human form. Ron took this revelation as a personal insult, and refused to listen to Pettigrew's pleas for mercy.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Ron, Harry, and Hermione were captured and imprisoned in the cellar of <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a>. When the house-elf <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> came to rescue them, Peter was sent to investigate the noise. Harry and Ron ambushed Pettigrew, and Ron took his wand. Harry reminded Pettigrew of the life-debt he owed Harry when Pettigrew tried to strangle him, and Peter momentarily loosened his grip. However, the <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_silver_hand" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s silver hand">silver hand</a> given to Peter by Voldemort turned on him instead, and, despite Harry and Ron's attempts to save him, Pettigrew was killed for showing the slightest bit of mercy. Ron subsequently gained possession of <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s wand">Pettigrew's wand</a>. This could be seen as poetic justice for Pettigrew, who had deceived Ron for so long.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Rubeus_Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=71" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=71" title="Edit section: Rubeus Hagrid"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Look, Hagrid is our friend, so why don't we just go and ask him?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>That will be a cheerful visit. "Hello Hagrid. Tell us, have you sent anything mad and hairy loose in the castle lately?"</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> on whether to ask Hagrid about the monster in the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160121163026" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160121163026" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160121163026" decoding="async" width="180" height="247" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rubeus Hagrid.jpg" data-image-key="Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/cd/Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20160121163026" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rubeus_Hagrid.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, his teacher and friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron first met Rubeus Hagrid, the <a href="/wiki/Keeper_of_Keys_and_Grounds" title="Keeper of Keys and Grounds">gamekeeper</a> for <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, during his first year at the school in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>. Hagrid was very fond of Harry, Ron and Hermione, regularly inviting them to his hut for tea. Though all three returned Hagrid's affections, Ron was openly incredulous of Hagrid's <a href="/wiki/Love" title="Love">love</a> of dangerous <a href="/wiki/Creature" title="Creature">Creatures</a>, and was furious with Hagrid after his pet <a href="/wiki/Acromantula" title="Acromantula">Acromantula</a>, <a href="/wiki/Aragog" title="Aragog">Aragog</a>, and Aragog's family tried to eat him and Harry. During Ron's fourth year, it was revealed to the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a> that Hagrid was a <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giant</a>, and Hagrid consequently received a good deal of hate mail, which led to his self-imposed seclusion within his hut. Through the efforts of Ron, Harry, Hermione and <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, Hagrid became convinced that people still loved him and wanted him around.
</p><p>Ron and Hagrid also fought alongside one another in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> and in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. After the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron and Hagrid probably remained friends.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Remus_Lupin">Remus Lupin</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=72" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Remus Lupin">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=72" title="Edit section: Remus Lupin"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Harry! How could you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>You shouldn't have said that stuff to Lupin.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Hermione and Ron after Harry yells at Remus for leaving his wife<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119235913" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Remus Lupin Deathly Hallows promo image.jpg" data-image-key="Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e2/Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119235913" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Remus_Lupin_Deathly_Hallows_promo_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, his former DADA professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was among the students who were very impressed by <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>'s teaching when he was professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>, during Ron's third year at Hogwarts. Though Ron was initially afraid when he learned Lupin was a <a href="/wiki/Werewolf" title="Werewolf">werewolf</a>, he quickly realised that being a werewolf didn't change who Lupin was in human form, and the issue never came between them. In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, when Harry fought with Remus for attempting to temporarily leave his pregnant <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">wife</a> to aid Harry, Ron, and Hermione in their mission, Ron expressed his disappointment in the way Harry handled the situation, despite agreeing with the point Harry was trying to make.
</p><p>Ron and Lupin fought alongside each other in the: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_the_Burrow" title="Attack at the Burrow">Attack at the Burrow</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, where Remus was murdered by <a href="/wiki/Antonin_Dolohov" title="Antonin Dolohov">Antonin Dolohov</a>. After Remus was murdered in the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron remained close with Remus's son <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy Lupin</a>, who was also <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>'s godson.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sirius_Black">Sirius Black</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=73" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Sirius Black">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=73" title="Edit section: Sirius Black"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>But they'll catch Black, won't they? I mean, everyone's looking for him.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Sure. Except no one's ever broken out of Azkaban before... and he's a murderous raving lunatic.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron about Sirius Black after he escaped from prison<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20200420034321" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sirius Black Profile.JPG" data-image-key="Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200420034321" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG/revision/latest?cb=20200420034321" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200420034321" decoding="async" width="180" height="266" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sirius Black Profile.JPG" data-image-key="Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/f4/Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200420034321" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sirius_Black_Profile.JPG" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, his best friend's godfather</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>Ron first learned about Sirius Black in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, when the latter became the first wizard to escape from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>, and was believed to be planning to track down and kill Harry at Hogwarts. As it turned out, Sirius was actually after Ron's pet rat, who was actually the <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a> in disguise. At the end of their third year, Ron, Harry and Hermione learned that Sirius was not only innocent of the crime of betraying <a href="/wiki/Lily_J._Potter" title="Lily J. Potter">Lily</a> and <a href="/wiki/James_Potter_I" title="James Potter I">James Potter</a> to <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, but that he was, in fact, Harry's godfather. After revealing Pettigrew's true form, Sirius felt responsible for Ron's loss of "<i>Scabbers</i>," and gave him an owl as replacement. During their fourth year Ron along with Harry and Hermione provided food for Sirius, who was hiding in a cave outside of Hogsmeade.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>, Ron and Sirius bonded during their time cooped up at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>, and Ron defended Sirius against all of Hermione's critical remarks about Sirius's selfish treatment of Harry as a friend rather than a godson, as well as her belief that Sirius was trying to live vicariously through Harry, Ron, and herself.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Minerva_McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=74" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=74" title="Edit section: Minerva McGonagall"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)"><b>Ron</b>: "<i>[McGonagall Transforms] That was bloody brilliant!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Minerva McGonagall</b>: "<i>Thank you for that assessment, Mr Weasley. Perhaps it would be more useful if I were to transfigure Mr Potter and yourself into a pocket watch. That way, one of you might be on time.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron and Professor McGonagall in Transfiguration class<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521115100" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Minerva McGonagall POAF promo.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140521115100" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" decoding="async" width="180" height="253" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Minerva McGonagall POAF promo.jpg" data-image-key="Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/f/fe/Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140521115100" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Minerva_McGonagall_POAF_promo.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, his head of house and professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Minerva McGonagall was the <a href="/wiki/Transfiguration_(class)" title="Transfiguration (class)">Transfiguration</a> Professor and <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> <a href="/wiki/Head_of_House" title="Head of House">Head of House</a> during Ron's time at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>. She was very strict, and regularly reprimanded Ron, Harry and Hermione for the many instances they ended up bending or outright breaking school rules. However, she was just and impartial as a disciplinarian, and always acted in the best interest of all Hogwarts students, often showing lenience and understanding where it was deserved. She clearly cared about Ron, as she cared about all of her students, and Ron fought alongside McGonagall during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, both surviving the <a href="/wiki/Second_Wizarding_War" title="Second Wizarding War">Second Wizarding War</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Nymphadora_Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=75" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Nymphadora Tonks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=75" title="Edit section: Nymphadora Tonks"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Listen, no bloke in his right mind's going to fancy Tonks when Fleur's around. I mean, Tonks is okay-looking when she isn't doing stupid things to her hair and her nose, but </i>[...]<i> </i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ginny Weasley</b>: "<i>She's a damn sight nicer than <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Phlegm</a>!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron and <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> comparing Tonks and Fleur<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
