<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222048" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161119222048" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222048" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nymphadora Tonks DH promo headshot .jpg" data-image-key="Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/c/c8/Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161119222048" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nymphadora_Tonks_DH_promo_headshot_.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, his friend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Nymphadora Tonks was a young witch, a <a href="/wiki/Metamorphmagus" title="Metamorphmagus">metamorphmagus</a>, and an <a href="/wiki/Auror" title="Auror">Auror</a>. Ron met Tonks in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, when both became members of the <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a>. Ron generally liked Tonks and found her amusing, despite at one point comparing her looks unfavourably to Fleur Delacour's. Saying that she was merely okay looking "<i>when not doing stupid stuff to her nose and hair</i>". He also mentioned that she was not as much of laugh anymore as she was starting to "<i>look more and more like <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Moaning Myrtle</a></i>".
</p><p>Tonks and Ron fought alongside each other during the: <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>, <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a> (where they were paired together), the <a href="/wiki/Attack_at_the_Burrow" title="Attack at the Burrow">Attack at the Burrow</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, where Tonks was murdered by <a href="/wiki/Bellatrix_Lestrange" title="Bellatrix Lestrange">Bellatrix Lestrange</a>. Ron was devastated by her death and after the war, he became a friend of Tonks's son, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Lupin" title="Edward Lupin">Teddy</a>. It can also be assumed that he was around Teddy often, seeing as his best friend was Teddy's godfather.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Severus_Snape">Severus Snape</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=76" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Severus Snape">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=76" title="Edit section: Severus Snape"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>How many times have you suspected Snape, and when have you ever been right? Dumbledore trusts him, he works for the Order, that ought to be enough.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>He used to be a Death Eater. And we've never seen proof that he really swapped sides.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron's mistrust towards Snape<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20081103135333" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Severus Snape Profile.jpg" data-image-key="Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/8b/Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20081103135333" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Severus_Snape_Profile.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a>, his professor</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Severus Snape was the <a href="/wiki/Potions_Master" title="Potions Master">Potions Master</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_Slytherin_House" title="Head of Slytherin House">Head of Slytherin House</a> during Ron's time at Hogwarts. He made no attempt to hide his preference for his own House, nor his disdain for the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students, and showed particular dislike for both Ron and Hermione as Harry's best friends. Ron believed that Snape, who was a former Death Eater, had never truly joined their side, and that he was still working as a double agent for Voldemort. During his fifth year, Ron suggested that Snape was trying to open Harry's mind to Voldemort rather than close it during Harry's <a href="/wiki/Occlumency" title="Occlumency">Occlumency</a> lessons.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, Ron fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Astronomy_Tower" title="Battle of the Astronomy Tower">Battle of the Astronomy Tower</a>, after which he learned that Snape had killed <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, and a few months later, during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, Snape accidentally cursed off George Weasley's ear, while aiming a <i><a href="/wiki/Sectumsempra" title="Sectumsempra">Sectumsempra</a></i> at a Death Eater who was poised to kill <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>. Ron, like most of the Order and Hogwarts staff, viewed Snape as a cowardly, heartless murderer. However, Ron witnessed Snape's <a href="/wiki/Death" title="Death">death</a> as ordered by <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a> during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, and eventually learned that Snape had been working for their side all along, at great personal risk. It was likely that Ron came to appreciate Snape's unwavering bravery.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Albus_Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=77" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=77" title="Edit section: Albus Dumbledore"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">"<i>Yeah, Dumbledore's off his rocker all right!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron's own unique compliment of Dumbledore<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091122115606" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="280" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore HBP.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091122115606" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20091122115606" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091122115606" decoding="async" width="180" height="280" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Albus Dumbledore HBP.jpg" data-image-key="Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/8/87/Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20091122115606" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Albus_Dumbledore_HBP.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>, his headmaster</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was raised within the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding world</a>, and knew of Albus Dumbledore, <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a> headmaster and probably the greatest wizard of the time, since childhood. Ron met Dumbledore when he first attended Hogwarts in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>. Although Ron never spent much, if any, one-on-one time with Dumbledore, it was clear that Dumbledore trusted Ron, along with Hermione, and valued their individual skills. He felt Ron and Hermione could be trusted to aid Harry in his mission to destroy Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>, the existence of which was a secret of vital importance unknown to a living a soul aside from the trio, Dumbledore, and Voldemort himself.
</p><p>After Dumbledore's death, it was discovered that the Headmaster had bequeathed Ron his <a href="/wiki/Deluminator" title="Deluminator">Deluminator</a>. Unknown to Ron at the time he received it, the Deluminator had the magical ability to return Ron to his friends if the time came, as Dumbledore had anticipated, when Ron would part ways with Harry and Hermione during their quest. The Deluminator's function as a homing device for Ron's friends suggested that Dumbledore understood Ron well enough to know that as surely as he would struggle with the mission, he would be just as certain to want to return to his friends' sides.
</p><p>In return, Ron admired Dumbledore for his extraordinary magical prowess and intelligence greatly and felt a great amount of respect for him. During Dumbledore's funeral, Ron was clearly distraught as Dumbledore's body was laid to rest. This respect clearly became greater than ever when Ron realised that Dumbledore valued him as Harry's friend enough to give him the Deluminator, showing great appreciation and gratitude for the Headmaster's trust in him. Due to his pragmatism, he is entirely unaffected by the revelation of Dumbledore's past with Gellert Grindelwald whereas even Hermione could not help but be deeply shocked by it, believing it only happened because Dumbledore was still growing up at that age and defending him from Harry when he mentioned about it.
</p><p>Ron, along with Hermione and Harry, visited <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore%27s_portrait" title="Albus Dumbledore&#39;s portrait">Dumbledore's portrait</a> after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> to discuss the fate of the <a href="/wiki/Deathly_Hallows" title="Deathly Hallows">Deathly Hallows</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lavender_Brown">Lavender Brown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=78" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lavender Brown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=78" title="Edit section: Lavender Brown"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince"><b>Ron</b>: "<i>I love you, Hermione.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Don't let Lavender hear you saying that.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>I won't. Or maybe I will...then she'll ditch me...</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron and Hermione discussing Ron's relationship with Lavender<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140220045014" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lavender Brown 1997.jpg" data-image-key="Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140220045014" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20140220045014" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140220045014" decoding="async" width="180" height="240" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lavender Brown 1997.jpg" data-image-key="Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e8/Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20140220045014" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lavender_Brown_1997.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, his ex-girlfriend</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Lavender Brown, a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> in Ron's year, developed a crush on him when they entered their <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">sixth year</a>. At first, Ron seemed vaguely flattered, but not particularly interested in Lavender's flirtatious behaviour. However, after becoming angry with Hermione and being taunted by Ginny over his lack of romantic experience, Ron began an exhibitionist relationship with Lavender. The couple was frequently seen snogging in public, much to the disgust of a jealous and hurt Hermione as well as Ginny, who considered him a "<i>filthy hypocrite</i>" because he insulted her for being caught kissing <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">her boyfriend</a> earlier in the year. Lavender threw herself into the relationship almost obsessively, alarming even her best friend, <a href="/wiki/Parvati_Patil" title="Parvati Patil">Parvati Patil</a>. Lavender called Ron by the annoying nickname of "Won-Won", pressed Harry for details of Ron's feelings for her, and gave him a necklace with the words 'my sweetheart' for <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a>. After that Christmas, Lavender tickled Ron, and was noticed by Harry. Ron found these traits irritating, and admitted to Harry that the relationship consisted of little talking and mostly snogging.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 247px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140307032955" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron and Lavender embrace.gif" data-image-key="Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140307032955" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif/revision/latest?cb=20140307032955" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140307032955" decoding="async" width="245" height="150" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron and Lavender embrace.gif" data-image-key="Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/ea/Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/245?cb=20140307032955" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron_and_Lavender_embrace.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron and Lavender kissing or "snogging"</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure> 
<p>By <a href="/wiki/1_March" title="1 March">his birthday</a>, Ron was unhappy in the relationship; he feigned sleep whenever Lavender visited him in the infirmary after his poisoning and said Hermione's name in his sleep. He was spared the task of breaking up with Lavender when she became suspicious that something was going on between him and Hermione, and ended the romance. Ron was happy to see things finished, though he felt guilty for it, but Lavender was upset for some time afterwards. It is unknown how Ron reacted to Lavender's death in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>. It can assumed that he was saddened by it, as they were once friends.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Viktor_Krum">Viktor Krum</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=79" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Viktor Krum">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=79" title="Edit section: Viktor Krum"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>Hasn't he asked you to call him Vicky yet?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron jealously mocking <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a>'s relationship with Viktor Krum<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 175px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141103135847" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="173" height="243" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-image-key="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/173?cb=20141103135847" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20141103135847" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/173?cb=20141103135847" decoding="async" width="173" height="243" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-image-key="Goffilm39.1.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/a/aa/Goffilm39.1.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/173?cb=20141103135847" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Goffilm39.1.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Viktor_Krum" title="Viktor Krum">Viktor Krum</a>, his rival</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron was a huge fan of Viktor Krum, as he was the <a href="/wiki/Seeker" title="Seeker">Seeker</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Bulgarian_National_Quidditch_team" title="Bulgarian National Quidditch team">Bulgarian National Quidditch team</a>, enthusiastic to the point of purchasing a miniature Krum figurine at the <a href="/wiki/Quidditch_World_Cup" title="Quidditch World Cup">Quidditch World Cup</a> and bringing it with him to school. However, his feelings changed markedly when Krum began seeing <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a> and the two attended the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> together in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>. Despite his jealousy, Ron asked Krum for his autograph following the end of the <a href="/wiki/Triwizard_Tournament" title="Triwizard Tournament">Triwizard Tournament</a>, much to Krum's surprise and Hermione's amusement. During Ron's sixth year, he discovered that Hermione had "snogged" Krum in the course of their brief romance, which caused Ron's jealousy of Krum to resurge. He expressed these feelings in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, at Bill and Fleur's wedding, when Krum's appearance as a guest inspired Ron to whisk Hermione away to dance.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pigwidgeon">Pigwidgeon</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=80" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Pigwidgeon">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=80" title="Edit section: Pigwidgeon"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">"<i>I've got to keep him up here because he annoys Errol and Hermes. He annoys me too, come to that.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron regarding his pet owl<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<p>Pigwidgeon became Ron's owl in <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>. He was given to Ron by <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, as Sirius felt partially responsible for the loss of Ron's pet rat, who turned out to be the <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a> and <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eater</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, in disguise. Initially, Ron loved him, and enjoyed having an owl of his own, but Pig, as Ron preferred to call him, turned out to be very tiny and hyperactive, and became mainly annoying to Ron (as <a href="/wiki/Errol" title="Errol">Errol</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hermes" title="Hermes">Hermes</a>, according to Ron) and had to be kept away from them. It can be assumed that deep down Ron still loved Pigwidgeon considering that before he found out the truth about Peter Pettigrew he still loved "Scabbers" despite complaining about his uselessness nonstop.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crookshanks">Crookshanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=81" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Crookshanks">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=81" title="Edit section: Crookshanks"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>OY! GET OFF, YOU STUPID ANIMAL!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Ron, don’t hurt him!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>CATCH THAT CAT! Look at him! He’s skin and bone! You keep that cat away from him!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Crookshanks doesn’t understand it’s wrong! All cats chase rats, Ron!</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>There’s something funny about that animal! It heard me say that Scabbers was in my bag!</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron's inital dislike of Hermione's cat<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/CrookshanksPottermore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161211062436" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="157" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="CrookshanksPottermore.png" data-image-key="CrookshanksPottermore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/CrookshanksPottermore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161211062436" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/CrookshanksPottermore.png/revision/latest?cb=20161211062436" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/CrookshanksPottermore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161211062436" decoding="async" width="180" height="157" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="CrookshanksPottermore.png" data-image-key="CrookshanksPottermore.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/71/CrookshanksPottermore.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20161211062436" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:CrookshanksPottermore.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Crookshanks</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Crookshanks was <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>'s large, bandy-legged, ginger-coloured, half-<a href="/wiki/Kneazle" title="Kneazle">Kneazle</a> <a href="/wiki/Cat" title="Cat">cat</a>. Ron strongly disliked him at first, largely due to his antagonistic behaviour towards Ron's pet rat, Scabbers. In <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>, Scabbers, who was actually the <a href="/wiki/Animagus" title="Animagus">Animagus</a>, <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew" title="Peter Pettigrew">Peter Pettigrew</a>, faked his own death for the second time after Sirius Black escaped from <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. Ron initially believed Scabbers had been eaten by Crookshanks, and he nearly ended his friendship with Hermione.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Ron discovered the truth about Scabbers, and found that Crookshanks had been helping Sirius all along, he seemed to appreciate Crookshanks as a good judge of character, and even half-jokingly asked the cat if <a href="/wiki/Pigwidgeon" title="Pigwidgeon">Pigwidgeon</a> was really an owl.<sup id="cite_ref-POA_6-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-POA-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> When Crookshanks meowed happily, Ron actually seemed relieved. It is unknown if Ron ever saw Crookshanks after the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, since he had been left at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> during Bill and Fleur's wedding.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Cormac_McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=82" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Cormac McLaggen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=82" title="Edit section: Cormac McLaggen"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">"<i>Well, good luck. Hope you hammer McLag — I mean, <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Smith</a>.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> before a <a href="/wiki/Quidditch" title="Quidditch">Quidditch</a> match<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110224235356" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="292" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Mclaggen.jpg" data-image-key="Mclaggen.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110224235356" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110224235356" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110224235356" decoding="async" width="180" height="292" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Mclaggen.jpg" data-image-key="Mclaggen.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/1/11/Mclaggen.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20110224235356" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Mclaggen.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Cormac_McLaggen" title="Cormac McLaggen">Cormac McLaggen</a>, his rival</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1996" title="1996">1996</a>, Ron's competition for the <a href="/wiki/Keeper" title="Keeper">Keeper</a> position on the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a> was Cormac McLaggen, a <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> a year above him. Before the try-outs, Hermione overheard McLaggen insulting Ron and Ginny, and placed a <a href="/wiki/Confundus_Charm" title="Confundus Charm">Confundus Charm</a> on him that made him miss his last save. Ron thus beat him, though McLaggen claimed that this was due to favouritism. Ron greatly disliked him, which prompted Hermione to attend <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Professor Slughorn</a>’s Christmas party with him to retaliate against Ron for his romance with <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>. Ron disliked McLaggen even more, and was happy when his date with Hermione did not go well, and when McLaggen did not perform well as replacement keeper while Ron was in the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dolores_Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=83" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dolores Umbridge">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=83" title="Edit section: Dolores Umbridge"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>She’s an awful woman, awful. You know, I was just saying to Ron when you came in . . . we’ve got to do something about her.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>I suggested <a href="/wiki/Poison" title="Poison">poison</a>.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>No . . . I mean, something about what a dreadful teacher she is, and how we’re not going to learn any defence from her at all.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Ron Weasley</b>: "<i>Well, what can we do about that? ’S too late, isn’t it? She got the job, she’s here to stay, Fudge’ll make sure of that.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron's hatred of Umbridge<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="238" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20101127041001" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" decoding="async" width="180" height="238" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dolores Umbridge Deathly Hallows promotional image.jpg" data-image-key="Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/68/Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20101127041001" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dolores_Umbridge_Deathly_Hallows_promotional_image.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, his former DADA professor and enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Dolores Umbridge, a <a href="/wiki/British_Ministry_of_Magic" title="British Ministry of Magic">Ministry</a> employee, was appointed <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a> professor. She was a sadistic, very unpleasant woman who derived great satisfaction from torturing students as punishment (most notably, forcing <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a> to carve the words "<i>I must not tell lies</i>" into the back of his own hand, using a <a href="/wiki/Black_Quill" title="Black Quill">Blood Quill</a>). Ron, like most of the students and faculty at <a href="/wiki/Hogwarts_School_of_Witchcraft_and_Wizardry" title="Hogwarts School of Witchcraft and Wizardry">Hogwarts</a>, greatly disliked her intrusive, hypocritical and often outright insulting ways, in return Umbridge disliked Ron, as he was a main offender of the rules and loyal to Harry and a member of Dumbledore's Army. She had an obsession with pure-blood status and both hated and feared people she called <i><a href="/wiki/Half-breed" title="Half-breed">half-breeds</a></i>, like <a href="/wiki/Centaur" title="Centaur">centaurs</a> and <a href="/wiki/Half-giant" title="Half-giant">half-giants</a>. She also hated <a href="/wiki/Muggle-born" title="Muggle-born">Muggle-borns</a>, and probably half-bloods, despite being half-blood herself. In the end of the year, she was attacked by a group of centaurs and eventually brought to the <a href="/wiki/Hospital_Wing" title="Hospital Wing">Hospital Wing</a> by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. Though she attempted to abscond, <a href="/wiki/Peeves" title="Peeves">Peeves</a> the <a href="/wiki/Poltergeist" title="Poltergeist">Poltergeist</a> discovered her sneaking away, and led the students in driving her out Hogwarts.
</p><p>Ron met again Umbridge in <a href="/wiki/1997" title="1997">1997</a>, when he was disguised as <a href="/wiki/Reginald_Cattermole" title="Reginald Cattermole">Reg Cattermole</a>, a Ministry official, and while Umbridge was in charge of trying Muggle-borns before they were sent to <a href="/wiki/Azkaban" title="Azkaban">Azkaban</a>. Harry stunned Umbridge during the interrogation of <a href="/wiki/Mary_Cattermole" title="Mary Cattermole">Mary Cattermole</a>, when Umbridge attempted to flaunt <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> as proof of her relation to the <a href="/wiki/Selwyn_family" title="Selwyn family">Selwyn family</a>. After Hermione retrieved the locket and replaced it with a decoy using the <a href="/wiki/Doubling_Charm" title="Doubling Charm">Geminio</a> curse, Harry, Ron, and Hermione proceeded to help the Muggle-borns awaiting trial escape from the Ministry. After the Second Wizarding War, Umbridge herself was imprisoned in Azkaban for life.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Ghosts">Ghosts</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=84" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Ghosts">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=84" title="Edit section: Ghosts"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets"><b>Moaning Myrtle</b>: "<i>Here I am, minding my own business, and someone thinks it's funny to throw a book at me.</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>But, it can't hurt if someone throws something at you. I mean, it would just go right through you.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; An example of Ron's unintentional insensitivity to <a href="/wiki/Ghost" title="Ghost">ghosts</a><sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png/revision/latest?cb=20200515191831" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington.png" data-image-key="Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200515191831" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png/revision/latest?cb=20200515191831" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200515191831" decoding="async" width="180" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington.png" data-image-key="Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/6/6d/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200515191831" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Nicholas_de_Mimsy-Porpington" title="Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington">Nicholas de Mimsy-Porpington</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Ron's lack of sensitivity causes him to be unpopular with the Hogwarts ghosts, namely Nearly Headless Nick and <a href="/wiki/Myrtle_Warren" title="Myrtle Warren">Moaning Myrtle</a>. Ron first met Nearly Headless Nick in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a> during his first welcoming feast. He knew Nick because he heard <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a> talking about him. Nick requested that Ron should address him as "<i>Sir Nicholas</i>" instead of Nearly Headless Nick. During later feasts, Ron would annoy Nick by reminding him he was dead and how much he enjoyed food.
</p><p>Ron met Moaning Myrtle in <a href="/wiki/1992" title="1992">1992</a>, during the re-opening of the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a>. Myrtle was upset since <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny</a> had unknowingly thrown <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle%27s_Diary" class="mw-redirect" title="Tom Riddle&#39;s Diary">a diary</a> at her. Ron pointed out that it couldn't hurt Myrtle since she was a ghost, and the book would go through her. Myrtle swooped down on Ron with rage and sarcastically commented that everyone should throw books at her and make a game out of it.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Lord_Voldemort">Lord Voldemort</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=85" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=85" title="Edit section: Lord Voldemort"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">"<i>He beat you!</i>"</span></dd>
<dd>&#8212;Ron to Voldemort (talking about <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>) during the Battle of Hogwarts<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">[src]</a></sup></dd>
<dd></dd></dl></div>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 182px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150829033655" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="180" height="223" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Lord Voldemort.jpg" data-image-key="Lord_Voldemort.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829033655" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20150829033655" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829033655" decoding="async" width="180" height="223" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Lord Voldemort.jpg" data-image-key="Lord_Voldemort.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/7/78/Lord_Voldemort.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20150829033655" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Lord_Voldemort.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>, a hated enemy</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Ron was raised within the <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">wizarding world</a>, he had grown up fearing the name of Lord Voldemort, the most dangerous <a href="/wiki/Dark_Wizard" title="Dark Wizard">Dark Wizard</a> of all time. He was afraid to say the name or even to hear it, and protested when Harry refused to refer to Voldemort as "You-Know-Who" or "He-Who-Must-Not-Be-Named." Ron helped Harry protect the <a href="/wiki/Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Philosopher's Stone</a> from Voldemort at the end of their first year, when he won a game of Wizard's chess by sacrificing himself. Ron also helped Harry get into the <a href="/wiki/Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Chamber of Secrets">Chamber of Secrets</a> and save Ron's <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">younger sister</a>.
</p><p>Ron's fear of saying Voldemort's name ended up being justified and delaying the capture of Harry, Hermione and himself, as he managed to convince Harry and Hermione to refer to Voldemort as "You-Know-Who" around the same time saying the name was made <a href="/wiki/Taboo" title="Taboo">Taboo</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, Ron used Godric Gryffindor's sword to destroy <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a>, one of Voldemort's <a href="/wiki/Horcrux" title="Horcrux">Horcruxes</a>. The locket tortured Ron, as a "Riddle-Harry" and a "Riddle-Hermione" appeared, eventually kissing, telling Ron that he was useless, that no woman would choose him over Harry, that his own mother will choose Harry as a son instead of him, and that she wanted a girl when she had him. Ron showed the strength of his personality in by overcoming his insecurities and stabbing the locket with <a href="/wiki/Godric_Gryffindor%27s_Sword" class="mw-redirect" title="Godric Gryffindor&#39;s Sword">Godric Gryffindor's Sword</a>, destroying the Horcrux.
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>, Ron was present when Voldemort told the crowd that Harry had been killed while trying to save himself. Forgetting his fear, and breaking the <a href="/wiki/Silencing_Charm" title="Silencing Charm">Silencing Charm</a> Voldemort had placed over the crowd, Ron shouted that Harry had defeated him. Ron also witnessed Voldemort's final duel with Harry.
</p>
<h3><span id="Dumbledore's_Army"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Dumbledore.27s_Army">Dumbledore's Army</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=86" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=86" title="Edit section: Dumbledore&#039;s Army"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Neville Longbottom</b>: "<i>Dumbledore's Army's supposed to be about doing something real. Or was all that just words to you?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Maybe you don't have to do this all by yourself, mate.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron, along with Neville, shows his loyalty to the Army, and to Harry<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div><figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161123060553" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" decoding="async" width="250" height="166" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Dumbledore&#39;s Army.jpg" data-image-key="Dumbledore&#39;s_Army.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/9/96/Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161123060553" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Dumbledore%27s_Army.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><a href="/wiki/Dumbledore%27s_Army" title="Dumbledore&#39;s Army">Dumbledore's Army</a>, his friends and allies</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Dumbledore's Army was an organisation led by Harry Potter, in order to oppose <a href="/wiki/Dolores_Umbridge" title="Dolores Umbridge">Dolores Umbridge</a>, and as a supplementary means of practising <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">defensive magic</a>. In <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>, Ron and Hermione convinced Harry to teach anyone who was interested about protective spells and counter-jinxes that had helped him survive his many encounters with Voldemort, as the purely theoretical instruction they were receiving from Umbridge was wholly inadequate. Six members of the D.A. fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a>. In addition to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ginevra_Weasley" title="Ginevra Weasley">Ginny Weasley</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fred_Weasley" title="Fred Weasley">Fred</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_Weasley" title="George Weasley">George</a>, <a href="/wiki/Neville_Longbottom" title="Neville Longbottom">Neville Longbottom</a>, <a href="/wiki/Luna_Lovegood" title="Luna Lovegood">Luna Lovegood</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lavender_Brown" title="Lavender Brown">Lavender Brown</a>, <a href="/wiki/Seamus_Finnigan" title="Seamus Finnigan">Seamus Finnigan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Dean_Thomas" title="Dean Thomas">Dean Thomas</a>, there were eighteen other known members.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> students who were members of the DA included <a href="/wiki/Colin_and_Dennis_Creevey" title="Colin and Dennis Creevey">Colin and Dennis Creevey</a>, <a href="/wiki/Parvati_Patil" title="Parvati Patil">Parvati Patil</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lee_Jordan" title="Lee Jordan">Lee Jordan</a> (Fred and George Weasley's best friend) <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Spinnet" title="Alicia Spinnet">Alicia Spinnet</a> and <a href="/wiki/Katie_Bell" title="Katie Bell">Katie Bell</a> (members of the <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor_Quidditch_team" title="Gryffindor Quidditch team">Gryffindor Quidditch team</a>) and <a href="/wiki/Angelina_Johnson" title="Angelina Johnson">Angelina Johnson</a> (captain of the Team, and Ron's future sister-in-law, after marrying George). Fred and Colin Creevey were both murdered by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a> in during the Battle.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Hufflepuff" title="Hufflepuff">Hufflepuff</a> students were <a href="/wiki/Hannah_Abbott" title="Hannah Abbott">Hannah Abbott</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ernest_Macmillan" title="Ernest Macmillan">Ernie Macmillan</a>, <a href="/wiki/Susan_Bones" title="Susan Bones">Susan Bones</a>, <a href="/wiki/Justin_Finch-Fletchley" title="Justin Finch-Fletchley">Justin Finch-Fletchley</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Zacharias_Smith" title="Zacharias Smith">Zacharias Smith</a>. Ron was friendly with all of them, except Zacharias, the only one who didn't fight in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a>.
</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Ravenclaw" title="Ravenclaw">Ravenclaw</a> students were <a href="/wiki/Padma_Patil" title="Padma Patil">Padma Patil</a> (Parvati's twin sister), <a href="/wiki/Cho_Chang" title="Cho Chang">Cho Chang</a>, <a href="/wiki/Terry_Boot" title="Terry Boot">Terry Boot</a>, <a href="/wiki/Anthony_Goldstein" title="Anthony Goldstein">Anthony Goldstein</a>, <a href="/wiki/Michael_Corner" title="Michael Corner">Michael Corner</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Marietta_Edgecombe" title="Marietta Edgecombe">Marietta Edgecombe</a>. Ron attended the <a href="/wiki/Yule_Ball" title="Yule Ball">Yule Ball</a> with Padma, who wasn't pleased with Ron's appearance in his tattered dress robes, and Ron wasn't particularly fond of Michael Corner, who was Ginny's ex-boyfriend. They all fought together during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> in <a href="/wiki/1998" title="1998">1998</a>, with the exception of Marietta, who did not return to Hogwarts at any point.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Order_of_the_Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=87" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=87" title="Edit section: Order of the Phoenix"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="quote">
<dl><dd><span title="Source:&#160;Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix"><b>Harry Potter</b>: "<i>So what is this place?</i>"</span></dd>
<dd><b>Ron</b>: "<i>Headquarters.</i>"</dd>
<dd><b>Hermione Granger</b>: "<i>Of the Order of the Phoenix. It's a secret society. Dumbledore formed it back when they first fought You-Know-Who.</i>"</dd>
<dd>&#8212; Ron and <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione</a> explaining to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry</a> the Order<sup class="noprint"><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">[src]</a></sup></dd></dl>
</div>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 252px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest?cb=20140511035621" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" decoding="async" width="250" height="105" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Order of the Phoenix.png" data-image-key="Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/5/58/Order_of_the_Phoenix.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140511035621" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Order_of_the_Phoenix.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The original <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Order of the Phoenix">Order of the Phoenix</a></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The Order of the Phoenix was an organisation founded and led by <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>. The Order included Ron's <a href="/wiki/Weasley_family" title="Weasley family">family</a>, <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hermione_Granger" title="Hermione Granger">Hermione Granger</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Rubeus Hagrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sirius_Black" title="Sirius Black">Sirius Black</a>, <a href="/wiki/Fleur_Delacour" title="Fleur Delacour">Fleur Delacour</a>, <a href="/wiki/Minerva_McGonagall" title="Minerva McGonagall">Minerva McGonagall</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nymphadora_Tonks" title="Nymphadora Tonks">Nymphadora Tonks</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Severus_Snape" title="Severus Snape">Severus Snape</a> as well as several other notable members of the <a href="/wiki/Wizarding_world" title="Wizarding world">wizarding community</a>.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/1994" title="1994">1994</a>, for Ron's fourth year at Hogwarts, <a href="/wiki/Alastor_Moody" title="Alastor Moody">Alastor "Mad Eye" Moody</a>, an Auror famous for his great skill, vast experience, and growing paranoia, was appointed professor of <a href="/wiki/Defence_Against_the_Dark_Arts" title="Defence Against the Dark Arts">Defence Against the Dark Arts</a>. Prior to the start of the school year, on <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Lord Voldemort</a>'s orders, Moody was attacked and imprisoned in his own magical trunk by <a href="/wiki/Bartemius_Crouch_Junior" title="Bartemius Crouch Junior">Barty Crouch Jnr</a>, who impersonated Moody and took his place at Hogwarts by using <a href="/wiki/Polyjuice_Potion" title="Polyjuice Potion">Polyjuice Potion</a> until 24 June, <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. Ron clearly held Moody in high regard, as he looked forward to his classes and persistently hoped that Moody would tell him he would make a good Auror, as he had Harry and Hermione (albeit, it was actually Barty Crouch Jnr who suggested Harry and Hermione consider becoming Aurors). Ron met the real Mad-Eye later in 1995, at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a>, the headquarters of the Order. Ron and Moody fought alongside one another in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Department_of_Mysteries" title="Battle of the Department of Mysteries">Battle of the Department of Mysteries</a> and in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_the_Seven_Potters" title="Battle of the Seven Potters">Battle of the Seven Potters</a>, where Mad-Eye was killed. Ron, like the other members of the Order, was shocked and devastated by the death of someone as tough and skilled as Moody.
</p><p>Ron was also familiar with the "<i>useless git</i>" <a href="/wiki/Mundungus_Fletcher" title="Mundungus Fletcher">Mundungus Fletcher</a>, an almost grudging member of the Order. Though Ron was initially amused by Mundungus, he quickly grew disgusted with Mundungus's continued general disregard for other people, or their property and safety, particularly when he abandoned Alastor Moody in the midst of the Battle of the Seven Potters. Ron met Mundungus again when he, Harry and Hermione wanted information regarding the whereabouts of <a href="/wiki/Salazar_Slytherin%27s_Locket" class="mw-redirect" title="Salazar Slytherin&#39;s Locket">Salazar Slytherin's Locket</a> and appeared amused by Kreacher's repeated abuse of Fletcher.
</p><p>When Ron, Harry and Hermione apparated into <a href="/wiki/Hogsmeade" title="Hogsmeade">Hogsmeade</a>, intent on sneaking into Hogwarts to find an object that had once belonged to Rowena Ravenclaw, they found themselves in a trap set by <a href="/wiki/Death_Eaters" title="Death Eaters">Death Eaters</a>. They were saved by <a href="/wiki/Aberforth_Dumbledore" title="Aberforth Dumbledore">Aberforth Dumbledore</a>, <a href="/wiki/Albus_Dumbledore" title="Albus Dumbledore">Albus Dumbledore</a>'s younger brother, and owner of the <a href="/wiki/Hog%27s_Head" class="mw-redirect" title="Hog&#39;s Head">Hog's Head</a>. They discovered that they had been saved by him once before; it was Aberforth who had sent <a href="/wiki/Dobby" title="Dobby">Dobby</a> to rescue them from the <a href="/wiki/Malfoy_Manor" title="Malfoy Manor">Malfoy Manor</a> after Harry saw his eye in the remaining shard of Sirius's <a href="/wiki/Two-way_mirror" title="Two-way mirror">two-way mirror</a>. They were later also informed by Neville that Aberforth had been supporting Neville and the other DA members remaining at Hogwarts by feeding them, passing messages using enchanted coins, and generally backing them in their resistance against Severus Snape and the <a href="/wiki/Carrow_family" title="Carrow family">Carrows</a>.
</p><p>Other Order members Ron encountered were <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Shacklebolt" title="Kingsley Shacklebolt">Kingsley Shacklebolt</a>, a skilled Auror who would later go on to become <a href="/wiki/Minister_for_Magic" title="Minister for Magic">Minister for Magic</a> and who was greatly admired by Ron, Harry, Hermione, and the Weasleys; <a href="/wiki/Elphias_Doge" title="Elphias Doge">Elphias Doge</a>, Albus Dumbledore's friend; as well as <a href="/wiki/Dedalus_Diggle" title="Dedalus Diggle">Dedalus Diggle</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hestia_Jones" title="Hestia Jones">Hestia Jones</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sturgis_Podmore" title="Sturgis Podmore">Sturgis Podmore</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Emmeline_Vance" title="Emmeline Vance">Emmeline Vance</a>. Emmeline Vance was killed by Death Eaters in 1996, and Podmore was imprisoned because he attempted to get into the Department of Mysteries, under the <a href="/wiki/Imperius_Curse" title="Imperius Curse">Imperius Curse</a>, the news of which shocked and horrified Ron.
</p><p>It is likely that every surviving member of the Order (except <a href="/wiki/Arabella_Figg" title="Arabella Figg">Arabella Figg</a>, who was a Squib and unable to fight, but might have helped in another way) fought in the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Hogwarts" title="Battle of Hogwarts">Battle of Hogwarts</a> alongside Ron, Harry, and Hermione.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=88" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Etymology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=88" title="Edit section: Etymology"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ronald" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ronald">Ronald</a></i> is the Scottish form of the Scandinavian name <i>Ragnvald</i>, which was derived from the Old Norse <i>Ragnvaldr</i>, composed of the elements <i>ragn</i>, "advice", and <i>valdr</i>, "ruler".<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> It is a cognate of the name <i><a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reginald" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Reginald">Reginald</a></i>, which is derived from the Germanic form of the name, <i>Raginwald</i>, meaning "the prince's counsellor". All these names carry the meaning of a person who acts as a trusted advisor to a person in power, much as Ron acted as a friend and confidant to <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter" title="Harry Potter">Harry Potter</a>.
</p><p>In keeping with the pattern of Weasley family members taking names from Arthurian legend, "Ron" is the name of Arthur's lance in Geoffrey of Monmouth's <i>History of the Kings of Britain</i>. Ron is short for <i>Rhongomyniad</i>, which means "striker spear" in Welsh.
</p><p><i>Bilius</i> comes from the word "<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/bile" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:bile">bile</a>", as one of the <a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Humourism" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Humourism">four humours</a> discussed by Ancient Greek philosophers. Yellow bile was connected to the element of fire, which is the element of <a href="/wiki/Gryffindor" title="Gryffindor">Gryffindor</a> house, and someone with an excess of it was believed to be bad-tempered, as Ron is. The English adjective <i>"bilious"</i> also applies to those who have an irritable temper.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Behind_the_scenes">Behind the scenes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=89" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=89" title="Edit section: Behind the scenes"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
