<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 152px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110909103658" class="image"><img alt="" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" width="150" height="248" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Ron-lego y 5-7.jpg" data-image-key="Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110909103658" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110909103658" class="image"><img alt="" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110909103658" decoding="async" width="150" height="248" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Ron-lego y 5-7.jpg" data-image-key="Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/harrypotter/images/e/e7/Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20110909103658" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Ron-lego_y_5-7.jpg" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Ron Weasley in <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_5-7" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 5-7</a></i></p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Ron was the second friend Harry ever made, after Hagrid.</li>
<li>Ron's favourite sandwich type is <a href="/wiki/Bacon_sandwich" title="Bacon sandwich">bacon</a> and his least favourite is corned beef.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wikipedia:Citing sources"><i><span title="The material in the vicinity of this tag needs references to reliable sources." style="white-space: nowrap;">citation needed</span></i></a>&#93;</sup></li>
<li>Ron's least favourite colour is maroon as he said when he received his Christmas jumper from his mother. Ironically, both he and all his family have red hair, the colour that maroon is related to.<sup class="noprint">&#91;<a href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Wikipedia:Citing sources"><i><span title="The material in the vicinity of this tag needs references to reliable sources." style="white-space: nowrap;">citation needed</span></i></a>&#93;</sup></li>
<li>Ron is related to Draco Malfoy distantly; his paternal grandmother was a Black, who are related to the Malfoys through Narcissa's marriage to Lucius, Draco's father. They are third cousins, however it is unknown if they know of this.</li>
<li>Ron is portrayed by <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">British</a> actor <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Grint" title="Rupert Grint">Rupert Grint</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_(film_series)" title="Harry Potter (film series)">film adaptations</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">Goblet of Fire</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince (film)">Half-Blood Prince</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Part 2</a></i> and is one of the 14 characters to appear in all 8 film adaptations; by British actor <a href="/wiki/Paul_Thornley" title="Paul Thornley">Paul Thornley</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child_(play)#Original_West_End_production" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child (play)">original West End production</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Cursed_Child" title="Harry Potter and the Cursed Child">Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-cast1_55-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cast1-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>Rupert Grint does not have a long nose, as Ron is described as having in the novels, but he does have freckles - make-up covers them and they aren't on his face, causing some fans to claim he has no freckles at all. He also has green eyes, in contrast to Ron's blue eyes. Ironically, co-star <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Radcliffe" title="Daniel Radcliffe">Daniel Radcliffe</a> has blue eyes in contrast to his character's green eyes. Unlike Ron, Rupert is not particularly tall, nor does he have large hands or feet. Although, like Ron, Rupert is the tallest of the three actors however.</li>
<li>Just like Ron Weasley, Rupert Grint comes from a large family, has red hair, and suffers from arachnophobia. Although Weasley's accent origin is not divulged, Rupert speak in a combination of modern Received Pronunciation and Cockney accents.</li>
<li>Rupert Grint says his favourite scene is the Yule Ball scene in the fourth film, the same as his co-star <a href="/wiki/Emma_Watson" title="Emma Watson">Emma Watson</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Jamie_Waylett" title="Jamie Waylett">Jamie Waylett</a> plays Ron when he is disguised as <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Crabbe" title="Vincent Crabbe">Vincent Crabbe</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (film)">Chamber of Secrets</a></i>, as do <a href="/wiki/Steffan_Rhodri" title="Steffan Rhodri">Steffan Rhodri</a> when he is disguised as <a href="/wiki/Reginald_Cattermole" title="Reginald Cattermole">Reginald Cattermole</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> (with no voice change) and Rupert Grint (himself) when he is disguised as "Dragomir Despard" in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>. <a href="/wiki/Daniel_Radcliffe" title="Daniel Radcliffe">Daniel Radcliffe</a> also plays Ron in the "Seven Potters" scene.</li></ul></li>
<li>Ron was one of the few characters who was created before <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a> began writing the series, and whose name never changed from the original drafts.</li>
<li>Rowling described Ron's <a href="/wiki/Patronus_Charm" title="Patronus Charm">Patronus</a> as a "really sentimental choice" on her part, since she has a Jack Russell.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Rowling has also said that if she had a <a href="/wiki/Boggart" title="Boggart">Boggart</a>, hers would likely be the same as Ron's, as she also dislikes <a href="/wiki/Spider" title="Spider">spiders</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-AccioQuote_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-AccioQuote-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Throughout most of the series, Ron does not like to hear <a href="/wiki/Tom_Riddle" title="Tom Riddle">Voldemort</a>'s name spoken out loud, and as such, never says it even when Harry and Hermione do. However, he says the name three times in <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>, even after asking Harry and Hermione not to. The first is at <a href="/wiki/The_Burrow" title="The Burrow">the Burrow</a> when Hermione is packing books to take with them, and Ron says, "<i>I forgot we'll be hunting down <b>Voldemort</b> in a mobile library</i>". The second is at <a href="/wiki/12_Grimmauld_Place" title="12 Grimmauld Place">12 Grimmauld Place</a> when <a href="/wiki/Remus_Lupin" title="Remus Lupin">Remus Lupin</a> tells them that <a href="/wiki/Pius_Thicknesse" title="Pius Thicknesse">Pius Thicknesse</a> is Minister for Magic, and Ron says, "<i>Why didn't <b>Voldemort</b> declare himself Minister for Magic?</i>". The third is again at 12 Grimmauld Place when Harry has a vision of Voldemort killing a woman and her children in his hunt for <a href="/wiki/Mykew_Gregorovitch" title="Mykew Gregorovitch">Gregorovitch</a>. Together, the three try to work out what it means and Ron says, "<i>But according to you, <b>Voldemort's</b> got Ollivander locked up somewhere</i>". Ron also said the name in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Queen%27s_Handbag" title="The Queen&#39;s Handbag">The Queen's Handbag</a></i>, where he jokingly says, "<i><b>Voldemort's</b> gettin' really inventive</i>."</li>
<li>In the films:
<ul><li>Ron is shown as the one to lose his head in a crisis (early on) rather than Hermione.</li>
<li>Ron is well known for using the phrase, "Bloody hell" when he is surprised or frightened.</li></ul></li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher%27s_Stone" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher&#39;s Stone">Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a></i>, Ron is one of the group of four students to serve detention by helping out Hagrid in the Forbidden Forest. This differs from the book, since Neville was the fourth student (along with Hermione, Harry, and Draco Malfoy). This can be attributed to the significantly less amount of time spent on Hagrid having Norbert, along with the differing circumstances on how they were caught. In the book, Ron wasn't helping deliver Norbert because he was being treated for injuries suffered when he was helping Hagrid take care of Norbert.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Prisoner_of_Azkaban" title="Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban">Harry Potter and the Prisoner of Azkaban</a></i>, Ron is dragged away by the foot instead of by the arm by Sirius Black in his Animagus form causing the leg to break instead of having Ron break it when hooking it to the <a href="/wiki/Whomping_Willow" title="Whomping Willow">Whomping Willow</a>'s root to avoid being dragged away.</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Goblet_of_Fire" title="Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire">Harry Potter and the Goblet of Fire</a></i>, Ron supports Bulgaria instead of Ireland, which is who he supports in the book (despite being a Krum fanatic at the time).</li>
<li>In the <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix_(film)" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix (film)">film adaptation</a> of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Order_of_the_Phoenix" title="Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix">Harry Potter and the Order of the Phoenix</a></i>, Ron was introduced to <a href="/wiki/Rubeus_Hagrid" title="Rubeus Hagrid">Hagrid</a>'s half-brother <a href="/wiki/Grawp" title="Grawp">Grawp</a> at the same time as Harry and Hermione. In the book however Ron was playing in the final match of Quidditch championship during that time. This change was due to the removal of Quidditch from the film.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Half-Blood_Prince" title="Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince">Harry Potter and the Half-Blood Prince</a></i>, Professor <a href="/wiki/Horace_Slughorn" title="Horace Slughorn">Horace Slughorn</a> refers to Ron by several names, one of which is <a href="/wiki/Rupert_Grint" title="Rupert Grint">Rupert</a>, which, in fact, is the name of the actor who plays Ron.<sup id="cite_ref-HBP_10-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-HBP-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows</a></i>:
<ul><li>Ron is revolted by the coffee Hermione ordered for them at the Muggle café, from which we can either assume he didn't like the café's coffee or he doesn't like coffee at all. The latter is more likely since he was raised a wizard and knew little about Muggles except from possibly his father's work with Muggle objects and from being friends with two wizards/witches who were raised by Muggles</li>
<li>Ron was shocked that Harry and Hermione had never heard of the children's stories by <a href="/wiki/Beedle_the_Bard" title="Beedle the Bard">Beedle the Bard</a> wizard kids grew up with and when Hermione reminded him that she and Harry were raised by Muggles and that they had grown up with Muggle fairy tales such as "Snow White and the Seven Dwarves" and "Cinderella", Ron thought the latter was an illness.</li></ul></li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_1" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 1</a></i> it is George who walks in on Harry and Ginny kissing in the kitchen on Harry's birthday. In the book, it is Ron bursting in on them in Ginny's bedroom.</li>
<li>In <i><a href="/wiki/LEGO_Harry_Potter:_Years_1-4" title="LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4">LEGO Harry Potter: Years 1-4</a></i>, Ron has the ability to control Scabbers.</li>
<li>The wand that Ron wields in his two full body shot posters for <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i> differs. In the first, the wand he is pointing is his <a href="/wiki/Ron_Weasley%27s_second_wand" class="mw-redirect" title="Ron Weasley&#39;s second wand">second wand</a>, which was taken from him prior to the film. In the second poster, he is holding the <a href="/wiki/Peter_Pettigrew%27s_second_wand" title="Peter Pettigrew&#39;s second wand">wand</a> he obtained after the <a href="/wiki/Skirmish_at_Malfoy_Manor" title="Skirmish at Malfoy Manor">Skirmish at Malfoy Manor</a>.</li>
<li>Many fans feared the possible death of Ronald Weasley, yet in 2000, Rowling seemed dismissive of these fears, stating "As if I'm going to kill Harry's best friend."<sup id="cite_ref-goodscare_57-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-goodscare-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Yet, when Daniel Radcliffe interviewed Rowling for a special feature on the combo pack Blu-ray edition of <i><a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Deathly_Hallows:_Part_2" title="Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2">Harry Potter and the Deathly Hallows: Part 2</a></i>, Rowling stated that at a time she had considered killing one of three members of the <a href="/wiki/Trio" title="Trio">Trio</a>, specifically Ron. Reflecting upon this, she noted that she wasn't in a good place in her life at the time.</li>
<li>He is the only known Pureblood wizard who obtains a Muggle driving licence. It is unclear when Ron obtained his driving licence. However, it has to be after the Second Wizarding War and before the epilogue, which means between May 2nd, 1998 and September 1st, 2017.</li></ul>
<h3><span id="Author's_comments"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Author.27s_comments">Author's comments</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?veaction=edit&amp;section=90" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-divider"> | </span><a href="/wiki/Ronald_Weasley?action=edit&amp;section=90" title="Edit section: Author&#039;s comments"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny section-edit-pencil-icon"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg>edit source</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In an interview with J. K. Rowling and Mugglenet, when asked about Ron and the deluminator she says:
</p><p>"<i>He wasn’t the most skilled, or the most intelligent, but he held the trio together; his humour and his good heart were essential.</i>"
</p><p>“<i>Ron and Hermione, however, are drawn to each other because they balance each other out. Hermione’s got the sensitivity and maturity that’s been left out of Ron, and Ron loosens up Hermione a bit, gets her to have some fun. They love each other and they bicker a bit, but they enjoy bickering, so we shouldn’t worry about it.</i>” -JK Rowling
</p>
